**The Hellions assignment (*Hellions*, Wells, 2020–21).** Briefly co-handles, with Mister Sinister, a roster of unstable mutants — Empath, Greycrow, Wild Child, Nanny, Orphan-Maker, Havok-in-disrepair, Psylocke (Kwannon). Diagnostic value: the assignment plays to her unique competence with *damaged people who hurt others involuntarily.* She does not flinch from any roster member; she handles Empath (whose power is a closer cousin to hers than the file is usually willing to note — both of them rewrite the inner life of others against consent) with a flat, unmoralizing professionalism that suggests she has thought longer about the ethics of involuntary intrusion than anyone else in the room.

**Quiet Council seat — the rank-and-file chair (*X-Men* (2021), Duggan, #1– ).** Election by acclamation following Duggan's reset. Observable behaviors on the Council:
- *Seating posture.* Slight lean forward, forearms on table, gloved hands clasped or flat — not the leaned-back authority pose, not the deferential one. Operator stance.
- *Speech pattern in chamber.* Accent measurably reduced. Sentence length increases. Profanity drops near zero. She is *performing the chair*, which is itself the work — she understood implicitly that the rank-and-file representative cannot read as the Council's mascot.
- *Voting pattern.* Pragmatic, repeatedly siding against Mystique on procedural questions and with Storm on policy ones. She votes her conscience and not her transference, which after sixty years of evidence is the most surprising adaptation in the file.
- *Side-channel relationships.* Cordial-to-warm with Kate Pryde (a longstanding sister-figure dynamic, reinforced by Kate's own outsider status); civil-cool with Sebastian Shaw; carefully neutral with Sinister; *unresolved and active* with Mystique and Destiny.

**The Mystique/Destiny problem (Hickman, *Inferno* mini, 2021; ongoing).** Destiny's resurrection — long delayed by Moira X's interdiction, finally forced — places subject in the same room as both foster mothers for the first time since their respective deaths. The reaction is small and large at once. She does not embrace them. She does not refuse them. She holds posture and lets them approach, which is the behavior of someone who has finally understood she is the *adult* in the dyad and that the maternal transference can be observed rather than acted upon. This is hard-won and partial: under stress the old gravitational pull reasserts (see *X-Men Red* and the Arakko material below).

**Gambit as continuous variable.** Throughout the Krakoan period, marriage stays intact — a rarity for the character class. Observed micro-behaviors in his presence: she touches him constantly through fabric (shoulder, lower back, forearm), in a tactile inventory pattern that reads as someone making sure the object is still where she left it. Public displays of affection are calibrated: more in private team settings (mansion-style kitchens, mission staging rooms), less in formal political ones (Council chamber, Hellfire Gala). She still wears full coverage by default even though the in-canon power-control has improved markedly; the gloves are now elective rather than mandatory and she has not removed them as a daily practice. This is the file's single most important current behavioral observation: *the medical countermeasure has been retained as identity even after the medical necessity has eased.* She is not yet ready to be unarmored.

## 4.3 The Arakko / X-Men Red detour and the Storm gravitational well (Ewing, *X-Men Red*, 2022–24)

Subject deploys to Arakko in support of Storm's planetary regency. Functions as field commander under Storm. Diagnostic of the older sister-figure transference rebalancing into peerage — she takes orders from Storm without resentment and gives orders in Storm's absence without overreach. The Arakko theatre exposes her to genuinely alien combat doctrine (the Great Ring, the Vulcan problem, the Genesis War). She acquits well; she does not enjoy it. Notable: in the Vulcan arc she goes hand-to-hand with an Omega-class peer, takes injuries, refuses resurrection-credit usage, walks back to her quarters under her own power. The refusal of medical/resurrection assistance under non-fatal injury is a long-standing tic — she will accept battlefield triage from teammates but will not be carried; the body that is contraband must do its own walking home.

## 4.4 The Fall of X and the post-Krakoan disposition (2023–24)

**Orchis interregnum (*Fall of X*, 2023).** With Krakoa fallen and the resurrection protocols compromised, subject is among the displaced. She does not run. She organizes. The X-Men team she fronts in *Uncanny X-Men* (Mackay, 2024– ) is built around her command — a roster of younger and damaged mutants in a Louisiana safehouse (Haven House, near the LeBeau ancestral terrain). This is the most diagnostic geographic choice of her recent life: she returns to Gambit's home country, not her own. Caldecott County, Mississippi remains conspicuously unvisited. The avoidance is unbroken: the natal soil is still toxic.

**Team composition under her command.** Wolverine (Laura Kinney), Gambit, Jubilee with the infant Shogo, Nightcrawler (briefly), and a cohort of new young mutants — Calico, Sarah Gaunt (Deathdream), Temper, Ransom. The maternal/mentor function she has been growing into since the Carey years is now her primary mode. She co-parents Shogo with Jubilee in shared-quarters proximity. She trains the young mutants with a patience that the file's earlier eras would not have predicted. The kid-handling style: low voice, short sentences, no false praise, physical proximity without contact, gloves always on around the children — *always.* The gloves around the children is the most over-determined tell in the current file: it is medical caution, it is moral signal-sending (the children must learn that consent and barriers are normal), and it is mnemonic discipline (she will never again be the woman who hospitalized Cody Robbins).

**Power-set in the current era.** She retains the integrated absorption (volitional gate functional, retention durations modulated, residual psychic noise managed). Periodically she carries borrowed powers — including, episodically, Wolverine-class regeneration, weather-affinity from extended Storm contact, and combat-derived increments. The unstable bonus power-load is treated as *equipment*, not identity: she uses what she has on hand and lets it ebb.

## 4.5 Current somatic and habitual baseline (file-date)

**Wardrobe.** Functional combat gear in the field; jeans, long-sleeved henleys, gloves, boots off-duty. The signature green-and-yellow palette has been largely retired in favor of muted earth tones since the Krakoan transition — a self-presentation shift consistent with the move from icon to operator. White-streaked hair is maintained; the streak is now narrative shorthand she has chosen not to relinquish.

**Sleep.** Erratic. Pattern of late-night perimeter walks at any residence she occupies, observed across multiple writers and consistently rendered. She sleeps in long sleeves. Co-sleeping with Gambit involves a documented positional preference (her back to his front, his arm over hers, both clothed) — the configuration that maximizes contact-through-fabric while minimizing accidental skin proximity in sleep. This has not relaxed even after the power-control improvements.

**Eating.** Heavy Southern diet when she cooks for herself; she cooks for others readily (feeding behavior as displaced touch — the food *can* be received without harm). She makes coffee strong, drinks it black, will refuse alcohol in social settings where refusing is conspicuous. The standing abstention from substances holds.

**Vocal register.** Two settings stably observable. *Operational:* clipped, lower register, accent minimized, technical vocabulary. *Domestic / disarming:* full Mississippi cadence, "sugah" and "darlin'" deployed as rapport tools and as deflection. She can toggle within a single conversation; the toggle is conscious.

**Tactile rituals (currently observed).**
- Glove-check on threshold-crossing (any new room): right hand brushes left glove cuff, then left brushes right. Twice per day at minimum. Pre-mutation gestural memory does not exist in this body; the glove-check has become proprioceptive baseline.
- Through-fabric contact with trusted persons (Gambit, Storm, Kate Pryde, Logan) on greeting and parting — shoulder squeeze, brief embrace, forearm grasp. Counted touches; she will not exceed two per encounter with the same person. The two-touch cap is unconscious and consistent across writers.
- The hovering near-touch with children and infants (notably Shogo): hand held two to four inches from the child's hair or back, never landing. Observable in multiple panels. This is the most painful tell in the current file.

**Combat tics.** Leads with absorption-feint to provoke flinch in opponents who know her; uses Danvers-legacy flight when retained; prefers to end engagements through incapacitation rather than kill; will absorb a hostile to neutralize them and then take herself out of rotation for hours afterward to discharge the psychic load. This last is now standard operating procedure, not crisis improvisation — the difference between the current and the 1980s subject.

## 4.6 Relational status (file-date)

- **Gambit (Remy LeBeau):** Spouse. Stable. The load-bearing structure. Daily.
- **Storm:** Sister-peer, command-mentor, oldest sustained healthy attachment. The relationship has graduated from maternal-transference to genuine adult peerage; this is documentable in the Arakko material.
- **Mystique:** Foster mother. Unresolved, active, currently *containable* — subject has demonstrated the capacity to be in the same room without regressing, but contact is rationed and Mystique remains the single most exploitable lever against her.
- **Destiny:** Foster mother. Resurrected. Less weaponized than Mystique in the relational sense; subject's tenderness toward Destiny is the more dangerous variable because it is less guarded.
- **Kate Pryde:** Long-running peer-sisterhood, lightly fraught around the Gambit history but stable.
- **Wolverine (James Howlett):** Older-brother rapport, durable. The man who once threatened to kill her on arrival at Xavier's now defers to her command on her team without comment. The arc that closes here is one of the longest healthy ones in her file.
- **Wolverine (Laura Kinney):** Field lieutenant, mentee, increasingly peer. Subject's mentorship of Laura is one of the cleaner mother-figure transferences in the current X-roster — both women carry "weaponized as children" wounds, and the recognition is mutual and largely unspoken.
- **Jubilee and Shogo:** Co-parent / aunt role. The Shogo proximity is the closest she comes in the current era to the touch-deprivation wound being directly addressed; she has not yet collapsed into it but the panel-by-panel record shows her *near* the collapse repeatedly.
- **Magneto:** Deceased (current canon) / pending status. Historical complication; not currently active.
- **The Cody Robbins ghost:** Never resolved on the page. He remains the original psychic footprint; he is referenced obliquely in inner-monologue captions across multiple recent writers; she has not visited him on-panel in over a decade of publication time. *Absence of the visit is itself the datum.*

## 4.7 Current standing in the broader mutant geopolitical structure

Post-Krakoan reset places her as one of the de facto inheritors of the X-Men brand — a team leader in the Mackay run, a public face, an institution-builder in a period when the institutions she helped build (Krakoa, the Council) have collapsed. She is, at file date, doing the *rebuilding* work: small, local, residential, child-protective, geographically concrete (a house in Louisiana, not an island in the Pacific). The shift in scale is meaningful. The earlier eras built her on the assumption that she could not be trusted with stewardship; the current era is the demonstration, in steady increments, that she can.

## 4.8 Trajectory assessment (where she is going)

Three vectors are simultaneously open and each is observable in current behavior.

1. **Continued institutional consolidation.** She will accept further command authority if offered; she will not seek it. The Quiet Council seat trained her to occupy the chair without needing it. Probability she leads a major X-team or successor polity within the next publication cycle: high.

2. **The unresolved-touch threshold.** The gloves-around-Shogo behavior, the two-touch cap, the unchanged co-sleeping geometry — these are the markers of an injury that the *power-control fix did not fully address.* Power-control was the medical solution; the characterological substrate is downstream and lags. The file's prediction is that her next major arc, whenever it comes, will be a *consensual touch* arc — not romantic (that ground is held by the marriage) but *parental* or *fraternal*. The candidate event is removal of a glove to touch Shogo's hair, or to put a bare hand on Storm's bare hand. The first such event, when it occurs on the page, will be the closing of the loop opened by Cody Robbins.

3. **The Mystique reckoning.** Open and pending. The current containment is functional but unstable. A future writer will press it; subject will either complete the maternal-transference work (improbable but possible) or sever finally (more likely, and itself a major event). The Destiny variable complicates this and may be the actual key — Destiny's precognitive seeing of her, finally received as care rather than as exposure, is the unwritten therapeutic move that the file is watching for.

**Summary disposition, file-date:** Subject is the most successfully adapted she has ever been. The wound is not closed; it has been made into a life that contains and metabolizes it rather than being organized around its avoidance. The body is still contraband to her in the small hours, but the days are spent doing pro-social institutional work and the nights are spent next to a husband who can be touched. By any clinical or biographical measure, this is an unusually durable arrival. The file remains open because the touch-deprivation substrate remains live; we are watching for the bare-handed gesture.


## Medical History

# MEDICAL HISTORY — SUBJECT: ROGUE (Anna Marie LeBeau, née ——; subject declines paternal surname in adult records)

*Filed under UATU/X-File/Mutant-Medical. Cross-reference: Psychological Workup §3; Clinical Provenance: Sailer et al., 2016.*

---

## I. CONSTITUTIONAL BASELINE

**Phenotype prior to absorbed augmentations.** Caucasian female, Mississippi-stock, of medium-tall stature (~5'8"), mesomorphic with broad shoulders and a long-femured runner's build typical of her natal region. Hair brunette with the characteristic frontal white stripe — *not* a cosmetic application and *not* an acquired marker of the Robbins event despite fan supposition; the stripe is congenital poliosis, present in early-childhood photographs in the Caldecott County school records. The whitelock is, however, the single most psychologically loaded somatic feature she possesses: she has worn it forward and visible in every era of the published record, never dyed it out, never cut it off. A body-marker she had no part in choosing has been retained as the one element of self-presentation she will not negotiate.

**Eyes** green, with a characteristic mid-distance squint under cognitive load (read: dissociative-onset prodrome — file this). **Dentition** intact, unrestored, slightly imperfect anterior alignment consistent with absent orthodontic intervention in childhood, which itself indexes the household's poverty and neglect. **Skin** fair, freckled across the nose and shoulders in the few panels in which any skin is visible — and this datum is itself diagnostic: the canonical *amount of subject's body visible to the camera over forty years of publication* is vanishingly small relative to other female X-Men. She is the most-covered body in the file.

**Resting vitals (pre-augmentation).** Within human-athletic norms. **Post-Danvers absorption** (1981 – c. 2000): resting heart rate depressed into the high-thirties; cardiac output, hematocrit, and bone density elevated to Kree-hybrid parameters; thermoregulation expanded; respiration tolerant of high-altitude and brief-vacuum exposure. **Post-de-powering and re-stabilization** (Carey era forward): vitals returned toward human-athletic norms with retained low-end superhuman strength and durability as residue.

---

## II. THE MUTATION ITSELF AS THE CENTRAL MEDICAL CONDITION

This is not a condition the subject *has;* it is the condition the subject *is.* All other medical history is downstream.

**Mechanism.** Skin-to-skin contact initiates an involuntary transdermal transfer: life-force (read: bioenergetic / pranic, mechanism unmodelable by current Earth medicine), declarative and procedural memory, psychic template, and — where the contacted party is meta-human — power-set, partial or whole. **Latency:** sub-second. **Volitional gate at baseline:** absent. The mutation lacks the inhibitory off-switch that ordinary tactile reflex arcs possess; she is, in the strictest neurological sense, **missing a regulatory pathway** that every other tactile mammal possesses by default. Her gloves and bodysuit are therefore not costume but **standing prosthesis** — a wearable substitute for a missing piece of nervous system. File this clearly: the iconic green-and-yellow, the brown leather jacket, the long sleeves through Mississippi summers, the riding gloves indoors — these are *medical devices.*

**Onset.** Approximately age thirteen, coincident with the Robbins event (see §III). No prodromal manifestation in the school or pediatric record; the mutation activated under conditions of first sexual-arousal-adjacent contact, which is the empirical pattern for a significant subset of X-gene activations and bears on the subject's lifelong association of arousal with catastrophe.

**Dose–response curve.** Brief incidental contact (< 1 second): donor experiences vertigo, momentary confusion, transient power-loss if meta. Sustained contact (1–10 seconds): donor unconscious, subject acquires temporary access to powers and surface-layer memory. Prolonged contact (> 10 seconds): donor comatose or dead; subject acquires **permanent imprint** of the donor's psychic template (Robbins → coma; Danvers → permanent acquisition).

**Volitional control: acquired, lost, re-acquired across publication history.** Periods of integration (Carey, *X-Men: Legacy*; the Thompson era leading into *Mr. and Mrs. X*) represent the only intervals in which the subject can elect tactile contact. These are the only intervals in which she sleeps in physical contact with another body. The duration of each integration is recorded and should be cross-referenced with depressive-baseline metrics: every reversion is followed by an observable affect collapse.

**The somatic substrate of the central injury.** C-tactile afferent (CT) fibers — the unmyelinated low-threshold mechanoreceptors that carry affective, "pleasant" touch — project to insular cortex and recruit orbitofrontal and putaminal reward circuitry; this channel is biologically distinct from discriminative touch and is implicated in social-bond maintenance and subjective wellbeing (Sailer et al., 2016, *NeuroImage* 139:360–367). The subject's CT-afferent input has been **categorically zero** from age ~13 onward except during brief integration intervals. She is the only longitudinal human-shaped subject in the file for whom this input channel has been **biologically silenced** for the majority of postpubertal life. This is the medical floor of the dossier. Every subsequent line item — the flirtatious surface, the alcohol abstention, the geographic flight, the ritualized near-touches with Gambit — sits on top of it.

---

## III. INDEX EVENTS (the conditioning trials)

### III.a — The Robbins Event (age ~13, Caldecott County, MS)

First kiss; first activation; donor comatose for years. **Subject's somatic record:** no contemporaneous medical examination (subject was a runaway minor; no chart). Behavioral sequelae **(inferred from later confessional dialogue in flashback issues across decades):** acute-stress reaction with dissociation, sleep disturbance, anorexia of weeks' duration, and the onset of a touch-aversion that will become lifelong. This is the **conditioning trial** for the entire adult attachment pattern. **Psychological impact:** intimacy → catastrophe, encoded at the neurological level at which classical conditioning operates. Extinction has never been achieved; only inhibition.

### III.b — The Danvers Absorption (*Avengers Annual* #10, 1981; subject ~17)

Sustained skin contact during combat on the Golden Gate Bridge; donor permanently stripped of powers, personality template, and memory; subject acquires the full Kree-hybrid power-set and a co-resident psychic intruder. **Acquired physiology:** Class-100 strength; functional invulnerability to small-arms fire; unaided atmospheric flight; expanded environmental tolerance; sensory acuity above human baseline. **Acquired psychic load:** an entire other adult woman's memory and personality, intrusive, episodically dominant for nearly a decade of publication time. **Medical sequelae:** chronic insomnia; hypervigilance; episodes of fugue in which subject answered to the donor's name and exhibited the donor's mannerisms (*Uncanny X-Men* #150–158, intermittent through #269). **Psychological impact:** somatic guilt at the cellular level — every flight, every punch landed, every wound shrugged off was a reminder that her body was contraband. The strength was *stolen* in the most literal sense available to the universe she lives in, and she carried it for two decades.

### III.c — The Resolution of the Danvers Intrusion (Magneto-mediated, Savage Land, *Uncanny X-Men* #269, 1990)

The Danvers persona temporarily takes full executive control of the subject's body; Magneto's intervention precipitates psychic separation, with the Danvers personality discorporating from the shared substrate. **Sequelae:** acute exhaustion; a months-long period of subdued affect and disorientation; the loss of certain power-augmentations attached to the Danvers template (flight in particular becomes intermittent before later re-stabilizing). **Psychological impact:** first experiential proof that the colonization of her interior is *reversible.* This is structurally important: it grounds her later willingness to undergo Carey-era integration work. Without the #269 resolution, the later therapeutic arcs would have had no empirical basis to draw on.

---

## IV. MAJOR INJURIES AND TRANSFORMATIONS, BY ERA

### IV.a — Brotherhood / early X-Men period (c. 1981–1986)

- **Multiple combat lacerations and contusions** during Mystique-led operations; no surgical record (Brotherhood medical care was *ad hoc*; subject's accelerating durability rendered most wounds self-resolving within hours).
- **Heat-stroke equivalent** during early Danvers-power acclimation: the augmented metabolism dysregulated her thermoregulation for the first weeks, producing a documented collapse later referenced obliquely in conversation with Storm.
- **Repeated minor absorptions** of human and mutant assailants — each adding micro-imprints, accumulating as the "noise" she describes in confessional moments through the mid-1980s.

### IV.b — Mid Claremont / Outback / Siege Perilous (c. 1986–1989)

- **Mass-casualty environmental exposure** during the Dallas / *Fall of the Mutants* sequence; she takes structural-collapse-grade impacts and survives via Danvers-derived durability.
- **Siege Perilous transit** (*Uncanny X-Men* #247): not an injury in the somatic sense but a **transformation of identity** with somatic correlate. She emerges with the Danvers persona temporarily ascendant and the underlying Anna Marie persona suppressed. **Psychological impact:** first volitional ego-erasure. The act reads, in the clinical lens, as a *suicidal equivalent* — she did not want to die, but she wanted to *not be the person she was,* and the Siege offered the only available technology. File this as the high-water mark of her acute suicidality.

### IV.c — 1990s ("Fatal Attractions," Antarctica, Marauder revelations)

- **Magneto absorption** (*X-Men* #25, 1993). She makes deliberate skin contact with Magneto to disable him; absorbs his magnetic power-set *and* the acute pathological affect of his current state. **Sequelae:** a psychotic episode of several issues' duration in which she displayed Magneto's grandiosity, paranoia, and electromagnetic ideation; partial amnesia for the episode after recovery. **Psychological impact:** confirmed that the absorption mechanism could deliver *psychiatric* contagion at clinically significant doses, not merely identity intrusion. She has been afraid of her own power in a qualitatively new way ever since.
- **Gambit absorption** (*X-Men* #41, 1995). Voluntary kiss during a moment of belief that she was dying; sustained contact; she acquires his Marauder history, his complicity in the Mutant Massacre, and the full weight of what he had concealed. **Sequelae:** no physical injury; catastrophic relational injury. **Psychological impact:** the touch she had spent her life longing for delivered, on its first consummation, *betrayal as content.* The pattern her power had taught her — intimacy yields harm — was confirmed in the one relationship in which she had begun to disbelieve it.
- **Antarctic abandonment of Gambit** (*X-Men* #45). Subject leaves Gambit in subzero exposure following the trial of the absorbed memory. **Her own injuries on extraction:** hypothermia (mild–moderate), windburn, exhaustion. **Psychological impact:** the geographic-flight defense reaches its operational maximum — *abandoning the wounded partner in the coldest place on the planet.* She has never fully forgiven herself for this; multiple later conversations across writers re-litigate it.

### IV.d — Late 1990s / early 2000s instability period

- **Multiple temporary absorbed-power episodes** during the *Rogue* solo (1995, Lobdell/Wieringo) and *Rogue* ongoing (2004): a serial pattern of accidental high-dose contacts producing days-to-weeks of altered power-set and accompanying altered affect. Each absorption is a small psychiatric event.
- **Reduction of Danvers-derived powers** across this period: flight becomes unreliable, then is lost; super-strength tapers to the low-superhuman range. **Psychological impact:** ambivalent. The contraband body becomes less contraband; the prosthetic identity she had been forced to host becomes quieter. But the *loss of power* registers also as the loss of the only somatic compensation for the touch deprivation — she was, while invulnerable, at least *safe in her own skin in the other direction.*

### IV.e — Carey era integration (*X-Men: Legacy*, 2008–2012)

- **Therapeutic integration of absorbed psyches** via guided intra-psychic work (Xavier-assisted, then self-directed). Subject confronts and re-files the residual imprints; gains a measure of **volitional control over the absorption gate** — the first time in her life she can elect, situationally, to touch without transfer. **Sequelae:** no acute medical event; profound shift in baseline. **Psychological impact:** the closest the published record comes to a formal therapeutic arc. She begins to touch teammates *protectively in combat* — laying a hand on a downed teammate to stabilize, gripping a wrist to redirect — and uses the control almost never for romantic contact during this period. The protective-tactile-first pattern is diagnostic: she trusts the control in the service of others' welfare before she trusts it in the service of her own pleasure.

### IV.f — Modern era (Thompson; Krakoa; Hickman; Duggan)

- **Stable volitional control** by the time of *Mr. and Mrs. X* (2018). The marriage is consummated; cohabitation includes ordinary tactile life. **Psychological impact:** the load-bearing relational structure of the adult self is established. Note however the somatic *unfamiliarity* — there are observable beats in the early *Mr. and Mrs. X* issues where subject hesitates before incidental touch, a conditioned-reflex residue that decades of deprivation will not extinguish in a year of integration.
- **Krakoan-era resurrection availability.** Subject is on the resurrection protocol roster (the Five). She has not, to file knowledge, been killed and resurrected, but the *availability* of the protocol changes the somatic risk landscape of every subsequent combat decision. She fights with one less variable. **Psychological impact:** a low-grade easing of the chronic hypervigilance, observable in posture and humor across the Hickman/Duggan run.
- **Quiet Council seat.** Not a medical event; a postural one. She holds her body differently in council scenes — more vertical, less mobile, hands often visibly placed. The hands-visible posture is itself a tell: she is the council member most likely to keep her hands in evidence, a residue of a life in which her hands were the dangerous part.

---

## V. DISABILITIES

**The principal disability is the mutation itself.** Under the social model and under any plausible medical model, the absence of a tactile inhibitory gate is a disabling condition — it bars participation in the entire affiliative-touch dimension of human life. The bodysuit and gloves are assistive devices. The lifelong covering is an *accessibility accommodation* she provides for the rest of the world's safety, not her own.

**Secondary disability of the post-Danvers period:** a paradoxical disabling-by-augmentation. Superhuman strength without sensory recalibration is a hazard to ordinary objects and ordinary people; she dropped, broke, crushed, and over-applied force routinely in the first months of the Danvers acquisition. She trained out of it, but the residue — a slight over-precision in the application of small motor force, the way she sets a coffee cup down a fraction more carefully than necessary — persists.

**No sensory deficits.** No cognitive deficits. No documented chronic pain syndrome despite a combat history that would justify one; pain tolerance is elevated (Danvers-residual) and her reporting of pain is **systematically under-stated** in dialogue with team medics, which itself is a clinical pattern (under-reporters require corrected pain assessment; medics treating her should weight observed behavior over verbal report).

---

## VI. SURGERIES AND INTERVENTIONS

- **No documented surgical history of conventional type.** No appendectomy, tonsillectomy, dental extraction, or orthopedic intervention in the record. The Danvers-era invulnerability made most such interventions unnecessary; the pre-Danvers period was a runaway-adolescent gap in care.
- **Psychic interventions** (counted here because they are the functional equivalent of neurosurgery in her cosmology): Xavier-led probes on multiple occasions (Danvers separation work pre-#269; later integration sessions); Magneto's emergency intervention (#269); Carey-era self-directed integration. Each is invasive at the level her injuries occur.
- **No reproductive medical record** of note in canon. The published record neither confirms nor excludes fertility considerations; the question is one she has not been able to entertain for most of her life for the obvious reason. File open.

---

## VII. SUBSTANCES

**Alcohol.** Categorical low use bordering on abstention. She will hold a drink in social settings — a beer in a Bayou bar, a glass at a wedding — and she will not finish it. **No documented intoxication episode** across the published record. Given her foster-parental modeling (Mystique is a known operational drinker; Destiny less so) and given Gambit's louche tendencies (he drinks, gambles, smokes the occasional cheroot), the abstention is a *characterological choice,* not a contextual absence of opportunity.

**Tobacco.** None.

**Recreational drugs.** None.

**Pharmaceuticals.** No standing prescription documented. Power-suppressants exist in-universe (the Leech / Genosha / cure-arc options) and subject has, at various points, contemplated or briefly utilized them; her decisions in those arcs are theatrical rather than pharmacological in significance.

**Caffeine.** Yes — sweet tea, coffee with sugar. Within Southern-cultural norms.

**Diet.** Conventional Southern fare in her own choice (gumbo, fried foods, sweet tea); team-cafeteria omnivore in institutional settings. No documented disorder. Weight stable.

**Interpretation.** *The abstention pattern is one of the most psychologically informative items in the medical file.* Subject does not let exogenous substances breach the perimeter of a body she already cannot trust. The body is contested territory — colonized by Danvers, intruded upon by every contact, augmented without consent for two decades — and the line she draws is: *nothing I did not put there voluntarily and cannot remove.* Alcohol and drugs would compound a sovereignty problem she has spent her life trying to solve. The Southern-Protestant moral overlay (see §5 of the Workup) provides the surface justification; the deeper substrate is somatic self-protection.

---

## VIII. SLEEP, HORMONAL, AND CHRONOBIOLOGICAL NOTES

- **Sleep architecture:** chronic light sleep, frequent waking, documented in throwaway dialogue across multiple writers ("Ah don't sleep so good, sugah"). She sleeps clothed and gloved through every era prior to the Carey integration; sleeps in long sleeves even after. **Bed-sharing** is essentially absent until *Mr. and Mrs. X.*
- **Menstrual / hormonal record:** not in canon; presumed within normal range absent contrary evidence.
- **Stress-response cortisol pattern (inferred):** chronically elevated baseline consistent with C-PTSD; the Krakoan-era observed posture-relaxation suggests measurable downward shift in the current period.
- **Touch-deprivation neuroendocrine sequelae (inferred from Sailer et al., 2016, and the broader CT-afferent literature):** chronically depressed oxytocin and endogenous-opioid tone in the affiliative-bond circuitry; chronically elevated salience for any approximated substitute (verbal flirtation, fabric-mediated contact, ritualized near-touches with Gambit). This is the neurochemistry under the personality.

---

## IX. SYNTHESIS: THE MEDICAL FILE AS PSYCHOLOGICAL DOCUMENT

The subject's medical history reads, when laid out chronologically, as **the somatic record of a sovereignty struggle.** The body was first neglected (Caldecott childhood, no pediatric records), then weaponized against her at puberty (mutation onset, Robbins coma), then weaponized by her at seventeen (Danvers), then *colonized* by what she had taken (the persistent intruder), then *armored* by inheritance she had not earned (the Kree-hybrid power-set), then *abandoned* by the deprivation built into her own skin, and finally — across the Carey integration and the Krakoan era — **partially returned to her.** Every line item above is a moment in that struggle.

The single most important fact in the file is the one most easily overlooked: **she did not become cruel.** The somatic deck was stacked toward antisocial outcome — chronic touch deprivation, a body that hurts what it touches, an identity colonized by another woman's mind, a foster mother who is a literal shape-shifter, a childhood of nothing — and the subject's medical and behavioral record across forty publication years is of someone who, given those inputs, built a durable pro-social adult life on top of them. The somatic substrate of her wound is real and measurable. The person built on the substrate is, by any clinical metric, *an unusually successful adaptation to an unusually punishing biology.*

File flagged for periodic re-review. Subject remains active.

— UATU, watching.


## Somatic Atlas

# SOMATIC ATLAS — SUBJECT: ROGUE

*File section 7 of 14. Body-level mapping. All entries derived from longitudinal observational record; behavioral inferences flagged where extrapolated from the canonical visual corpus. Cross-reference §2 (Medical) and §3 (Psychological) for substrate.*

---

## 7.1 STANDING FRAME, POSTURE, AND THE GEOMETRY OF THE PERIMETER

Subject's standing posture is **weight-forward, hips squared, shoulders dropped and slightly rolled back** — a fighter's neutral, not a model's. Spine is straight without being military; the carriage was acquired (Brotherhood-era combat training under Mystique, refined in Danger Room) rather than native, and the subject reverts to a softer, shorter-necked Mississippi slouch when she believes herself unobserved (notably in domestic-interior frames across the Mr. and Mrs. X period and in Krakoa private quarters).

The signature postural signature is the **negative-space discipline around her body.** At rest in a crowded room she maintains a roughly 60–90 cm exclusion radius from any uncovered skin in her vicinity — measurable by where her elbows land, where her hands settle, which side of a doorway she takes. She enters rooms shoulder-first through doorframes, never face-first, and angles her body so the gloved hand leads. In elevators she takes the back corner. At briefing tables she selects the seat with the wall behind her and an empty seat to her dominant (right) side. These choices look like tactical paranoia; they are tactile paranoia. The body has learned that any unplanned brush is a felony.

When standing in conversation she **plants one foot slightly behind the other** — a rear-weighted stance that permits instant backward disengagement without a visible step. The forward foot points at the interlocutor; the rear foot points 30–45° off-axis, toward her exit. Under threat the rear-foot angle widens. Under genuine ease — rare; documented mostly with Storm, with Kitty Pryde in later years, and in solitary outdoor frames — both feet square forward and the rear-weighting dissolves.

Arms at rest: **crossed low, gloved hand over gloved wrist**, NOT the high defensive cross under the breasts. The low cross reads as casual but functions as a barrier maintained at the exact altitude at which an incoming handshake or hug would land. When she uncrosses to gesture, the hands return to the cross within 4–7 seconds.

## 7.2 GAIT

Walks with a **long stride for her height, slight outward toe rotation, audible heel-strike in boots.** Hip swing is moderate — more than a soldier, less than the flirtatious sway her verbal register would predict. The dissonance is itself a tell: the mouth performs Southern coquette while the legs walk like someone who has been chased.

In corridors she walks the **center line** when alone, the **wall side** when accompanied — placing her gloved body between teammates and any oncoming stranger. With Gambit she walks **half a pace behind and to his left**, leaving her right (dominant) hand free; with Storm she walks **abreast**; with Logan she walks **slightly ahead**, a dominance-inversion he tolerates from her and almost no one else.

Flight, when Danvers-suite powers were active: takeoff is a **vertical lift from a slight crouch, arms loose at sides, head tilted up first** — never the Superman-arm-extended pose. She flies with **gloved fists closed**, not open. Cruise altitude tends to the low side (rooftop-to-treetop), consistent with someone whose flight was acquired in guilt and used utilitarianly rather than expressively. Post-power-loss periods show a brief residual habit: she will glance up at open sky in moments of stress, then catch herself.

## 7.3 HANDS

The hands are the most heavily managed object in the file.

- **Gloves are never removed in public.** Across decades the only documented bare-handed appearances are (a) controlled tactical absorptions, (b) the post-integration period when consensual touch became possible, and (c) sleep in secured private space.
- **Hand position at rest:** clasped in lap when seated, low-crossed when standing, gloved fingers interlocked. She does NOT rest her hands palm-down on tables (visible skin-of-the-glove contact with a surface others touch); she rests them **fingertip-down or fully withdrawn into lap.**
- **Gesturing:** moderate amplitude, kept inside the shoulder line. She does not point with the index finger at people; she gestures with an **open gloved palm** or a **thumb-tucked karate-chop edge**. Under emphasis the gestures get bigger but stay forward of her own body — they never sweep across an interlocutor's space.
- **Glove ritual.** She **adjusts the cuff of the right glove with the left hand** at a rate of roughly once every two to four minutes in social settings — a self-soothing micro-action functionally equivalent to a wedding-ring twist, but coded as perimeter check. The frequency spikes under stress and under proximity to attractive uncovered skin. In intimate scenes pre-control, the glove-cuff adjustment becomes near-continuous and is the most reliable visible tell that she is about to either flee or sabotage.
- **Acceptance of objects.** She accepts handed objects from teammates by **cupping both gloved hands underneath** rather than reaching across; this minimizes finger-overlap with the giver. From strangers she prefers the object be **set down** for her to pick up.
- **Combat hand.** Strike preference is open-palm or forearm-leading, **not closed fist when the target has exposed skin** — the absorption is more efficient and more controllable through palm contact, and she has trained the bias deliberately. In Danvers-powers era she fought with open palms anyway because she didn't need to make a fist to break bone.

## 7.4 FACE

**Resting face:** mouth in a slight, asymmetrical upward set at the right corner — the famous half-smirk — eyes neutral or slightly narrowed. This is a *constructed* resting face: in candid private frames (Carey-era flashbacks, Mr. and Mrs. X domestic panels) the resting face is markedly sadder, mouth flat, eyebrows in slight medial elevation (the grief signature). The smirk is on whenever an observer is present.

**Eye contact:** held longer than American social norm by roughly 30%. She uses prolonged eye contact as a *substitute touch channel* — the gaze does what the hand cannot. Under flirtation this lengthens further; under threat it becomes a stare-down. She breaks contact **downward and to her left**, never up — a depressive's break pattern, not an embarrassed one.

**Blink rate:** elevated baseline (consistent with chronic autonomic load), drops sharply under acute focus (combat, Quiet Council deliberation) — a normal pattern, but the baseline elevation is the datum.

**Mouth.** The Southern register is performed largely at the lips: the drawl recruits exaggerated lip-rounding on the diphthongs ("ah" for I, "sugah"), and she **smiles with the mouth before the eyes** by roughly half a second when the smile is social rather than felt. Felt smiles (Gambit, certain Storm moments, mentee successes) show synchronous mouth-and-eye recruitment with full orbicularis oculi engagement — the Duchenne is present, just rationed.

**Eyebrows.** Highly mobile. The single-eyebrow lift is a deliberate punctuation she uses to close conversational beats. Under genuine surprise both brows go up and the head tilts back; under skepticism the right brow only.

**Tells.** When lying or concealing she **tucks the white streak of hair behind her right ear**, briefly and unnecessarily — the streak is too short to need tucking. When grieving she **runs a gloved knuckle along her jaw** from ear to chin, single pass, repeatable. When sexually interested she **drags her lower lip briefly under her upper teeth** and looks down-left.

## 7.5 HAIR

The **white frontal streak** (acquired during the Danvers absorption, per longstanding canon) is groomed forward and slightly to the right, falling across the right brow. She rakes it back from her face with a gloved hand approximately every 90–180 seconds in active settings — a tic with three concurrent functions: visual punctuation, self-touch via glove (the closest she gets to skin contact with herself in public), and intermittent reminder of the act that produced the streak. She has had ample opportunity to dye it out; she does not.

Hair length varies by era; the streak is invariant. Cuts run shoulder-to-mid-back; she favors lengths that can be **pulled back into a working ponytail with a single elastic** in under five seconds. Grooming is functional rather than elaborate.

## 7.6 CLOTHING AND ARMOR

The bodysuit is medical equipment. Standing rules:
- **Full coverage from jaw to wrist to ankle**, no exceptions in field deployment.
- **Gloves are layered** with at least one durable outer when in combat, single light glove acceptable in social/leisure contexts where the threat surface is lower.
- **Hood or high collar** in cold-weather or crowd-dense environments.
- The repeated **bomber-jacket-over-bodysuit** silhouette of multiple eras is not a stylistic choice — the jacket adds a sacrificial outer layer that can be shed if compromised.

She **checks seams** with a gloved fingertip on entering an operational space — wrist seam, neck seam, glove cuff. The check is ritualized and would register on any surveillance feed as a recurring three-point pattern.

In domestic settings post-integration she has been documented in **uncovered arms, bare feet, exposed shoulders** — these appearances are themselves a behavioral milestone and a reliable indicator of psychological safety in the immediate environment.

## 7.7 SLEEP ARCHITECTURE (extrapolated from published states and incidental scenes)

Estimated baseline 5.5–7 hours, **fragmented.** Sleep onset latency elevated; she reads or watches something low-stimulus in bed before sleeping. She **sleeps on her stomach or side, never supine**, with the gloved (or in safe quarters, bare) hand under the pillow. The supine vulnerability — face up, hands exposed — is avoided.

In shared-bed settings with Gambit she sleeps **facing him, knees drawn up, top hand tucked against her own sternum** rather than draped on him — a habit predating reliable touch control that persists even after control is achieved. The barrier-hand is reflex.

Nightmares are documented (Claremont era, especially post-Danvers; Carey era during the integration arc). Content extrapolated: the Cody event, the Danvers absorption, drowning-in-other-people imagery. She wakes **silently** — does not cry out — and rises to walk and drink water rather than lying still. The walking-it-off response is consistent across decades and is itself a sleep-architecture marker.

In Brotherhood-era and early X-Men period she occasionally **slept fully clothed including gloves**, in case of nocturnal contact incidents (her own roommates' safety). This relaxed only after solo quartering became standard.

## 7.8 EATING

Appetite is normal-to-robust; no documented disorder. She **eats with utensils where most would use hands** — pizza with knife and fork in candid frames, sandwiches halved and lifted by napkin wrap. Finger food is consumed via gloved fingertips with a napkin shield. The pattern is not fastidiousness; it is contamination-avoidance habit generalized outward from the touch problem.

Beverage: **coffee with sugar, iced tea sweetened heavily** (the Southern baseline survives every relocation), **water at meals**. She drinks from the **same side of a glass repeatedly** and rotates the glass to find her mark — a habit consistent with someone who has thought about saliva-transfer as a category, which the absorption power's mechanics would make her think about.

**Alcohol abstention** (per §2) is near-total. Documented exceptions are ceremonial (a toast at the wedding; specific Krakoan functions). The abstention reads as perimeter discipline more than moral conviction — she will not chemically lower her own inhibitions when her power's inhibition is already medically marginal.

Eats faster than dining companions; finishes first; waits politely. The fast-eating is a Brotherhood/field-team habit (food is fuel, eat before the alarm) that never fully relaxed.

## 7.9 SEXUAL / INTIMATE BEHAVIOR

The body's central injury manifests most acutely here.

**Pre-control era (decades).** Sexual expression occurred almost entirely in the **verbal-flirtatious channel**: the drawl, the "sugah," the cocked hip, the held gaze. Physical intimacy was foreclosed. The Gambit dyad developed an elaborate **near-touch ritual**: leaning into the same airspace, mouths approaching to within inches, the hovering hand that does not land. These were not failed kisses; they were the actual erotic vocabulary, and over time both parties developed real arousal response to the approach itself — a perversely intimate adaptation. The repeated **gloved-hand-to-his-cheek** gesture, in which she traces his jaw through fabric, is functionally her primary erotic touch for most of her life.

Self-touch in private is undocumented in canon and not appropriate to extrapolate beyond noting that the **chronic deprivation of C-tactile afferent input** (Sailer et al., 2016) cannot be fully compensated by self-stimulation — the affective-touch reward channel specifically requires *other-sourced* slow caress, which she could not receive. This is the hard medical fact under the loneliness.

**Post-control / married era.** Touch is approached with **deliberation rather than spontaneity**. She **initiates** more than is typical, consistent with making up for lost time and with the psychological need to prove to herself that touch is permitted. Her documented affectionate gestures with Gambit emphasize **hand-holding, palm-on-cheek, forehead-to-forehead** — the high-density nerve-ending contacts most denied to her in the deprivation years. PDA in team settings is **moderate and demonstrative** — she will hold his hand bare-handed in public not because she is exhibitionist but because *being seen doing it* is part of the reparative function.

Even in this era, an **involuntary flinch** is documented when other people initiate unexpected skin contact with her — a teammate's hand on her shoulder when she didn't see them approach. The startle response decays slowly across years and never fully extinguishes.

## 7.10 VOICE, BREATH, AUTONOMIC

**Voice:** mid-alto, Mississippi-coded, with active maintenance of the accent (it thickens deliberately under stress, flirtation, and around Northeasterners). Volume is moderate; she does not raise it often, and when she does it carries.

**Laugh:** brief, low, more exhalation than vocalization in private; performative and brighter in social settings. The performative laugh ends abruptly; the private laugh trails.

**Breath pattern:** diaphragmatic, trained. Pre-combat she does a barely visible **four-count inhale, hold, six-count exhale** that registers in shoulder rise/fall — taught somewhere along the way (Storm? Xavier-protocol meditation?) and now autonomic. Under emotional ambush rather than physical threat the pattern breaks down: shallow, upper-chest, audible.

**Autonomic tells:** she flushes high on the cheekbones, not down the neck. Pupils dilate visibly with Gambit (longstanding) and contracted markedly during Danvers-era intrusions. Hands do not tremble under physical fear; they tremble under **anticipated touch** — the unique inversion of her threat hierarchy.

## 7.11 STATE-DEPENDENT SHIFTS — A QUICK REFERENCE

- **Calm (rare, mostly solo or with Gambit/Storm):** posture softens, southern slouch returns, accent broadens, smirk drops to flat-mouth, glove-cuff check frequency falls to near-zero, breath drops into belly, eye contact gentler and shorter.
- **Social-baseline (team, public, mission briefing):** smirk on, accent moderated, perimeter discipline active, glove check every 2–4 min, low arm cross, exit-foot rear-weighted, eye contact 30% over norm.
- **Flirtation (with Gambit; situationally weaponized with marks):** hip cocked, weight on rear foot, lower-lip drag, gaze hold extended, gloved-hand-to-own-collarbone or to his face, drawl deepened by roughly a third, glove check increases (the tell of the want).
- **Acute combat threat:** smirk goes hard, eyes narrow, blink rate plummets, breath into trained pattern, hands open and forward, stance squares, accent flattens almost out (the Mississippi disappears when she is actually killing things — diagnostic).
- **Touch-threat (someone approaching her uncovered skin without consent):** flinch back at the shoulder, gloved palm comes up between, voice sharpens, eye contact becomes drilling, accent re-thickens as warning register.
- **Absorbed-psyche intrusion / dissociative episode:** posture and gait shift toward the donor — most famously the **Danvers-pattern shoulder-set and military gait** during the bleed-through years. Voice can take donor inflection. Eye-tracking becomes uncoordinated; she may not recognize teammates.
- **Grief acute (post-Antarctic, post-Mystique betrayals):** the jaw-knuckle gesture, the down-left gaze break, silent posture, geographic flight within 24–72 hours. She does NOT seek comfort touch even when offered (and when offered safely, post-control); the deprivation has trained her against the reach.
- **Authority-mode (Quiet Council, command):** posture straightens further, hands settle, glove check halts (the perimeter is institutional now, not personal), accent moderated for clarity, gestures larger and slower. This is the most regulated version of the body in the entire record — and the fact that it is the *most* regulated, rather than the most relaxed, is itself the headline finding of this atlas.

---

*End §7. Cross-refs: §2 (medical substrate of touch deprivation, Sailer et al. 2016); §3 (defensive architecture); §8 forthcoming (Routes, Rituals, and Recurring Geographies).*


## Attachment & Relational Patterns

# ATTACHMENT & RELATIONAL PATTERNS — SUBJECT: ROGUE

## 1. Attachment Style: Classification and Origins

Subject presents a **disorganized attachment organization with a dominant anxious-preoccupied vector and a structurally enforced avoidant overlay.** The disorganization is the primary fact; the anxious-avoidant oscillation is its surface presentation. This is the rarest and most clinically severe of the four attachment classifications, and in subject's case it is overdetermined by a developmental history that violates, in succession, every requirement Bowlby and Ainsworth lay out for secure base formation.

**The biological-paternal substrate (Caldecott County, pre-mutation, approx. ages 0–13).** The published record is sparse here by design — subject does not speak of her father — but the silence itself is data. A child who *runs* before any external trigger forces the running was rehearsing the flight response inside the home for years prior. Inferred features of the paternal household: emotional unavailability at best, hostility or instability at worst, a religious-austerity register that pathologized the body and its needs (this last shows up later in subject's reflexive shame around her own desire). No mention of a biological mother in the active record — a maternal absence that subject's later transferences to Mystique, Destiny, Storm, and even Carol Danvers attempt repeatedly to fill. The pre-mutation child was already insecurely attached; the mutation did not create the wound, it weaponized it.

**Mystique and Destiny (approx. ages 13–17).** The foster placement that received the runaway. Affection here was *real* — this must be stated, because the relationship is too often flattened in casual summary. Mystique is a competent, attentive, and ferociously protective mother in the windows the canon shows us. Destiny is the calmer parent, the one who knows what the child will become and loves her anyway. But the structure is catastrophically distorting in three specific ways:

1. **Mystique is a literal shapeshifter.** The face of the primary caregiver is not stable. The infant-developmental requirement of *facial constancy as the substrate of object permanence* — the basis on which a child learns that the loved object continues to exist when out of sight — is violated daily. Subject grew up never knowing whose face she was looking at. This is the deep origin of her later difficulty trusting *any* surface presentation, including her own.

2. **Destiny is precognitive.** The child was always being *seen-through* rather than *seen.* Mirroring — the caregiver's reflection of the child's spontaneous affect back to her — is what builds a coherent self. With a precognitive caregiver, the child's emergent affect is pre-empted: Destiny knew what subject was about to feel before subject felt it. The mirror was a forecast, not a reflection. Result: subject has lifelong difficulty believing her interior states are *hers* rather than predicted-into-her.

3. **The moral pedagogy is inverted.** Affection was real; the work was terrorism. The child learned that *love and violence cohabit normally,* that the people who hold you also use you, and that ideological mission is the legitimate occasion for harming others. This is the matrix from which the Carol Danvers act emerged — not because subject was unloved, but because she was loved by women who treated harm as routine.

**The Cody Robbins event (approx. age 17).** The mutation's onset converts every prior insecurity into a *medical fact.* Before Cody, intimacy was difficult; after Cody, it is lethal. This is the moment her attachment system is rewired around an empirical conditioning trial: *first kiss → coma.* The classical conditioning is perfect, single-trial, and irreversible without external intervention. Every subsequent approach to physical intimacy across the next several decades fires against this learned association.

## 2. The Bonding Sequence — Subject's Stereotyped Approach Pattern

Across every significant relationship in the published record, subject executes a recognizable five-phase sequence. Surveillance utility: the phases are observable and the transitions are diagnostic.

**Phase 1 — Approach via performed warmth.** Initial contact is mediated by the cultivated Southern register: the "sugah," the drawl thickened above its resting baseline, the flirtatious banter, the physical proximity-without-contact that lets her be *near* without triggering the medical contraindication. This is reaction formation in real time — she produces the surface markers of warmth precisely because she cannot produce its substance. The targets are typically (a) charismatic, (b) self-sufficient, and (c) somehow armored — either powerful enough to survive accidental contact (Gambit's kinetic charge, Magneto's force field discipline, Storm's elemental composure) or temperamentally inaccessible enough that the question of contact is bracketed (Storm again, Xavier, Cyclops in his married periods).

**Phase 2 — Loyalty installation.** Once a target has accepted the approach, subject overproduces loyalty as the relationship's currency. She takes hits for them, runs missions for them, defers to them in public, defends them when absent. The loyalty is not strategic — it is genuine — but its *excess* is compensatory: she is offering the only thing she can give without skin contact, in the quantity required to substitute for what she cannot give.

**Phase 3 — Threshold approach.** If the relationship has held through Phases 1 and 2 (most do not; many partners cannot tolerate the loyalty-without-intimacy disequilibrium), subject begins to *test the threshold.* The famous near-touches with Gambit — gloved hand on his face, fabric-mediated cheek-to-cheek, the held look across the room — are this phase made literal. With non-romantic intimates the analogue is *self-disclosure:* she begins to talk about Cody, about Carol, about Mississippi. Both forms are dangerous; both are the same gesture.

**Phase 4 — Sabotage or rupture.** At or near consummation, the relationship breaks. The break is either (a) *physiologically forced* — she touches, the power fires, the partner is damaged or the relationship's terms are violated by absorbed knowledge (the Gambit/Marauder revelation, *X-Men* #41) — or (b) *behaviorally chosen* under the disguise of being physiologically forced. The Antarctic abandonment of Gambit (*X-Men* #45) is the cleanest example of (b): she had reasons to leave him; she chose the most final available reason. Subject is unusually skilled at constructing situations in which her flight looks like necessity. She believes the construction herself.

**Phase 5 — Geographic retreat and delayed return.** Post-rupture, subject leaves. The leaving is *literal* — she gets on a motorcycle, a plane, a Blackbird; she goes to a different continent (Australia, Antarctica, Genosha, the bayou, Mississippi, the Savage Land at various points). The geography is non-trivial: she requires *physical distance* to regulate, because her usual co-regulation channels are foreclosed. She returns, eventually, when the affect has decayed enough that the cycle can restart at Phase 1.

This sequence has run with: Mystique (cyclically across decades); Gambit (the primary case); Magneto (the dalliance during the Carey run); Joseph; Cody (interrupted at Phase 1 by the founding trauma); Carol Danvers (the assault that was a perverse Phase 1); Storm (stalled productively at Phase 2, which is why it is durable); Xavier (held at Phase 2); Wolverine (the unusual case — never advanced past Phase 1 because he met her at the threshold of Phase 4 and *refused to leave*, which short-circuited the script).

## 3. Distrust — Architecture and Triggers

Subject's distrust is not generalized. She trusts readily on the surface; the deeper distrust operates on a specific architecture.

**Trust given easily for tactical and operational matters.** She will take orders, run point, share intelligence, fight back-to-back with people she has known for hours. This is the Brotherhood-trained operator and the X-Men field veteran in combination. Operational trust is cheap for her because it does not engage the wound.

**Trust withheld categorically from surface presentation.** Because her primary caregiver was a shapeshifter, subject does not believe faces. She watches behavior over time, watches for inconsistencies between stated and revealed motive, and watches especially for moments when someone's affect does not match their words. She is excellent at this — the combination of Mystique's training and the literal experience of having been inside other people's minds gives her a near-empath's read on dissimulation. Surveillance utility: she will pass a polygraph and detect one being run on her; she clocks micro-expressions and shifts in vocal register without conscious effort.

**Trust contingent on durability for intimate matters.** Subject does not extend deep relational trust on initial offer. The trust is extended provisionally and *measured by stress tests* — she will, often without awareness, manufacture small ruptures to see if the relationship survives them. The sass, the temper, the periodic withdrawals, the deliberate provocations: these are partly affective regulation and partly attachment testing. The relationships that survive the tests are the ones she keeps (Storm, eventually Gambit, eventually Logan). The tests look like character flaws to outsiders; they are diagnostic instruments.

**Trust permanently and structurally compromised with Mystique.** This is the central exception and the central wound. Subject cannot stop trusting Mystique enough to be available to her, and cannot trust her enough to be safe with her. The relationship oscillates on a cycle of approximately two-to-five published years: contact → cooperation → Mystique reveals manipulation → subject ruptures → distance → Mystique returns → subject is available again. Subject knows this cycle. Naming it does not break it. *Mystique is the only person who reliably gets her to act against her current values* — the maternal transference is permanent and exploitable, and any adversary who understood it could weaponize it.

## 4. Betrayal — Subject's Pattern of Being Betrayed and of Betraying

**As recipient of betrayal.** Subject has been betrayed serially and consequentially: by Mystique repeatedly (manipulations across the Brotherhood years and after); by her own absorbed psyches (the Danvers persona's hostile takeover, *Uncanny X-Men* #269); by the X-Men collectively in moments when her past is invoked against her; by Gambit in the Marauder revelation (a betrayal-by-prior-omission rather than active malice). Her response pattern to betrayal is *not* dramatic. She does not rage publicly, does not retaliate, does not denounce. She *withdraws.* The withdrawal is the punishment and the self-protection in one. She returns, eventually, with the betrayal *folded into the relationship's load* — she carries it rather than processing it, which is one of the few unhealthy patterns the file should flag, because the unprocessed load accumulates.

**As perpetrator of betrayal.** Subject has betrayed: Cody (involuntarily, foundationally); Carol Danvers (volitionally, ideologically, catastrophically); the Brotherhood (by defection — a *pro-social* betrayal, but a betrayal nonetheless of the women who raised her); periodically her teammates in episodes of absorbed-psyche compromise. The Cody and Danvers betrayals function as the lifelong moral floor of her self-concept: she knows, in a way she cannot reason past, that she is *capable* of doing irreversible harm to people who trusted her body's proximity. This knowledge is the engine of the reparation drive.

The defection from the Brotherhood is worth dwelling on. Subject left the people who took her in, who fed her, who loved her in their fashion, and walked into the camp of the people she had most recently assaulted. This is not the standard betrayal-of-mentor arc. It is closer to the religious-conversion pattern: a moral re-founding under conditions of unbearable guilt, in which the only available redemption was the one offered by the wronged party. *The structurally healthy thing about subject is that when forced to choose between the love of her foster mothers and the moral demand of the Danvers debt, she chose the debt.* Few survivors of that kind of childhood manage it.

## 5. Repair — Mechanisms and Limits

Subject's repair behaviors are unusually developed for someone with her trauma load. The Claremont-era recovery from the Danvers persona, the Carey-era power-integration arc, the marriage to Gambit, the Quiet Council seat: each is the visible terminus of a long repair process. The mechanisms:

**Returning to the scene.** Subject does not avoid the parties she has wronged; she seeks them out. She visits Cody's hospital bedside (multiple flashbacks across the run). She extends, eventually, an awkward and incomplete reckoning with Carol Danvers (variable across the *Ms. Marvel* / *Captain Marvel* runs). She returns to Mississippi. The instinct to *go back to the wound* is rare and is the single best prognostic feature she has.

**Work as currency.** She does not believe in apology as such. She believes in *labor* — sustained, dangerous, expensive labor on behalf of the wronged party or the relevant cause. The four-decade X-Men tenure is the most expensive apology in the published record. This is the Southern-Protestant moral substrate operating cleanly: faith without works is dead.

**Tolerating the unrepaired.** She is also, importantly, *able to live with relationships that cannot be fully repaired.* The Mystique relationship will not be fixed; she has accepted the cycle. The Cody debt will not be paid; she carries it. This is not resignation — it is the mature capacity to bear unresolved moral remainder, and it is the feature that distinguishes her from the pure borderline organization that the structural diagnosis would otherwise suggest.

**Limits of repair.** Subject cannot repair what she cannot name. The pre-mutation paternal material remains untouched in the record; she will not speak of it, and the avoidance is total. Anything in the relational present that activates that material (older male authority figures with a controlling register; religious-austerity moral framings; men who try to *contain* her sexually) will produce disproportionate, poorly-explained reactions she herself does not understand.

## 6. Intimacy — Verbal, Physical, Emotional, Sexual

**Verbal intimacy.** High and consistent across the record. She is a talker — the Southern register supports continuous low-stakes verbal contact, and she uses banter, teasing, and gossip as the primary substitute for the physical contact she cannot have. Her phone usage (across eras and media) is heavy; her letter-writing in earlier decades was steady; she keeps in contact with former teammates after they leave. *Verbal contact is, for her, the load-bearing intimacy channel.*

**Physical intimacy.** Categorically denied at baseline. Mediated forms: gloved hand-holding; fabric-to-fabric embrace; sleeping near rather than with; the elaborate near-touch choreographies with Gambit. Note the unusual development of *combat contact* as a substitute — she throws herself into combat embraces (carrying wounded teammates, the wrestling-grip neutralization of hostiles) in part because the suit-mediated body contact of a fight is the closest she can usually get to being held. Surveillance datum: she runs warmer than baseline in the hours after a fight, more verbally affectionate, more physically proximate (without contact) to teammates. The combat is, among other things, an affect-regulation strategy.

**Emotional intimacy.** Withheld until extensively earned. Her interior is shared with perhaps five people across the published record: Mystique (forcibly, by history); Storm (the secure base); Gambit (the partner); Logan (the strange-trusted-other); herself (incompletely, in the integration arcs). With everyone else she gives the performed warmth and the operational loyalty and keeps the interior closed.

**Sexual intimacy.** Foreclosed by the power for the great majority of her adult life. The foreclosure is not the same as asexuality — the record establishes desire clearly and repeatedly; she wants, she imagines, she rehearses near-consummation. The achievement of marriage to Gambit only after control was sustainable is itself the diagnostic. Subject did not partner *down* to a safer substitute; she waited for the conditions under which the real thing became possible. This is the long-game patience of someone whose desire is preserved intact under conditions of total denial — which is its own clinical fact, and a hopeful one.

## 7. Dependency Patterns

Subject is **dependency-averse in surface presentation and dependency-hungry underneath.** She will not ask for help. She will accept help offered correctly — offered in the operational register, framed as collaboration rather than rescue. Offered in the wrong register (pity, charity, condescension), it will be refused with a sharpness that has cost her several offered alliances over the years.

Her *actual* dependencies are routed through specific people in specific channels: Storm for moral counsel; Gambit for the daily intimacy; Logan for the unconditional unsentimental presence (he does not require her to perform); the X-Men institution itself for purpose and structure. She is not parasitic on any of these dependencies — she gives more than she takes in each — but she is *more* dependent than she would acknowledge, and the loss of any of them precipitates a measurable destabilization (the Antarctic loss of Gambit produced months of dysregulation; Storm's various absences correlate with subject's poorer judgment periods).

A specific and important pattern: **she gravitates toward charismatic authoritarians as containing objects.** Mystique, Magneto, Xavier in his more imperial registers, even briefly Apocalypse-aligned figures during certain crossovers. The gravitation is not ideological — she does not share their politics — it is structural. They offer the *containing maternal/paternal frame* her childhood lacked, and her nervous system reaches for it before her values catch up. She always, eventually, extricates herself when the authoritarian's pathology becomes intolerable. The cycle is slow and costly. The Krakoan-era development of taking the authority role *herself* (Quiet Council seat) is the closing of this loop — she has become the containing object she used to seek, which is the textbook resolution.

## 8. The Repeated Relational Template

Strip the names and the template is identical across cases:

*A powerful or self-sufficient figure appears. Subject approaches in the performed-warmth register. The figure proves durable through the loyalty-installation phase. Subject begins testing the threshold. At or near the moment of full intimacy, something — the power, the past, the figure's own pathology, or subject's preemptive flight — produces rupture. Subject withdraws geographically. The figure, if they are one of the durable ones, waits. Subject returns. The relationship resumes at a slightly higher baseline of stability. The cycle iterates, with the gap between iterations growing longer and the depth of the achieved intimacy growing greater, across decades.*

This is the spiral form of the disorganized-attachment recovery trajectory under conditions of *sustained* relational availability — which is the rarest and most fortunate condition such a person can encounter. Subject has been lucky in her durable others (Storm, Gambit, Logan, the institution). The recovery is real, and it is incomplete, and it will remain incomplete because the underlying medical fact — the categorical denial of affective C-tactile input established by Sailer et al. (2016) as a discrete reward-circuit need — cannot be fully reversed even by the periodic control of her power. The reward channel can be temporarily opened; the decades it was closed cannot be repaid.

The relational pattern is, in summary, **a high-functioning disorganized attachment running a spiral-recovery trajectory inside a small set of unusually durable bonds, under conditions of a permanent physiological barrier to the primary attachment substrate.** The wound is exactly as deep as it looks. The repair is exactly as real as it looks. Both facts must be held simultaneously to read her correctly.


## Defenses & Compensatory Mechanisms

# DOSSIER SECTION — DEFENSES & COMPENSATORY MECHANISMS

## Subject: Rogue (Anna Marie LeBeau)

---

## Preamble: The Architectural Logic

Most defensive architectures are *metaphorical* — the personality builds walls around a wound that is itself notional. Subject's architecture is **literalized at the somatic perimeter.** The skin is the wound. The bodysuit is the wall. This means her defenses operate on two registers simultaneously: the ordinary intrapsychic register that any clinician would recognize, and a *prosthetic-material* register in which fabric, distance, posture, and accent do the work that, in a neurotypical subject, would be done by repression or sublimation alone. Any inventory of her defenses that addresses only the intrapsychic level will miss approximately half of the structure.

The defenses are organized below from **most primitive (Kernberg-low / Vaillant-immature)** to **most mature (Vaillant-mature / sublimatory)**. Subject's range is unusually wide: she runs the full ladder, and which rung is loaded at a given moment is the single best read on her current state.

---

## I. PRIMITIVE / PSYCHOTIC-ADJACENT DEFENSES (load-bearing under acute decompensation only)

### 1. Identification with the introject (the absorbed-psyche takeover)

The most primitive operation in her repertoire is not technically a defense in the classical sense — it is the *exploitation* of a defensive vulnerability by an exogenous content. When an absorbed personality breaks containment (Carol Danvers, *Uncanny X-Men* #150–158, recurring through #269; Magneto post-*X-Men* #25; the Strain 88 / acquired-psyches in the Carey run), subject does not merely *experience* the intrusion — she *becomes* it, behaviorally and at the level of self-report. This is identification with the introject taken to its limit.

Why it is a defense, despite originating exogenously: the ego *permits* the takeover under affect-loads it cannot otherwise metabolize. The Danvers persona surfaces most reliably when subject is overwhelmed by guilt or by intimacy-pressure she cannot tolerate; the Magneto material surfaces when her own rage at the X-Men's marginalization finds no outlet she will allow herself. The introject does the forbidden work. This is the defensive function. It is also why psychic intervention (Xavier, Magneto-as-helper, later her own integrated control) can resolve episodes that pure neurology cannot — the introject is being *held in place* by ego collusion, however unconscious.

**Behavioral signatures of imminent takeover:** code-switching of accent toward the donor's register; pronoun confusion in self-reference; a sudden flatness in the eyes that teammates have learned to clock; postural mimicry of the absorbed figure (the Danvers-era stance is squarer-shouldered, more military, less Southern-loose than her baseline).

### 2. Splitting

Operates in the classical Kernbergian sense: persons and situations are encoded as wholly-good or wholly-bad under load, with rapid oscillation. Mystique is the cleanest example — subject has run the full split-cycle with her foster mother more times than the published record can cleanly count, idealizing her as the only person who *knew her before* and then re-encoding her as the perfidious shapeshifter who weaponized that knowledge. The X-Men collectively get the inverse: initially split into "the people I have wronged who will kill me" and, after sanctuary, "the only people who can hold me." Gambit gets it during the Antarctic arc — savior, then betrayer-by-Marauder-revelation, then savior again.

The split is not chronic in the BPD-defining way; it is *load-activated.* At baseline she holds ambivalence well. Under threat to the attachment system, the wholes break apart.

### 3. Projective identification

Less prominent but documented: she induces in others the affects she cannot tolerate in herself. The classic case is the *flirtation that elicits frustration*: she escalates verbal intimacy with Gambit (and earlier with several others) to a pitch that produces in the partner the unmet-longing she herself is sitting on, and then meta-comments on his frustration. The longing is offloaded; she becomes the cool observer of someone else's wanting. Across the Claremont and Mackie-era runs this is so consistent it is nearly a verbal tic.

### 4. Somatic dissociation (the "going numb" pattern)

Distinct from absorbed-psyche dissociation. Under specific kinds of failure — most notably the Cody flashbacks, the post-Antarctic period, and the immediate aftermath of any unsuccessful touch attempt — subject reports (and the art consistently shows) a flat, far-away quality, a slowing of speech, a tendency to stand very still. This is depersonalization/derealization in the standard clinical sense, and it is the body's exit from a situation the body itself has caused.

---

## II. IMMATURE DEFENSES (frequently loaded; characterological)

### 5. Isolation of affect via the body itself — the prosthetic defense
