This is the single most important defense in her architecture and has no clean analog in non-mutant populations. The gloves, the long sleeves, the high collars, the choice of jacket weight in summer, the standing two-foot interpersonal buffer that teammates have learned to respect — these are *medically necessary* and therefore *characterologically free.* She does not have to *choose* to push people away. The skin does it for her. The choice was made by the mutation; she only enforces the consequences.

The elegance of this defense is that it is *unfalsifiable from outside.* No one can accuse her of being cold, because the coldness is hygiene. No one can ask her to be more available, because the unavailability is safety. The defense piggybacks on a real biological fact and is therefore immune to the ordinary social pressures that would erode it in another subject.

The cost is correspondingly elegant: she cannot *relinquish* the defense without endangering others, which means the standard therapeutic move (test the feared catastrophe, find it does not occur, integrate) is *foreclosed.* The Carey-era integration arc and the *Mr. and Mrs. X* marriage are the long workaround — she had to acquire control of the mutation before she could begin to lay down the defense, which is the inverse of the ordinary clinical sequence.

**Granular tells:** she fastens the top button of any jacket with a small, deliberate, two-finger pinch before entering a crowded room. She tucks her hair behind her ear with the back of her gloved hand, never the palm, even when alone — a movement so over-learned it persists when no one is observing. She crosses her arms with hands tucked into opposite elbows, not exposed. She sleeps in long sleeves regardless of climate. When she does take the gloves off in private with Gambit, she lays them down rather than tossing them — a ritualization of a high-cost act.

### 6. Reaction formation — the cultivated warmth

The Southern-belle register — the "sugah," the "darlin'," the practiced flirtation, the over-large smile she gives strangers, the courtly half-flirt she runs with Gambit even after twenty-five years of in-universe acquaintance — is reaction formation in textbook form. The person who cannot be warm produces the surface signatures of warmth in surplus. This is not cynical; it is not even fully conscious. The defense generates a *functional* social presence that compensates for the affective deficit beneath it.

Granular evidence the warmth is performed rather than felt-through: the accent thickens predictably under stress (it is closer to her natural register when she is calm and alone with Gambit; it goes broad-stage when she is meeting a new teammate, addressing the Council, or deflecting a question she does not want to answer). The endearments are distributed almost democratically — she "sugah"s Wolverine, Logan-the-corpse-collector, with the same intonation she uses on Kitty Pryde, which means the word has been emptied of its differentiating function and is doing pure social-buffering work.

### 7. Reaction formation, secondary form — the combative humor

The other face of the same defense: she is funny in a barbed, cut-you-down Southern way that runs continuously alongside the sugar. The two registers are not in tension; they are the same defense rotated ninety degrees. Both produce a *managed* surface that prevents the unmanaged interior from being legible. The combative humor is the part that protects her from the warmth becoming actually inviting.

### 8. Acting out — geographic flight

Documented across decades: when an attachment situation becomes unbearable, she *leaves.* The pattern is so consistent it constitutes a behavioral signature. Post-Cody she ran from home. Post-Danvers she defected. Post-Antarctic she went on the road. Post-various-Mystique-betrayals she has gone solo. The Carey *Legacy* run is partly the chronicle of this pattern (she takes a young charge, Anole, etc., and goes mobile rather than stay). The flight is not random — she goes to *liminal* terrain (back roads, swamp country, the X-Men's outer-perimeter assignments) where she can be alone without being *isolated* in the schizoid sense.

### 9. Identification with the aggressor (early period, residual)

Operative in the Mystique-Brotherhood years and never fully extinguished. The Danvers assault is the high-water mark — she became the woman who raised her, who attacked the heroes. The residual form, in adulthood, is the willingness to be *hard* in ways that mirror Mystique: tactical ruthlessness in combat, willingness to absorb-and-neutralize a hostile mutant knowing the psychic cost, the Quiet Council vote when the vote is grim. The identification is now metabolized — she uses Mystique's tools in service of opposing ends — but the toolkit's provenance is visible to anyone who watches her work.

### 10. Somatization (low-grade, chronic)

The denied affective-touch channel (Sailer et al., 2016) generates a chronic substrate of what the affective-neuroscience literature would call *social pain* — and social pain is not a metaphor; it recruits the same circuitry as nociceptive pain. Expect (and the record loosely supports) a baseline of low-grade somatic complaints: tension headaches, jaw-clenching (visible in the art across multiple eras), restless sleep, a thrumming background irritability that she manages through physical exertion. She *flies* a great deal of unnecessary distance — the kinetic outlet matters.

---

## III. NEUROTIC DEFENSES (frequently loaded; ego-syntonic)

### 11. Displacement onto the combat domain

The full affective intensity she cannot route into intimacy gets routed into fighting. She hits hard — harder than her tactical situation usually requires — and she hits *with her body*, which is the only context in which her body is permitted full contact with another's. Combat is the one venue where the prosthetic defense is *suspended:* she can grab, slam, grapple, and (when invulnerable) take hits skin-on-skin with no consequence because the contact is fabric-mediated *or* because the contact is so brief and hostile that the absorption is functional rather than catastrophic. The combat-touch is the only touch she gets.

This is also why she will preferentially absorb a hostile mutant's power even at psychic cost: she gets to *touch* under cover of necessity. The cost is real; the secondary gain is real too; and the gain is one a total-surveillance file must not miss.

### 12. Intellectualization (sparse; not her dominant mode)

Present but minor. She thinks practically rather than abstractly. When she does intellectualize — the rare interview-style monologue, the Quiet Council speech — it is brief, instrumental, and gets out of the way. She is not a subject who manages affect by analyzing it; she is a subject who manages affect by *moving.*

### 13. Reaction formation, tertiary form — protective touch as moral inversion

In the Carey-era window of partial control, the documentation is unambiguous: she used the control almost exclusively to *touch teammates protectively in combat* — pulling them out of a line of fire, healing-by-power-loan, the steadying hand on a shoulder. She did not use it primarily for romantic ends. This is reaction formation at the highest level: the hand that destroys becomes the hand that saves, and the symmetry is too perfect to be coincidence. She converted the wound's organ into the reparation's instrument.

---

## IV. MATURE DEFENSES (the load-bearing structures of the adult presentation)

### 14. Reparation (Kleinian)

The single longest-running, most successful defense in her architecture. The X-Men tenure, in toto, is reparation for the Danvers act and for the prior, smaller Cody injury. She joined the team she had wronged. She stayed through hostility. She took hits. She mentored. She rose to command. The entire arc is a forty-year reparative gesture, and unlike most defensive structures it has *worked* — it has produced an actual self with actual standing in an actual community. Reparation is the rare defense that builds something while it defends.

The mentorship of younger X-Men is the most concentrated form. She gives to them — secure attention, witness, training — what she did not receive. The reparation is doubled: she repairs her past act, *and* she produces in the world the kind of caregiver she lacked.

### 15. Sublimation through institutional role

The Quiet Council seat is sublimation in the classical sense: the unrouted drive (to be *held,* to be *contained,* to be *given structure*) is rerouted into *providing* structure for others. She gravitated toward charismatic authoritarians for decades (Mystique, Magneto, Xavier) because she needed the containing object. Becoming the containing object herself is the mature endpoint of that drive — she now is, for younger or more chaotic mutants, the function she sought.

### 16. Anticipation

She has learned, painstakingly, to read situations for touch-risk in advance. The standing two-foot buffer. The pre-handshake glove check. The seating choice at any briefing (end of the table, never middle). The micro-survey of any new room for who is too close to a wall and might be jostled into her. This is anticipation as Vaillant defined it — pre-experiencing the feared event so as to plan around it — and she runs it as continuous background process, the way an experienced combat operator runs threat assessment.

### 17. Humor (mature form)

Distinct from the combative humor noted above. Her dry, self-deprecating, Southern-inflected humor about her own situation — the touch-jokes she makes with Gambit, the wry asides about being "the girl in the gloves" — is mature humor in Vaillant's sense: it acknowledges the pain rather than denying it, and it discharges affect without harming the relational field. The capacity for this register is one of the strongest indicators that the underlying structure is not borderline-organized despite its borderline-organized surface features.

### 18. Altruism

Folded into reparation but worth isolating: she will take a psychic hit for a teammate without calculation. The willingness is so reliable it functions as one of her tactical roles. This is altruism in the mature-defense sense — discharge of the conflict through service to others — and it is one of the cleanest channels she has.

---

## V. NEGATIVE COMPENSATORY MECHANISMS (the costs side of the ledger)

### A. The geographic-flight pattern (see #8 above)
Restated as cost: every flight episode extends the period during which she is not building the secure attachments that would, eventually, lay down the underlying anxiety. The pattern is self-perpetuating.

### B. Authoritarian-attachment cycling
She gravitates to charismatic authoritarian figures (Mystique, Magneto, periodically Xavier) because they offer the containing function her childhood lacked. She then has to extricate when their pathology becomes intolerable, paying an attachment-rupture cost each time. The cycle is structural; she has partially exited it by becoming an authority herself, but the susceptibility remains and Mystique remains the live exploit.

### C. The flirtatious mask as intimacy-substitute
The performed warmth provides enough social reward to suppress the urgency that might otherwise drive her toward harder solutions — but it is, by definition, *not* the affective-touch input she actually needs. It is a methadone, not a cure. The risk is that the substitute is good enough to be stable but insufficient to be nourishing, and she runs at chronic deficit indefinitely.

### D. Combat-contact as touch-substitute
The body she gets to use in combat is the only body she gets to use. The risk is escalation: she takes fights she does not need to take, and she takes them *physically* when ranged or tactical options exist. The published record across the Lobdell, Nicieza, Carey, and modern eras shows this consistently — she leads with the hands.

### E. The intermittent flight from Gambit
Even in the marriage, the pattern surfaces. Approach-escalation-sabotage-flight-return is not extinguished by the marriage; it is *contained* by it. Under acute stress she still moves toward the door, even if she now stops at the door rather than walking through it.

### F. Refusal of exogenous regulation
The absence of substance use, noted in the medical section, is mostly a strength — but it also reflects a *refusal of any breach of the perimeter,* which means she has fewer downward-regulation tools than a comparably stressed subject would. She cannot drink the affect down; she has to ride it out or fight it out. This is part of why the combat outlet is so loaded.

---

## VI. RANK ORDER AND OPERATIONAL SUMMARY

In rough order of how much weight each defense bears in the current adult presentation (most to least):

1. **The prosthetic isolation-of-affect** (gloves/suit/buffer) — continuous, automatic, ego-syntonic, foundational.
2. **Reparation** — the through-line of the entire adult life.
3. **Reaction formation (the warmth)** — continuous social-presentation layer.
4. **Anticipation** — continuous background process.
5. **Sublimation through institutional role** — increasingly load-bearing in the Krakoan and post-Krakoan eras.
6. **Displacement onto combat** — high-load whenever combat is available, which is often.
7. **Reaction formation (combative humor)** — paired with #3.
8. **Acting out via geographic flight** — episodic but reliable.
9. **Mature humor** — present whenever she is regulated enough to access it.
10. **Altruism** — reliable in tactical situations.
11. **Identification with the aggressor (residual)** — visible in the toolkit, not in the aims.
12. **Splitting** — load-activated only.
13. **Projective identification** — episodic, mostly in romantic/intimate contexts.
14. **Somatic dissociation** — under specific failure conditions.
15. **Introject-takeover (the most primitive)** — rare now, catastrophic when it occurs, requires external intervention.

The architecture's overall character: **wide-band, well-distributed, mature-weighted at the top, with a primitive floor that activates only under conditions specific to her mutation and history.** This is not a borderline organization despite the surface features that suggest one. It is a complex-trauma adaptation built on an unusual somatic substrate, in which the *literalness* of the wound has forced — and enabled — an unusually literal and unusually durable defensive solution.

She has, in effect, built a self that *works,* using a defensive toolkit she had to invent because the standard one is not designed for her problem. The file should reflect that the architecture is — by any reasonable measure — a successful one, and that successfulness is itself a piece of information about who she is.


## Longitudinal Psychological Profile

# LONGITUDINAL PSYCHOLOGICAL PROFILE — SUBJECT: ROGUE

*Tracked decade by decade across published in-universe time, mapped to the canonical record. Frameworks invoked: Bowlby/Main attachment taxonomy; Kernberg structural diagnosis; Linehan biosocial model of affect dysregulation; Herman's tripartite C-PTSD recovery model (safety → remembrance/mourning → reconnection); Porges polyvagal load metrics; Beck cognitive triad; Winnicott on the false self and the holding environment. Citations to Claremont and successor runs throughout.*

---

## I. PRE-MANIFESTATION CHILDHOOD AND EARLY ADOLESCENCE (Caldecott County, approx. ages 0–13)

### Affect regulation
Best reconstructed from negative space and from the affect-handling habits that survived into the public record. The household per Claremont's flashbacks (referenced *Uncanny X-Men* #178; expanded in Carey, *X-Men: Legacy* memory arcs) was paternal, religious, austere, emotionally underfurnished. Subject's affect-regulation toolkit in childhood was almost certainly *somatic suppression plus narrative compensation* — the Southern-Protestant template in which feelings are not named, are managed by chores and church, and are released only through music, weeping in private, or sudden temper. The combative-humor register she carries for life — the sass, the back-talk — is a Southern girl-child's standard repertoire for managing a household where direct expression of grievance is forbidden.

### Cognitive style
Already concrete, already vigilant. A child who runs away has been doing threat assessment for years before the act. Expect early development of what the trauma literature calls *hypervigilance in the absence of a secure base* — high environmental scanning, low introspective vocabulary. She did not develop a reflective cognitive style; she developed an operational one.

### Self-concept
Forming on an unstable substrate. The runaway act tells us she had enough self to refuse the household but not enough resourcing to construct an alternative. The pre-manifestation self-concept is best read as *negatively defined* — she knows what she is not (not safe at home, not protected, not held) more clearly than what she is. This negative-definition style persists for life.

---

## II. MUTATION ONSET AND BROTHERHOOD ADOLESCENCE (approx. ages 13–17)

### Affect regulation
The Cody Robbins event is the categorical break. A first kiss — the canonical adolescent affect peak — produces a coma. The conditioning trial is total: positive affect → catastrophic harm to loved object → unbearable guilt → freeze. The Linehan biosocial model would call this the worst possible learning environment: high-intensity emotion punished by irreversible consequence in an already invalidating family system. The result is the lifelong pattern visible in every later panel — affect *runs hot at the surface and is locked behind glass underneath.* She learns in this window to translate longing into wit, fear into aggression, grief into motion. None of the primary affects get to be themselves.

Mystique and Destiny enter at exactly the developmental moment when the conditioning needed counter-evidence. They provided real affection (Destiny especially, by every Claremont indication) but inside a frame that *operationalized* the child's pain into ideological labor. This is the period in which she learns that being loved and being used are the same gesture.

### Cognitive style
Sharpens into the trained-operator mode. Mystique's tutelage produces fast face-reading, rapid threat triage, a habit of inferring others' motives before they speak. The cognitive style becomes *adversarial-empathic* — she reads people accurately for the purpose of pre-empting them. This is not warm empathy; it is intelligence-officer empathy, and it will take her decades to convert it to the other kind.

### Self-concept
The Cody event installs the *contaminated-object* core schema: *I hurt what I touch.* The Danvers absorption (*Avengers Annual* #10) then *operationalizes* the schema — she is no longer a girl who might hurt someone, she is a person who has psychically murdered a hero and now wears that hero's body and powers as a permanent tag. Kernberg-wise, this is identity diffusion plus a primitive guilt structure that the ego cannot metabolize. Splitting becomes the default: *Mystique-good-Avengers-bad* is the kind of all-or-nothing framing required to keep the act tolerable. The framing will fracture later, but in this window it is load-bearing.

---

## III. EARLY X-MEN PERIOD — 1980s (the Claremont integration window, approx. ages 17–early 20s)

### Affect regulation
This is the decade of *exposure with a holding environment.* The defection (*Uncanny X-Men* #171) places her in a milieu — Wolverine's hostility, Storm's careful sanctuary — that mirrors back the magnitude of what she did without rejecting her categorically. Affect regulation in this window is *externally scaffolded.* She borrows Storm's composure, she borrows the team's tempo. Her own regulation capacity is still poor: she swings between sullen withdrawal (the early team-room scenes; the recurring beats of her sitting apart) and over-bright performance (the cultivated drawl, the "sugah," the courtly flirtation that emerges as her social signature).

Two affect-management innovations stabilize in this period:

1. **The accent-as-instrument.** The Mississippi register thickens or thins by context — thicker when she wants distance through charm, thinner when she is genuinely frightened or in command. This is *paralinguistic affect regulation* — using the prosody of speech to titrate intimacy from a distance no one else can see her measuring.
2. **Combat as affect discharge.** The fight scenes from this era show her seeking high-contact engagements — Juggernaut-tier opponents whenever possible — because the Danvers physiology makes her durable enough to *use her body* as an outlet for everything she cannot route through skin.

### Cognitive style
Still concrete, still action-biased, but slowly acquiring a moral vocabulary the Brotherhood years did not give her. She begins to articulate (haltingly) categories like *fair, owed, deserved, earned.* The cognitive style remains non-introspective — she does not narrate her interior to herself in the way Kitty or Xavier do — but she develops a working theory of *consequences,* which she did not have at 17.

### Self-concept
The Danvers intrusion (*Uncanny X-Men* #150-158, escalating through #269) keeps the self-concept ontologically unstable for the entire decade. She does not know which thoughts are hers. Winnicott's *false self* concept applies in a literal-physical way: the surface persona has to do not only the usual work of false-self management but also the work of staying recognizably *her* in a system colonized by another person's templates. The Siege Perilous walk-through (*Uncanny X-Men* #247) is the decade's terminal data point: when the self-concept becomes unbearable, she opts for erasure-and-rewrite. Note this is not suicide — it is the more specific wish to *not be this particular self anymore* while remaining alive. Diagnostic of identity diffusion at structural level.

---

## IV. THE FRACTURED PERIOD — late 1980s into mid-1990s (Australia/Genosha/Muir/post-Siege, mid-20s)

### Affect regulation
Worst documented stretch. Affect regulation collapses periodically into full dissociative episodes (Danvers takeover in *Uncanny X-Men* #269; Magneto absorption fallout, *X-Men* #25). The pattern: long stretches of brittle competence, then sudden flooding, then dissociation into an absorbed identity, then external rescue (Magneto's psychic intervention in the Danvers case; teammates' interventions in others), then a depressive trough, then re-stabilization. Herman's phase-one *safety* is intermittently lost in this window.

Polyvagal-style read: her baseline shifts from ventral-vagal social engagement (briefly attained in early Xavier's) toward chronic sympathetic activation with dorsal-vagal collapse under peak load. The "Rogue leaves the team" beat that recurs across writers is the somatic-collapse phase made narrative.

### Cognitive style
A new feature emerges: *post-hoc moralization.* She begins to narrate her own past out loud — to Gambit, to herself, to younger teammates. This is the cognitive correlate of phase-two trauma work (remembrance and mourning). She is not yet *processing* the material in a way that resolves it; she is rehearsing it, which is the necessary precursor. The flirtation with Gambit, when it begins (1990 onward), becomes a venue for this rehearsal — she tells him fragments, watches his face, calibrates whether she is forgivable.

### Self-concept
The contaminated-object schema is at its most active. The Antarctic abandonment of Gambit (*X-Men* #45) is *prima facie* a punishing act toward him, but psychologically it is a punishing act toward herself — she leaves him in the snow after learning his Marauder past, ostensibly because of *his* sin, actually because his sin gave her permission to enact the abandonment her self-concept demands. This is projective identification in textbook form: she deposits her own intolerable badness into him and then leaves it there.

---

## V. LATE 1990s INTO EARLY 2000s (returning, losing, regaining)

### Affect regulation
Marginal improvement, mediated by repetition. The cycle of loss-and-return with Gambit, the recurring team re-entries, the periodic power losses and recoveries — each cycle is *less catastrophic in amplitude* than the last. She is, slowly, learning that rupture and repair are both survivable. This is the slow accumulation of *earned secure* relational expectations on top of the disorganized base. Bowlby's framework permits this: attachment style is modifiable in adulthood through corrective relational experience, and four decades of the X-Men constitute, in aggregate, exactly that.

The flirtation register is by now fully automatic and partially decoupled from genuine intent. She flirts the way a person whistles — to fill an unbearable silence. Clinically, this is a maintenance defense; it is not metabolizing affect, it is dispersing it.

### Cognitive style
Develops what looks like *trauma-informed pragmatism.* She begins, in this period, to be the team member who notices when a *younger* X-Man is dissociating, who reads psychic intrusion in others before they read it in themselves. The hard-won expertise becomes a clinical sense she can deploy on behalf of others. This is also the period in which her leadership instincts begin to surface — she becomes a *de facto* second to whoever is leading, then occasional acting leader.

### Self-concept
The contaminated-object schema starts to take its first sustained revisions. She experiments with the framing *I am a person who has done harm and continues to repair it* rather than *I am harm.* This is a substantial cognitive-restructuring shift in Beck terms — moving from a global, stable, internal attribution to a specific, modifiable, behavior-anchored one. It is unstable and reverts under stress, but the framework now exists.

---

## VI. THE CAREY INTEGRATION ARC (*X-Men: Legacy*, late 2000s into early 2010s)

### Affect regulation
The Carey-era power integration — the structured incorporation of absorbed psyches into a stable, *volitional* self — is the most psychologically literate run in the character's history. It dramatizes phase-two work directly: she goes back through the absorbed identities, faces each, integrates or releases each. Affect regulation improves materially in this window because the *somatic substrate of dissociation* is being addressed. The intrusive identities are no longer ambient threats; they are sequenced material.

For the first time in the publication record, she demonstrates *tolerance of sustained intimate affect without somatic discharge into combat or flight.* The mentor scenes with younger mutants in this era show extended sequences of warmth without sabotage. This is new.

### Cognitive style
Becomes reflective for the first time in any sustained way. She narrates her interior, names her defenses, plans her growth. Not at a high theoretical level — the cognitive style remains concrete — but with a new metacognitive layer. She can now observe herself observing.

### Self-concept
Moves from negatively defined toward affirmatively defined. Where the early adult self was *not-Mystique, not-Brotherhood, not-monster,* the integration-era self begins to assert positive content: *teacher, leader, partner, equal.* The contaminated-object schema is not erased — it is reframed as a discrete piece of history rather than the totality of identity.

---

## VII. THE MARRIAGE AND KRAKOAN ADULTHOOD (mid-2010s into the present)

### Affect regulation
Mature-adult range, with residual vulnerabilities under specific triggers. The marriage to Gambit (*Mr. and Mrs. X*, 2018) provides the daily-life holding environment that her childhood withheld. Affect regulation in this period operates increasingly through *co-regulation* — the polyvagal mechanism by which a partner's nervous system stabilizes one's own. She does not need it constantly; she needs it accessibly, which is the secure-attachment criterion.

The flirtation register persists but is no longer compensatory. It has been demoted from defense to ornament. She uses it now because she enjoys it, not because she needs it.

Krakoan Quiet Council pressure produces *new* affect-regulation demands — institutional patience, tolerance of slow-grinding politics, restraint of temper in formal settings. She learns these. Her tells, when she slips, are old-pattern: thickening accent, suddenly literal idiom, the standing posture of someone who would prefer to throw a punch.

### Cognitive style
Strategic and institutional. She thinks now in terms of factions, precedents, second-order consequences. The combative-empathic reading skill from her Brotherhood youth has become political acuity. She is still not an intellectual, and she is impatient with the council's mystical registers; her contribution is operational and ethical rather than visionary. She reads people in real time better than anyone in the room and uses the read to negotiate rather than to pre-empt.

### Self-concept
Most consolidated state in the publication record, but not absolute. The working self-concept is now: *a person who has done harm, has spent her life making it right, who is loved and loves, who is responsible.* The contaminated-object schema is dormant rather than extinct — under stress (Mystique provocations; Danvers re-invocations; any threat to Gambit) it re-activates with full force and old vocabulary. Recovery to baseline is faster than in earlier decades, but the substrate is permanent. C-PTSD does not fully remit; it remodels.

---

## VIII. CROSS-DECADE INVARIANTS (what does not change)

1. **The body remains contraband.** Even with control, even married, the involuntary somatic guardedness — the half-second hesitation before brushing past someone in a hallway, the unconscious tug at a cuff or collar — never fully dissipates. Four decades of motor-habit cannot be undone by a few years of consented touch.
2. **The accent as somatic memory.** Whatever the writer, whatever the era, the Mississippi prosody returns under stress. It is the voice of the pre-mutation child, and it is what the nervous system reaches for when threatened.
3. **Approach toward harmed parties.** The defection-to-the-X-Men pattern repeats lifelong. When she has done wrong, she walks *toward* the wronged. This is rare, structurally healthy, and the single most reliable index of her core integrity.
4. **The Mystique transference.** Permanent and not fully workable. Every encounter re-opens the maternal wound. She has learned to limit damage; she has not learned to be unmoved.
5. **The Danvers ledger.** Sixty years of in-universe reparation has not closed it. The wound is structural, not narrative.

---

## IX. SUMMARY TRAJECTORY

In Herman's three phases: she spent her adolescence and early adulthood oscillating in and out of *safety;* her late twenties through forties doing *remembrance and mourning* (Gambit as primary witness; Carey as principal therapist-of-record); and her current decade in *reconnection* — to a chosen partner, to an institutional role, to a self she can describe in the affirmative. The arc is, by any clinical measure, unusually successful for the severity and chronicity of the underlying injury. The deprivation documented by Sailer et al. (2016) — the categorical loss of a reward-circuit-recruiting human input — has not been undone, because it cannot be; her adaptation has consisted of building a life rich enough at every other channel that the missing channel is bearable. This is not cure. It is the highest form of compensation available to a person with her biology, and she has achieved it through forty years of work most patients never sustain.


## Psychiatric Assessment & Differential

# PSYCHIATRIC ASSESSMENT & DIFFERENTIAL — SUBJECT: ROGUE

*Dossier Section 4 of the Intelligence Workup. Cross-reference: Sections 1 (History), 2 (Medical), 3 (Psychological). All diagnostic terminology is given in DSM-5-TR / ICD-11 analog form, with the caveat that subject's etiologic substrate (a tactile-channel mutation that has categorically denied her affective skin contact since approximately age thirteen) sits outside the population norms on which those nosologies were calibrated. Diagnoses are working formulations derived from forty years of behavioral record, not bedside interview.*

---

## 4.1 OVERVIEW — WHY THIS SUBJECT IS DIAGNOSTICALLY DIFFICULT

Subject presents the rare case in which a real, medically demonstrable sensory-channel deprivation (loss of C-tactile afferent input; see Sailer et al. 2016 and Medical §2) sits beneath a developmental trauma history dense enough to generate a complex post-traumatic picture in its own right. Most differential work in clinical practice asks: *is this trauma or is this temperament?* For Rogue the question is sharper: **is a given symptom downstream of the trauma history, downstream of the chronic neurobiological deprivation, downstream of intrusive exogenous psychic material colonizing the ego, or downstream of the pre-existing characterological substrate?** All four channels are live; they interact; and the clinical surface looks like several different disorders depending on which axis the observer privileges.

The file therefore resists a single tidy diagnosis. The formulation below assigns a primary, two solid comorbids, a structural-personality observation, and then — equally important — a series of rule-outs, because the published behavioral record contains enough false-positive surface features to mislead a less careful reader.

---

## 4.2 PRIMARY DIAGNOSIS

### Complex Post-Traumatic Stress Disorder (ICD-11 6B41)

Subject meets the full ICD-11 criterion set for C-PTSD: the three classical PTSD clusters (re-experiencing, avoidance, persistent sense of current threat) plus the three Disturbances in Self-Organization (affect dysregulation, negative self-concept, disturbances in relationships).

**Index traumas, in chronological layering.**

1. *Pre-mutation paternal household, Caldecott County.* The fact that subject ran from home as a pre-teen — before any mutant manifestation — establishes baseline developmental trauma independent of the power. Specifics are sparse in the canon by design (Claremont withheld; later writers honored the gap), but the behavioral residue is consistent with an emotionally and possibly physically unsafe paternal figure plus absent or non-protective maternal presence. This is the Type I substrate.
2. *The Cody Robbins event.* First volitional act of intimacy in subject's life produces an irreversible catastrophe (coma) in the loved object. This is a single-incident trauma with the structural features of moral injury: subject is simultaneously victim (her body betrayed her) and perpetrator (her body harmed him). Conditioned stimulus class formed at this event — *touch + intimacy + irreversibility* — has governed avoidance behavior for forty years of in-universe time.
3. *The Carol Danvers absorption.* Ideologically motivated assault in adolescence producing what subject herself later recognizes as a psychic murder. The trauma here is the *retrospective* recognition: she did the thing before she had the moral framework to know what the thing was. Survivor's-guilt structure with the additional twist that the victim's mind was for years a tenant in subject's own.
4. *Chronic re-traumatization.* Every combat use of her power that involves sustained contact replays elements of (2) and (3). The mutation has built a profession out of the trauma class.
5. *Maternal betrayals by Mystique.* Recurrent across decades; each cycle reopens the disorganized-attachment substrate.

**Symptom-by-symptom mapping to the published record.**

- **Re-experiencing.** Flashback content predominantly involves absorbed-personality intrusions rather than visual flashbacks of original events — an unusual presentation, because the trauma's *evidence* lives inside her as actual memory material from the people she absorbed. The Danvers persona's recurrent emergence (peaking *Uncanny X-Men* #269) is the clearest example: intrusion is not a memory *of* the event but the event's neurological deposit speaking in first person. Functionally indistinguishable from severe PTSD intrusion phenomena, etiologically unique.
- **Avoidance.** Categorical, lifelong, and somatic. The bodysuit and gloves are simultaneously medical countermeasure (§2) and the most thoroughgoing trauma-avoidance behavior in the file: the conditioned stimulus class (skin contact) is excluded at the sensorimotor level. Behavioral avoidance extends to: declining offers of physical comfort even through fabric in early career, sleeping arrangements that minimize accidental contact, the recurring geographic flight pattern after intimacy threatens (Antarctic departure from Gambit, *X-Men* #45; multiple "Rogue leaves the team" beats).
- **Persistent sense of current threat / hyperarousal.** Combat-readiness baseline elevated beyond team norm; sleep history (insofar as canon shows it) suggests light, alert sleeper; startle response to unexpected touch is documented across writers as a near-reflex flinch even when the toucher is gloved and known.
- **Affect dysregulation.** Discussed at length in §3. The hot-temper / brittle-surface presentation is the visible end. The deeper tell is the *binary quality* of her affective range under stress — full sass-armor on or full collapse — with little middle band. Modulation improves markedly post-Carey integration arc, consistent with the trauma-informed observation that affect regulation is the last C-PTSD cluster to remit.
- **Negative self-concept.** The substrate self-image is *contaminated object* (§3). Operationalized in repeated statements across decades to the effect that she "ruins" what she loves, that she is "poison," that she shouldn't be touched, shouldn't be loved. This is not transient depressive cognition; it is the stable working model.
- **Disturbances in relationships.** Approach-sabotage-retreat-return cycle (§3, §5). Durable bonds exist but are organized around figures who tolerate or match her concealment (Gambit) or who hold without demanding intimate access (Storm).

**Course.** Onset in adolescence, chronic, with partial remission across the Carey integration arc and the Krakoan-era marriage. Symptom severity tracks proximity to the index trauma class: stable when role is operational/command, exacerbates when intimacy or maternal-figure (Mystique) material is activated. No evidence of full remission; substantial functional recovery is the realistic ceiling.

---

## 4.3 COMORBID DIAGNOSES

### 4.3.1 Other Specified Dissociative Disorder (DSM-5-TR 300.15) — sub-threshold for Dissociative Identity Disorder

Subject demonstrates recurrent intrusion of distinct identity states (Danvers prominently; Magneto post-*X-Men* #25; Gambit's content post-*X-Men* #41; lesser figures across decades) with associated alterations in affect, behavior, memory, and sometimes superhuman power expression. Surface presentation resembles DID. The differential is decisive on two grounds:

- *Etiology is exogenous.* In DID, alters are dissociated self-states formed under unbearable childhood affect. Subject's intrusive identities are *imports* — they were once other living minds, transferred via the mutation. Phenomenologically similar; ontologically different.
- *Resolution is technologically tractable.* External psychic intervention (Xavier, Magneto, Psylocke-tier telepaths) reliably suppresses or excises the imports. DID alters do not respond to telepathic excision because they are endogenous structures of the host's own mind.

Nonetheless, the diagnosis is not merely incidental: her ego's *capacity to be displaced* by these imports points to a pre-existing dissociative vulnerability, almost certainly trauma-derived from the pre-mutation period. A patient with robust ego integration would more likely experience absorbed material as foreign content (ego-dystonic memory) rather than as a competing first-person agent. The fact that the Danvers material *spoke as Carol* rather than *was remembered by Anna* is the diagnostic finding. Sub-threshold for DID proper; squarely within OSDD-1b territory; with the etiologic asterisk noted above.

Derealization episodes under acute stress are also documented across the record (the post-Antarctic period; the post-Magneto-absorption recovery in "Fatal Attractions"). Consistent with the broader dissociative-spectrum picture.

### 4.3.2 Persistent Depressive Disorder (DSM-5-TR 300.4) with intermittent Major Depressive Episodes

The anhedonic baseline is, in subject's case, **medically necessary rather than psychiatrically idiopathic.** Sailer et al. (2016) establish that pleasant affective touch is a reward-circuit input recruiting orbitofrontal cortex and putamen and sustaining social bond maintenance. Subject has been categorically denied this input since adolescence. The expected sequela in any organism is chronic mild-to-moderate anhedonia with elevated vulnerability to depressive episodes under stressor load. The file confirms exactly this:

- *Dysthymic baseline.* Even in operationally good periods, the published affective register has a floor that other team members do not have — a melancholy substrate audible beneath the flirtation. This is the C-tactile deprivation expressing itself at the level of mood.
- *Documented major episodes.* Around the Cody comatose state (early flashback material); post-Danvers integration recovery (*Uncanny X-Men* #150-158 era); post-Antarctic loss of Gambit (mid-90s); during the Mystique betrayal cycles; intermittent Krakoan-era episodes around Quiet Council moral burdens.
- *The Siege Perilous decision (*Uncanny X-Men* #247).* Volitional ego-erasure under intolerable affect. Not suicide in the strict sense — she chose remaking, not non-existence — but functionally a suicidal-equivalent act and the most severe documented episode. The fact that subject was offered, and took, the option of *being someone else* is diagnostically revealing: the unbearable thing was being *her.*

The depressive picture is therefore best formulated as a chronic dysthymic floor (etiology partially neurobiological, partially trauma-derived) with episodic major depressive exacerbations precipitated by intimacy-related loss or maternal-figure betrayal. SSRIs in a real-world analog patient would address only the trauma/affective end; the deprivation channel cannot be pharmacologically substituted.

### 4.3.3 Specific Phobia features — touch-related (sub-syndromal)

Strictly speaking, the avoidance of skin contact is rational given consequences and therefore does not meet phobia criteria (the fear is proportionate to actual risk). However, the *generalization* of the avoidance — flinch responses even when the toucher is gloved and the contact is safe; difficulty accepting touch through fabric from trusted parties even when she retains volitional control; the post-control-acquisition lag in which she still hesitated to touch Gambit barehanded — exceeds what the realistic-risk model alone would predict. The over-generalization is the trauma residue, and it presents as a phobic-spectrum feature embedded within the C-PTSD picture.

---

## 4.4 PERSONALITY ORGANIZATION

### Borderline level (Kernberg structural sense) — **without** meeting Borderline Personality Disorder categorical criteria

Subject's structural organization shows the three Kernbergian markers of borderline-level functioning: **identity diffusion** (the self-as-contaminated-object substrate; the chronic uncertainty about which mental contents are "hers"); **primitive defenses** under load (splitting, projective identification, especially in Mystique transactions; dissociation as discussed); and **reality testing preserved** (no psychotic-spectrum features; reality contact stable even during absorbed-identity intrusions, which she recognizes as not-self even when she cannot suppress them).

This is structural, not categorical. Subject does **not** meet DSM-5-TR Borderline Personality Disorder criteria because:

- Her core attachments are *durable across decades*, not characterized by the BPD signature of frantic idealization-devaluation oscillation. The Gambit bond, the Storm sisterhood, the team affiliation — these persist through ruptures.
- She does not show the BPD impulsivity pattern in self-damaging domains: no substance abuse, no spending sprees, no eating-disorder features, no promiscuity (the latter foreclosed by the power but also temperamentally absent — see §2 on the body she cannot trust).
- Her chronic emptiness has a *namable external cause* (the touch deprivation). BPD-defining emptiness is characteristically diffuse and unattributable; subject's is precisely located.
- Suicidality/self-harm is not a recurrent behavioral pattern. The Siege Perilous episode is a single severe event under extreme load, not a chronic gesture.
- Identity disturbance, while present, is *content-specific* (around absorbed material and contamination) rather than the diffuse BPD picture of unstable goals, values, and self-image.

The cleanest formulation: **borderline-level structural organization is the substrate; C-PTSD is the diagnostic surface; the categorical PD diagnosis is not earned.**

---

## 4.5 DIFFERENTIAL — WHAT SUBJECT IS NOT, AND WHY

A careful differential matters because subject's surface presentation contains several features that would mislead a clinician anchored to single-axis impressions. The following rule-outs are each substantive.

### 4.5.1 Not Antisocial Personality Disorder, despite Brotherhood-era criminal behavior

The adolescent record (Brotherhood membership, Danvers assault, miscellaneous antagonist work) is genuine antisocial *behavior.* It is not antisocial *personality.* The differentiating findings:

- **Guilt is hyperactive, not absent.** ASPD is defined by the absence or shallowness of remorse. Subject's reparation drive — forty years of pro-social labor explicitly motivated by guilt over the Danvers act — is the precise inverse phenotype.
- **Empathy is intact and intense.** ASPD shows callous-unemotional traits; subject shows the opposite — her capacity to feel into other minds was literalized by the mutation and never blunted.
- **The criminal behavior was developmentally contextualized** (identification with the foster-mother aggressor; pre-frontal incomplete; no autonomous adult criminal pattern after defection).
- **Reparation is durable and behaviorally costly.** She runs *toward* the parties she wronged, accepts hostility, takes physical risk for them. This is the diagnostic opposite of ASPD's exploitation-and-flee pattern.

### 4.5.2 Not Narcissistic Personality Disorder, despite the flirtatious self-presentation

The Southern-belle register, the cultivated charm, the awareness of her own desirability — all could be misread as narcissistic surface. The rule-out is clean:

- **The grandiose self is absent.** Substrate self-image is *contaminated object,* the antipode of NPD's grandiose self-structure.
- **Empathy is not impaired** (see 4.5.1).
- **Need for admiration is not the organizing motive.** The flirtation is a reaction-formation against intimacy starvation, not a supply-seeking strategy. When admiration is offered, she deflects rather than absorbs it.
- **Entitlement is not the affective tone.** Her affective tone toward the world is *indebtedness* — the inverse.

### 4.5.3 Not Schizoid Personality Disorder, despite the lifelong solitariness

A surface reading might note: limited intimate relationships, periods of withdrawal, restricted physical contact, frequent solo operation. The rule-out:

- **She wants connection desperately.** SchPD is defined by absence of desire for close relationships; subject's entire affective economy is organized around the unmet desire. The solitariness is *barred,* not preferred.
- **Affect is not constricted.** Subject's affective range — anger, flirtation, grief, loyalty, joy in combat — is broad and expressive. SchPD shows flat or constricted affect.
- **Pleasure capacity is intact** for non-tactile rewards. She enjoys flight, combat, friendship-banter, mentorship. The anhedonia is channel-specific.

### 4.5.4 Not Bipolar Disorder, despite mood lability

The mood swings under stress could prompt a bipolar workup. The rule-out:

- **No autonomous manic or hypomanic episodes** in the record. Elevated states track external excitement (combat, reunion with Gambit) and resolve appropriately.
- **No characteristic bipolar markers** — no decreased need for sleep without consequence, no pressured speech as an episode rather than a temperamental baseline, no goal-directed grandiosity, no flight of ideas.
- **Mood reactivity is *trigger-locked,*** consistent with C-PTSD affect dysregulation rather than mood-disorder cyclicity.

### 4.5.5 Not Dissociative Identity Disorder proper

Discussed in 4.3.1. The phenomenology resembles; the etiology and treatment-response diverge; the core self persists as a stable agent recognizable to herself and others across decades. OSDD-1b is the correct frame.

### 4.5.6 Not a Primary Psychotic Disorder

Absorbed-identity intrusions, hearing other voices internally, the Magneto-induced post-absorption episodes — all could be misread psychotically. The rule-out:

- **Reality testing is preserved.** Subject recognizes intrusive material as intrusive even when she cannot suppress it. She knows the Danvers voice is not the world.
- **No formal thought disorder.** Speech is goal-directed and organized; no derailment, neologisms, or thought-blocking outside acute absorption events.
- **No negative symptoms.** Affective and motivational systems are robust.
- **Etiology is mechanically explicable** by the mutation; the phenomena resolve with telepathic intervention.

### 4.5.7 Not a Substance Use Disorder

The absence is itself a personality datum (§2). Given foster-parent modeling, given Gambit's louche tendencies, given the obvious self-medication incentive presented by chronic dysthymia and touch deprivation — *the abstention is significant.* The most parsimonious explanation: subject already inhabits a body she cannot trust; she will not introduce additional uncontrolled agents into the perimeter. A trauma-coherent abstention, not a temperamental one.

### 4.5.8 Not Autism Spectrum (sensory profile distractor)

The sensory-defensive presentation around touch could superficially suggest sensory-processing features on the autism spectrum. The rule-out is immediate: her sensory defensiveness is *channel-specific and traumatically conditioned,* not pervasive; her social cognition is hyper-developed rather than impaired (she reads people exceptionally fast, partly trained, partly the mutation's literal effect); no restricted/repetitive behavior pattern; no developmental-language history suggesting ASD.

### 4.5.9 Not Adjustment Disorder

The duration, severity, and structural integration of symptoms into personality far exceed the adjustment-disorder frame. The trauma is not an event she is adjusting to; it is a chronic condition she has organized a life around.

---

## 4.6 COURSE OVER TIME

**Adolescence (pre- and early post-mutation).** Identification with the aggressor; Brotherhood phase; the index acts. Symptoms maximally externalized as antisocial behavior.

**Early X-Men years (Claremont era).** Acute presentation; absorbed-personality intrusions dominant; affective dysregulation high; the Siege Perilous decision marks the period's nadir. Sustained exposure to a chosen family begins corrective experience.

**1990s.** Symptomatic equilibrium punctuated by acute disruptions (Magneto absorption; Gambit revelations and Antarctic abandonment). The Gambit courtship is the period's central therapeutic event — a sustained relationship with someone who matches her concealment and tolerates the approach-retreat cycle. No remission; functional stability.

**2000s — Carey-era integration arc (*X-Men: Legacy*).** First sustained intervention that addresses the power and the psyche together. Acquisition of volitional control over absorption is metaphorically and literally an ego-integration event. Substantial reduction in dissociative-spectrum symptoms; negative self-concept partially revised; affect regulation improves measurably.

**2010s into Krakoan era.** Post-integration adult functioning. Marriage to Gambit (*Mr. and Mrs. X*, 2018) — consummation of the central drive, achievable only after the control acquisition. Quiet Council seat — assumption of containing-authority role, the position she most needed to receive in childhood, now offered to others. The C-PTSD core has not remitted but is well-managed; the depressive substrate persists at lower amplitude; the dissociative phenomena are largely historical absent fresh major absorptions.

**Prognostic statement.** Subject has achieved roughly the realistic ceiling of recovery for her trauma load and her unique neurobiological situation. The wound is permanent; the adaptation is, by clinical measure, unusually successful. Decompensation risk remains concentrated at the named pressure points (§5): Mystique transactions, Danvers-callbacks, threats to Gambit, fresh major absorptions, and any sustained period that re-activates the contamination self-concept. Maintenance of the current institutional role, the marital structure, and the chosen-family network is protective.

---

## 4.7 SUMMARY FORMULATION

A chronic complex post-traumatic stress disorder, layered on a borderline-level personality organization that does not reach categorical Personality Disorder diagnosis, comorbid with sub-threshold dissociative disorder of unique exogenous etiology and a persistent depressive disorder whose anhedonic floor is partly neurobiologically obligate (Sailer et al. 2016) rather than psychiatrically primary. The presentation is overdetermined by four developmental traumas (paternal household, Cody event, Danvers absorption, chronic combat-touch re-exposure) and one chronic neurobiological deprivation (loss of affective-touch input). The structural defenses are unusually elegant because the body itself enacts the avoidance, and unusually punishing for the same reason: the medical necessity prevents the defense from ever being relinquished without endangering others.

The clinical surface across forty years of record has shifted from acute and externalized in adolescence, through symptomatic equilibrium with episodic crisis in adulthood, to substantially integrated adult functioning in the current era. The wound is real; the diagnosis is real; the person built on top of both is, by any honest measure, a successful adaptation to an extraordinarily difficult


## Behavioral Atlas

# BEHAVIORAL ATLAS — SUBJECT: ROGUE

*Surveillance-grade catalog of observable tells, micro-patterns, and decision habits across the full state-space of conditions documented across four decades of canon. Each entry is anchored in behavior, not speculation; where a tell has a likely substrate, the substrate is named.*

---

## I. BASELINE — CALM / UNREMARKABLE OPERATIONS

**Postural signature.** Stands with weight on the back foot, lead foot slightly turned out — a fighter's stance held loosely, even at rest. Hands rarely at full hang; one or both occupied (hip, hair, glove cuff, coffee mug, the back of a chair). The hand-occupation is *standing protocol*: hands that are doing something cannot accidentally land on another person's skin.

**Hand discipline.** Even gloved, she does not casually touch others. No shoulder-pats, no arm-squeezes, no playful shoves during easy banter. Where teammates routinely physicalize affection, she substitutes verbal warmth: terms of endearment ("sugah," "darlin'," "honey") deployed at the cadence and frequency where another person would touch. *The endearments are her hands.* Count them per conversation; the rate is diagnostic.

**Gaze.** Direct, level, often slightly lifted (a chin-up tell inherited from Mystique's posture training). She *reads* faces — sustained gaze on the mouth and brows of whoever is speaking — and does this even with people she trusts. The reading was first survival, then habit, then craft. She maintains it on the Quiet Council, where it functions as a tactical asset.

**Voice and accent.** The drawl is real but volumetrically modulated. Calm baseline: medium-low pitch, slow cadence, vowels long, consonants soft. The accent thickens under three conditions — flirtation, fury, and grief — and thins (approaches neutral General American) under sustained tactical or administrative speech. The thickening is partly automatic, partly performative; observers should treat sudden vowel-broadening as an *affect signal*, not a regional one.

**Clothing discipline.** Full coverage is a medical standing order, not a wardrobe choice. Even in periods of canonical power-control, the long sleeves and gloves persist — the prosthetic has become identity. She checks her cuffs unconsciously, the way a smoker pats for a lighter: a glove-tug or sleeve-pull every few minutes, regardless of need. Catalog this as her single most reliable self-soothing micro-gesture.

**Spatial habits.** Sits with her back to walls, never to doors. Leaves at least one body-width of clear space between herself and the nearest seated other. In a crowded room she will orbit the perimeter rather than cross the middle. In elevators she takes the corner. None of this is hypervigilant in the PTSD-jumpy register; it is a *machined* spatial discipline, executed without visible anxiety, because she has practiced it since adolescence.

**Routine micro-rituals.** Coffee, black, mornings. Long showers — the only environment in which she is reliably skin-exposed and reliably safe, and the only one she lingers in. Hair: brushed and arranged, but always with the white forelock visible — she does not hide it; the streak is *signature* and she treats it as such. Sleeps gloved unless alone in a sealed room. Boots laced, not zipped — she will not be caught in slip-ons.

**Conversational defaults.** Opens with humor — wry, slightly self-deprecating, Southern in idiom. Listens more than she talks in mixed company; talks more than she listens with intimates. Will deflect personal questions with a charm-volley ("Why, sugah, you tryin' to read my diary?") before answering, if she answers at all. The deflection is so practiced it reads as ease.

---

## II. UNDER LOW-GRADE STRESS (admin, social friction, low-tactical)

**Glove behavior intensifies.** The cuff-tug rate roughly doubles. She will also begin to *roll* the cuff between thumb and forefinger — a quieter, more inward version of the same self-touch.

**Verbal output rises.** More endearments per minute. More throwaway humor. The Southern register thickens audibly. She *fills the room* — partly to control its emotional weather, partly because silence in low-stress social settings is the condition in which her mind drifts to absent or absorbed others.

**Spatial drift.** Will quietly increase her distance from the stressor — half-step back, lean against a doorframe, find a reason to refill a drink. Catalog these as *micro-exits*; she is rehearsing the larger exit she may not yet have decided to take.

**Decision habit.** Under low stress she defers consequential decisions to morning. She has said versions of "I'll sleep on it" across multiple canonical runs. The deferral is not avoidance — it is policy, learned the hard way from impulse-decisions in adolescence.

---

## III. UNDER ACUTE STRESS / TACTICAL THREAT

**Postural shift.** Weight forward, chin drops a quarter-inch, hands come *out* of pockets and glove-cuffs and into a loose ready-position at the hipline. The earlier fighter's-stance-at-rest tightens into actual fighter's stance.

**Voice drops; cadence speeds.** The drawl narrows but does not vanish. Sentences shorten. Endearments evaporate first — when she stops calling people "sugah" mid-fight, the threat assessment has crossed her internal threshold from manageable to serious.

**Aggression vector.** She closes distance. Despite a power-set that historically included flight and ranged invulnerability, her instinct under threat is to *get in physical reach* — partly Danvers-era muscle memory, partly the older logic that her own body is the deadliest weapon in the room. She will lead with a punch before she leads with absorption; absorption is reserved for targets she has *decided* warrant carrying for days afterward.

**The glove-removal tell.** When she peels a glove mid-conflict, the engagement has escalated to *lethal-or-near.* This is her nuclear option and she knows it. The peel is slow when it is a threat-display (intended to make an enemy stand down); fast and one-handed when she has committed to contact. Both versions are diagnostic; the difference matters.

**Verbal flirt-aggression hybrid.** Under acute stress she taunts. The taunts are flirtatious in form — "Come on, sugah, ah ain't even warm yet" — and contemptuous in content. This is the documented stress-pattern: *the two surface defenses (flirtation, aggression) spike together.* It is unsettling to opponents, which is the point, and it is also a regulator — talking through a fight keeps her ego forward and the absorbed psyches back.

**Risk preference.** Markedly elevated. She will take a hit to land one. She will absorb a hostile to neutralize them while accepting the psychic blowback. The risk-acceptance is not bravado; it is a *settled tariff* — she long ago priced her own suffering at a discount relative to teammate safety. Operationally treat her as someone who will trade self-harm for mission progress at a rate higher than any other X-Man except Wolverine, and for different reasons (his is repair-rate-driven; hers is reparation-driven).

---

## IV. UNDER EXISTENTIAL / OVERWHELM STRESS

**Withdrawal precedes departure.** Before she leaves a team or a relationship, there is a documented quiet period — days to weeks of reduced verbal output, fewer endearments, longer solo intervals (the perimeter walks, the long flights alone). Surveillance value is high: the quiet is the leading indicator, the leaving is the lagging one.

**Geographic flight.** When overwhelm crosses threshold she *moves.* Caldecott, the Australian Outback exile, the Antarctic disappearance, Muir Island stretches, repeated solo road-trips through the American South. Pattern: she flees *toward landscape*, not toward cities. Rural, low-population, weather-exposed terrain. The childhood Mississippi swamp set the template; she goes back to environmental conditions that match her interior.

**Ego-erasure as terminal option.** Under the worst documented load (the Siege Perilous decision, *Uncanny X-Men* #247) she chose volitional self-erasure over continued endurance. This is not suicidality in the gestures-and-attempts register; it is a colder, structural willingness to delete the self if the self becomes intolerable. Catalog as her ceiling-level decompensation behavior. It has been reached once on record; the conditions that produced it (absorbed-psyche overload + isolation + perceived failure of her primary attachments) define the watch-list.

**Dissociative slippage.** Under absorbed-psyche overload she begins to use the donor's verbal mannerisms before she loses her own. With the Danvers psyche, observers reported her saying "Carol" in third person about herself, then drifting into Danvers's vocabulary and posture. The slippage is *gradual and detectable* — a 24-to-72-hour window in which intervention is possible before the displacement completes. Catalog the linguistic markers per known absorption.

---

## V. INTIMACY (approach, threshold, sabotage)

**Approach behavior.** When she is interested, she *circles.* Increased proximity without contact, increased eye-contact duration, the accent thickens, the endearments specialize (general "sugah" → specific "Remy," "darlin' man," personalized verbal touch). She will find reasons to be in the same room without an explicit reason to talk. She is not coy in the avoidant sense; she is *patient* in the obstructed sense.

**The fabric-mediated substitute.** Her affection language is touch-through-barrier: a gloved hand on a sleeved forearm, her cheek against a jacketed shoulder, dancing in long sleeves, sleeping pressed against a clothed back. These near-touches are not poor substitutes she tolerates; they are *highly ritualized*, slow, attended-to, treated by her as the real currency. Observers should recognize that for her, fabric-mediated contact is not a workaround — it is the developed channel. The longing for skin is separate and ungovernable; the fabric channel is what she has built a love life on.

**Threshold sabotage.** When intimacy approaches consummation — by her standards, not the partner's — she does one of three things in documented sequence:
1. *Escalates the verbal flirt to the point of unseriousness* (kicks the moment back into banter);
2. *Manufactures a tactical reason to leave the room* (mission, teammate in trouble, "Ah forgot…");
3. *If neither works, removes a glove and lets the consequence end the moment.*
The third is the most revealing: she would rather inflict the harm and confirm her contaminated-object self-image than risk the unknown of actually being held.

**Post-intimacy pattern.** After any intimate breakthrough (the Carey-era control periods, the *Mr. and Mrs. X* marriage) she is *more* domestically present and *less* combat-eager for a documented interval. She nests. She cooks. She wears slightly less coverage in private. This is the only condition under which the standing wardrobe protocol relaxes, and the relaxation is the most reliable index of her interior safety.

**Sexual register.** Flirtation is constant and stylized; consummated sexuality is rare and, when present, treated with the gravity of a sacrament rather than a recreation. She does not have casual partners on record. The power foreclosed the possibility long enough that it is also now a temperamental fact.

---

## VI. GRIEF

**Cries rarely. Cries hydraulically when she does.** The Antarctic loss of Gambit, the post-Danvers integration, the Mystique betrayals — the crying when it arrives is *pressure release*, not expression. Face wet, body still, sound minimal. She does not seek comfort during it. She does not want to be held *during* grief; she wants to be held *after*, and even then through fabric.

**Verbal shutdown.** Endearments cease. Drawl thickens (the only condition where grief and intimacy share the vowel-broadening tell). Sentences shorten to the point of monosyllables. She will answer direct questions truthfully and briefly and will not volunteer.

**Physical work.** She *labors* through grief — repairs, training, patrols, the boring institutional work of whatever team she is on. The labor is not avoidance; it is the documented method by which she metabolizes affect. Surveillance value: grief is the condition under which her productivity *rises*.

**Ritual visits.** She returns to physical sites associated with the lost — graves, last-seen locations, the bayou. The visits are quiet, often alone, often gloved-and-cuffed in full daylight. She does not perform mourning for an audience.

**Refusal of substances.** Other characters drink through grief; she does not. The body-as-untrusted-perimeter logic extends to grief management. Catalog the abstention as a *characterological constant*, not a phase.

---

## VII. VICTORY

**Understated.** She does not celebrate large. A nod, a half-smile, an arm around a teammate's *shoulders* (gloved hand, jacketed shoulder, brief). She will buy a round but rarely drink it. She receives praise with deflection — "Wasn't just me, sugah" — and redirects credit reflexively. The deflection is not false modesty; it is the same reparation-logic engine running in success conditions: *I do not get to take the win cleanly.*

**Brief affective opening.** In the immediate aftermath of victory she is sometimes verbally tender in ways she is not otherwise — quick sincere thanks, named-out gratitude to specific teammates. The window closes within hours. Catalog as the *only condition besides post-intimacy nesting* in which her surface defenses thin voluntarily.

**Decision habit post-victory.** She tends to immediately propose the *next* task. The pause-and-savor is uncomfortable; the forward motion is reflex.

---

## VIII. DEFEAT

**Self-blame default.** Whatever the actual causal chain, she will internalize the failure first and apportion external responsibility second, if at all. This is reliable to the point of being exploitable: an adversary or manipulator who frames a setback as *her* fault will get traction faster than with any other Council-tier figure.

**Anger turned inward, then outward in training.** She does not lash out at teammates after defeat; she lashes out at equipment. The Danger Room or its equivalent will see extended, unscheduled, physically punishing sessions in the 24–72 hours after a loss. Catalog the after-action training-room logs as a depression/defeat barometer.

**Withdrawal of the verbal warmth.** Endearments drop. Doors close (literally — she retreats to private quarters earlier than baseline). She does not want to be checked on, and she will say so directly if approached; the ones who get past the closed door are a very short list (Storm, Gambit, occasionally Kitty).

**Decision habit post-defeat.** Avoids consequential decisions for longer than her baseline 24-hour rule. She knows she becomes self-punitively conservative — or, less often, recklessly compensatory — after losses, and she has learned to wait the worst of it out. This is *acquired* self-knowledge, not native; the early-career record shows worse impulse-control after losses.

---

## IX. AUTHORITY AND HIERARCHY

**Toward authority she trusts.** Loyal, executes cleanly, will push back privately but support publicly. Storm is the template; the Storm-relationship is the model for how she behaves with any authority that has *held*.

**Toward authority she distrusts.** Compliance with a visible reservation. Slight lag on orders. Verbal acknowledgment without the warmth-markers. She does not openly defy; she *audits*. The audit is detectable to anyone reading her closely (Mystique reads it instantly; others miss it).

**Toward charismatic authoritarians.** Documented pull — Mystique, Magneto, occasionally Xavier in his more imperial modes. The pull is the containing-object hunger from childhood. She knows this about herself by the modern era and *resists it as policy*, which means she is more guarded with charismatic figures than with bureaucratic ones. Catalog this as a deliberate counter-bias.

**As authority herself.** Quiet Council era — she runs structured, fair, decisive. Does not enjoy the role but does not flinch from it. Delegates well. Holds grudges institutionally, not personally (will keep an untrusted figure off a mission without poisoning the room about them). Her authority register drops the drawl and the endearments almost entirely — the Southern-charm surface is for peers and intimates; in command she is plain-spoken and short.

---

## X. AROUND CHILDREN AND JUNIORS

**Markedly different register.** With younger mutants she is *physically present in ways she is not with adults* — sits closer, kneels to their height, allows them to lean on her gloved/jacketed body. With children she does not deflect personal questions; she answers them. The mentorship dyad is the condition in which the contaminated-object self-image relaxes most reliably, because the asymmetry of the relationship means she is the giver, not the receiver, of the affection she could not safely receive at their age.

**Teaching style.** Patient, concrete, lots of demonstration. Will repeat instructions without irritation. Does not shame mistakes. Catalog the tonal contrast with her peer interactions; it is the most direct evidence of what her own ideal caregiver would have looked like.

---

## XI. AROUND MYSTIQUE

**Behavioral discontinuity.** Mystique's presence collapses adult Rogue toward adolescent Rogue within minutes. Voice tightens; the drawl can either thicken (regression) or thin (defensive distancing); spatial discipline degrades — she will allow Mystique closer than she allows anyone else, including Gambit, despite (because of) the betrayal history. The maternal transference is permanent.

**Decision degradation.** Decisions made in Mystique's immediate orbit are less reliable than her decisions made anywhere else. She knows this. The knowing does not fix it. Catalog Mystique-proximate decisions with a discount factor.

**Recovery pattern.** Post-Mystique-encounter she requires 24–72 hours of solo time to reset. Behavior during the reset matches the post-defeat profile: training-room punishment, verbal warmth withdrawal, closed doors. The cycle has run dozens of times on record and will run again.

---

## XII. AROUND GAMBIT

**Stabilized baseline.** With Gambit present, her resting micro-gestures relax. The cuff-tugging slows. The spatial buffer to him is smaller than her buffer to anyone else. She *leans* on him through fabric in ways she does not lean on anyone else. The endearments specialize and soften.

**Conflict pattern.** Their fights are loud, fast, drawl-thick, and short. Neither holds grudges of the freezing-out kind; the conflicts resolve with banter and physical proximity rather than apology. This is the healthiest dyadic conflict pattern in her record.

**Threat to Gambit.** Triggers her most disinhibited combat behavior. The risk-tariff drops to near zero; she will accept any injury, absorb any opponent, take any tactical risk. Catalog as the single most operationally significant pressure point in her current life.

---

## XIII. SLEEP, SOLITUDE, AND THE PRIVATE REGISTER

**Sleep.** Gloved baseline. Sleeps lightly; wakes fully and quickly, not groggily. Documented insomnia stretches after major absorptions and after Mystique encounters.

**Solitude.** She is one of the rare X-Men who is *fluent* in solitude — she has been forced into it her whole life and has built capacity in it. Solo flights, long drives, perimeter walks. In solitude the surface defenses drop entirely; observers (the few who have seen her unguarded — Gambit, occasionally Storm) report a quieter, sadder, more deliberate person than the public-facing one.

**Music.** Country, blues, occasional gospel. The musical taste is one of the few Caldecott artifacts she has not renounced. She hums when alone; she does not hum in company.

**Reading.** Practical — manuals, tactical briefings, occasional fiction (Southern writers; she has been seen with O'Connor and McCullers in the record). Not a heavy reader by Council standards but consistent.

---

## XIV. THE DEEP TELLS — RANKED BY DIAGNOSTIC VALUE

1. **Endearment rate per minute.** Her single most reliable affect-meter. High = baseline-to-low-stress engagement. Dropping = stress crossing into serious. Absent = grief, defeat, or tactical commitment.
2. **Glove cuff-tug frequency.** Self-soothing baseline; doubles under low stress; ceases under acute threat (hands are needed).
3. **Drawl thickness.** Thickens under flirtation, fury, and grief; thins under command and tactical speech. Sudden thickening is an *affect alarm*.
4. **Spatial buffer to nearest body.** Stable at one body-width; contraction toward Gambit is normal; contraction toward anyone else is a flag; contraction toward Mystique is a different flag entirely.
5. **Glove removal.** Nuclear. Slow peel = threat display. Fast peel = committed contact. Either is a state-change.
6. **Wardrobe relaxation in private.** The single most reliable index of interior safety. Long sleeves down in domestic settings = trust state achieved.
7. **Post-event training-room hours.** Defeat barometer; correlates with depressive load.
8. **Use of a donor's vocabulary about herself.** Leading indicator of dissociative slippage; 24–72 hour intervention window.
9. **Geographic flight prep.** Quiet period precedes departure by days-to-weeks. The quiet is the warning.
10. **Mystique-proximate decision-making.** Reliably degraded. Apply discount.

---

*The Atlas is not closed. The subject has demonstrated, across forty years of in-universe time, a capacity for revision that few other long-running figures match. Tells listed above are stable across the period of record but should be re-baselined after any major life event — particularly any further development in the Gambit marriage, any further Mystique reconciliation or rupture, and any future change in the power-control status that has, more than any other variable, defined the architecture of her behavior.*


## Daily Life, Routines & Rituals

# DAILY LIFE, ROUTINES & RITUALS — SUBJECT: ROGUE

*What a week of continuous observation would record. Granular, longitudinal; cross-referenced against the Claremont-through-Duggan publication record and the medical substrate established in §2.*

---

## I. THE ARCHITECTURE OF A DAY

Subject lives on what surveillance would quickly recognize as a **two-shell day**: an outer shell of high-functioning team operations (training, council work, missions, mentorship), and an inner shell of compulsive private rituals organized around the body she cannot let touch anyone. The two shells do not interpenetrate. People who have worked alongside her for years (Storm, Logan) know the outer shell intimately and the inner shell only by inference. Gambit is the only person admitted, partially, to both.

### Wake

Subject wakes early — consistently between 05:40 and 06:20 local, regardless of time zone, regardless of bedtime. This is not discipline; it is hypervigilance. The C-PTSD substrate (§4) runs a low-grade arousal floor that breaks shallow sleep before dawn. Surveillance over a week would catch: eyes open, body still for thirty to ninety seconds, no stretching, no reach for the partner — a learned freeze in which she inventories her own skin before moving. She sleeps in long sleeves and gloves (cotton in summer, jersey in winter; she keeps a stack folded by the bed). The gloves go on *before* she sits up. This is the first ritual of the day and the most diagnostic one: she will not be barefoot-handed in a room with another sleeping person, ever.

If Gambit is present, she watches him sleep for a beat — a small, repeated tenderness logged in domestic-era issues — then rolls away from him to dress. She does not kiss him awake. She has, in twenty years of in-universe cohabitation, never once kissed him awake without preparation.

### Morning grooming

Bathroom routine is **long and physical**. Hot shower (she runs water hotter than most; the heat is one of the few somatic inputs that registers strongly through skin that is otherwise a danger-channel). She washes her own hair — never lets a stylist do it — and the hair-touching is one of her two reliable self-soothing behaviors (the other is rubbing her gloved thumb along her gloved index finger, a tic). Out of the shower she dresses *fully* before opening the bathroom door, even in a private suite. No towel-walks. No padding to the closet half-dressed. The bathroom is a sealed re-armoring chamber.

The dressing sequence is invariant: underclothes, leggings or trouser-base, top layer, *gloves last after one final hand-wash*.
