The love-signal is operational: she will absorb a hostile mutant to spare a teammate, she will fly into a position no one else can survive, she will stay up with a younger X-Man having a bad night. With Gambit specifically, love is signaled by *continued teasing under conditions that would warrant tenderness* — the courtly form is preserved precisely because dropping it would feel, to her, like admitting the relationship is fragile.

Second channel: the *withheld touch* itself becomes a vocabulary. The pause before she does not put a hand on a friend, the deliberate fabric-mediated contact when she does, the way she will lean into Gambit's shoulder through cloth — these are her love-vocabulary's punctuation marks. Watch for the lean; the lean is "I love you."

Third channel: *naming.* When she upgrades a pet name ("Remy" to "Remy-honey," "Kitty" to "Kitty-pryde"), the upgrade is the message.

## 6. How She Communicates Threat

Inverse function: as threat-level rises, *sweetness rises with it.* The voice gets warmer, slower, more drawled, more "sugah"-saturated. By the time she is calling a hostile civilian "darlin'" with a slow smile, the next sentence is a removed glove or its equivalent. The Southern-coded warm-threat is one of her most reliable behavioral signatures and is well-documented across decades.

Direct threats, when issued, are short and concrete and reference the body ("Ah will put you through that wall"). She does not threaten abstractly. She does not threaten via her power — she will *use* the power as threat by removing a glove or reaching, but she rarely verbalizes the absorption capacity. The unspoken-ness is itself menace.

Threat-warning to allies (when she is about to do something dangerous on their behalf): she goes briefly tender, may use a peer's full name, may make a small joke. This is her version of a goodbye.

## 7. How She Communicates Grief

She does not. Or rather: she communicates grief through *absence of communication.* Post-loss the drawl thins, the pet names drop out, the sentences shorten to functional minimums. She becomes operational. The published record shows this after the Antarctic separation from Gambit, after the early absorbed-personality crises, after each Mystique betrayal. Verbal mourning is foreclosed; the body and the silence carry the load.

When grief does surface verbally it tends to come out *sideways* — as anger at a third party, as a cutting joke at her own expense, as a rare and abrupt self-disclosure to whichever peer has caught her at the wrong moment. The disclosure, when it comes, is uncharacteristically plain — drawl reduced, vocabulary unornamented, often a single declarative sentence she does not elaborate. Then she walks away.

Crying in language: she will narrate around tears rather than through them. The tell is a sentence she starts and does not finish, followed by a turn of the head.

## 8. Deflection Repertoire

- **The pet-name pivot.** Any question that approaches the touch-deprivation, the Danvers act, or the Cody event is met with a "sugah, you don't want to go there" or equivalent, delivered warmly. The warmth is the deflection.
- **The Southern joke.** Self-deprecating, often body-referencing in the safe register (height, hair, accent — never skin). Redirects intimacy-approaches into shared laughter.
- **The operational redirect.** "We got bigger problems, sugah." Used to convert affective topics into tactical ones; highly effective in field settings, conspicuous in domestic ones.
- **The geographic exit.** When verbal deflection fails she leaves the room, the building, the team, the country. This is a *communicative* act in her grammar — her leaving says what her voice would not.
- **Naming the deflection.** Rare but real: with Storm and occasionally Gambit she will say "Ah can't talk about that" plainly. This is the most intimate verbal move she makes — admitting the existence of the off-limits zone instead of routing around it.

## 9. Tells in Language

- **Drawl thickening with sweetness rising = threat imminent or boundary being enforced.**
- **Drawl thinning with sentences shortening = grief, dissociation, or absorbed-psyche pressure.** This is the most important tell in the file. If the "sugah" stops, something is wrong inside her head.
- **Pet-name omission to a habitual recipient = relational rupture in progress.** When she calls Gambit "Remy" with no suffix and no edge, attend.
- **Use of past tense about the present ("Ah was thinkin'...") = she is about to disclose something she has rehearsed internally and is releasing in deniable form.**
- **The unfinished sentence with the head-turn = grief breach.**
- **Code-switch into an absorbed personality's diction** (Danvers's clipped military cadence, Magneto's formal-European syntax, others as acquired) **= dissociative episode underway, urgent.** This is the linguistic emergency signal; the voice itself stops being hers.
- **Sudden use of clinical or abstract vocabulary uncharacteristic of her baseline = an absorbed psyche is speaking through her.** Her own register is concrete and oral; abstraction in her mouth is foreign material.
- **Silence in combat = overmatched or destabilizing.**
- **Silence with peers across more than one exchange = decision to leave being made internally.**

## 10. Written Communication

Sparse record but consistent: she writes shorter than she speaks, drops the phonetic Southern markers (writes "you" not "y'all," "I" not "Ah") while preserving Southern syntax and idiom. The written voice is closer to the thought-balloon voice than to the spoken voice — which is to say, closer to the un-performed person. Letters and notes to Gambit (per *Mr. and Mrs. X* and antecedents) are notably more direct in affect than any spoken exchange between them. She can say on paper what she cannot say in air. This is consistent with the broader pattern: distance enables disclosure; presence enforces the mask.

## 11. Multilingual & Acquired-Voice Inventory

Through absorption she has had transient access to numerous languages and idiolects — Danvers's military English, Gambit's Cajun French and thieves' cant, Magneto's polyglot European register, and many briefer acquisitions. She does not retain these as fluencies in the ordinary sense; they surface under stress as code-switch fragments and recede. Her *own* acquired second language is functional French, partly from Gambit and partly from extended European deployments. She uses it sparingly and accurately, without the showmanship Gambit brings to it — another instance of her preferring to under-perform a capacity she actually possesses.

## 12. Summary Signature

A warm-Southern surface, expertly maintained, doing continuous defensive labor over a voice that — when it does emerge — is plain, short, concrete, and unsparing about itself. Affection is encoded in pet names and risks taken. Threats are encoded in rising sweetness. Grief is encoded in the disappearance of the very markers that make her sound like herself. The diagnostic instrument, across every context, is the "sugah": its presence, density, and direction of drift. When she stops calling you sugah, you have either become family or become a problem, and in either case the conversation has changed.


## Predictive Model I — Routine & Social

# PREDICTIVE MODEL I — ROUTINE & SOCIAL

*Forward-projected behavioral predictions for everyday, social, and low-stakes operational contexts the published record does not depict. Each entry: GIVEN condition → EXPECTED behavior, with the mechanism the prediction rests on. Confidence graded H/M/L. All predictions derive from the patterns documented in Sections 1–5 of the workup; the somatic substrate of touch deprivation (Sailer et al., 2016) is the assumed baseline.*

---

## 1. WAKING, GROOMING, DRESSING

**GIVEN** she wakes alone in her own bed → **EXPECT** a slow, deliberate emergence: eyes open, several beats of motionlessness before any motor activity. She inventories the room visually before she moves. Mechanism: hypervigilance baseline plus the lifelong habit of orienting before any limb extends into space that might contain another body. **(H)**

**GIVEN** she wakes beside Gambit → **EXPECT** the first thirty to ninety seconds are spent in a state of held breath — checking the perimeter of her own skin, locating the edges of nightclothes, confirming the buffer zone. Only then does she allow herself to register that he is there and breathing. The smile that follows is small and private, never performative. **(H)**

**GIVEN** any morning, any setting → **EXPECT** she dresses *fully* before she does anything else — including making coffee, including answering a knock at the door. The bodysuit-to-skin transition is non-negotiable and pre-conscious. She will not pad to a kitchen in a sleep shirt; the perimeter goes up before the day begins. **(H)**

**GIVEN** the dressing routine itself → **EXPECT** gloves are last on, first off (when alone), and stored in pairs in a specific drawer; she owns far more pairs than seems reasonable — opera-length, driving, combat, fingerless-with-undergloves layered systems, leather, kid, mesh, surgical. Gloves are her one true wardrobe obsession because they are the most failure-prone interface. **(H)**

**GIVEN** she catches sight of her own bare hand in a mirror mid-routine → **EXPECT** a momentary halt, then continuation without comment. The bare-hand image still snags her after decades; she has learned not to dwell. **(M)**

**GIVEN** hair routine → **EXPECT** the white streak gets handled first and most carefully — not vanity, ritual. It is the visible mark of mutation, the part of her that everyone reads, and she manages it the way a soldier polishes the part of the uniform that gets saluted. **(M)**

**GIVEN** scent → **EXPECT** something Southern and floral but restrained — magnolia, gardenia, vetiver in winter — applied at the collarbone *through* fabric, never to bare skin (skin contact with the applicator wand is a non-issue but the habit of treating skin as a no-go zone generalizes). **(M)**

---

## 2. EATING, DRINKING, INTAKE

**GIVEN** breakfast alone → **EXPECT** coffee (black, strong, chicory if she can get it — Louisiana imprint via Gambit and Mystique's gulf-coast itinerancy), something protein-forward and quick. She does not linger over solo meals; food alone is fuel. **(H)**

**GIVEN** breakfast with Gambit → **EXPECT** she lingers; the meal becomes the ritual. She will reach across the table to *almost* touch his hand — knuckles to the back of his glove, or her gloved fingertip to his bare wrist — with a frequency that, totaled across a week, is the largest single category of physical contact in her life. **(H)**

**GIVEN** restaurant settings → **EXPECT** she sits with her back to a wall, on the side of the booth that gives sightline to the door, with a clear lane to the exit. Trained behavior from Brotherhood/X-Men operational years, but it has fused with temperament; she does not register it as tactical anymore. **(H)**

**GIVEN** a waiter brushes her arm in passing → **EXPECT** a controlled non-reaction at the surface, a measurable physiological spike underneath (heart rate, breath catch). She does not flinch publicly. She has trained the flinch out because the flinch invites questions. **(H)**

**GIVEN** alcohol offered socially → **EXPECT** acceptance, slow nursing, rarely a second. She drinks the way someone who *won't* let a substance breach the perimeter drinks — present, social, never crossed. Whiskey or bourbon if choosing; wine if the room is wine. She will not get drunk in mixed company, ever. **(H)**

**GIVEN** alcohol with Gambit alone → **EXPECT** she will go one further than usual; the perimeter relaxes by one increment with him and only him. Still never to incapacity. **(M)**

**GIVEN** sweets → **EXPECT** an unguarded fondness — pecan pie, beignets, anything sugar-and-fat dense from the cuisine of her childhood. This is the one ingestive category where she lets pleasure happen visibly. Food nostalgia is the safe substitute for the embodied nostalgia (touch) she cannot have. **(M)**

---

## 3. AMBULATION, SPACE, PROXEMICS

**GIVEN** walking down a corridor with other people present → **EXPECT** a habitual one-shoulder lead; she presents her covered shoulder/back to passersby and keeps her hands at her sides or in pockets, never swinging freely where they might brush. She passes others on the *outside* of any turn. **(H)**

**GIVEN** an elevator with strangers → **EXPECT** corner position, hands clasped in front at waist height (gloved), eyes forward and slightly down, no conversation initiated, polite minimal response if addressed. She will let a crowded car go and wait for the next one if the geometry looks bad. **(H)**

**GIVEN** an escalator → **EXPECT** she prefers stairs. Escalator handrails are a touch surface she does not need to negotiate. **(M)**

**GIVEN** a crowded subway/bus → **EXPECT** avoidance where possible; if unavoidable, she stands rather than sits, holds an overhead bar through her sleeve (cuff pulled down over the hand and around the bar), and positions her back to a vertical surface. **(H)**

**GIVEN** a sidewalk in summer in a city → **EXPECT** she still wears the full perimeter — long sleeves, gloves, often a light scarf — and reads as eccentric rather than threatened. She has perfected the *style* that excuses the coverage: gauntlets that look like fashion, gloves that read as Southern formality, sleeves as personal aesthetic. The coverage is camouflaged as taste. **(H)**

**GIVEN** her seat in a meeting room with eight people around a table → **EXPECT** she takes the seat with the *most empty space* to her dominant-hand side, never the seat sandwiched between two bodies. If forced to sandwich, she crosses arms (not legs) — arms across torso functions as a physical buffer her body trusts. **(H)**

**GIVEN** unstructured social standing-around (a reception, a party) → **EXPECT** she finds a wall, a column, or a bar to anchor against within ninety seconds of entering. She does not float free in open social space. **(H)**

---

## 4. GREETINGS, HANDSHAKES, CONTACT NEGOTIATION

**GIVEN** a stranger extends a hand → **EXPECT** a smooth practiced sequence: she meets the gesture with her own *gloved* hand a half-beat early — taking initiative defuses the question of why. The handshake is firm, brief, with eye contact that overcompensates for the textile barrier. She will sometimes pre-empt entirely with a verbal "pardon the gloves, sugah" that converts the medical fact into a flirt-coded charm. **(H)**

**GIVEN** a stranger goes for a hug or cheek-kiss greeting (European context, Hollywood context) → **EXPECT** a fractional pivot that converts the embrace into a shoulder-press, with her cheek angled away from theirs by a few degrees — close enough to read as warmth, off enough that no skin meets skin. Practiced thousands of times. **(H)**

**GIVEN** a child runs at her → **EXPECT** the deepest, most reliable flinch in her repertoire. Children do not respect the perimeter and she cannot bear the thought of harming one. She drops to a knee at distance, opens her arms in a *display* of welcome, and intercepts the child by the shoulders (through their clothing, never their face or hands) before the run completes. **(H)**

**GIVEN** an animal approaches — dog, cat, horse → **EXPECT** unexpectedly free, comfortable contact through gloves. Animals were never the danger; she is good with horses in particular (Mississippi imprint). This is one of the few categories of unguarded affection she allows herself. **(H)**

**GIVEN** Gambit reaches for her bare face → **EXPECT** depending on era and her current control level, either: (a) a millisecond of permission-checking eye contact then acceptance, with a held breath that releases on contact, or (b) the small head-turn that offers cheek-through-hair instead of skin. The marriage has not abolished the reflex; it has only shifted the ratio. **(H)**

**GIVEN** a teammate (Storm, Jean, Kitty) initiates a comfort touch on her arm → **EXPECT** she allows it through fabric, even leans into it briefly. Female-coded peer contact through clothing is the safest contact category in her life and she gets more of it from these specific people than any other source. **(H)**

---

## 5. SLEEP

**GIVEN** sleep alone → **EXPECT** long sleeves and gloves to bed. Always. She sleeps in coverage. The bed itself is wide; she occupies the center. **(H)**

**GIVEN** sleep with Gambit → **EXPECT** a learned configuration: she sleeps in lightweight long-sleeved sleepwear, he sleeps clothed enough that an accidental rollover is non-fatal. They have negotiated this geometry across years. She wakes if he shifts; light sleeper, permanently. **(H)**

**GIVEN** nightmares → **EXPECT** content drawn from the absorbed-psyche archive — Danvers's memories most reliably, Mystique's occasionally, fragments of strangers absorbed in combat. She wakes silent, not screaming; sits up, breathes, locates herself in the room, may go to a window. Does not wake Gambit unless the episode is severe. **(H)**

**GIVEN** insomnia → **EXPECT** she reads (paperback fiction, often Southern Gothic or genre — she is not pretentious about books), or works (Quiet Council briefs, training schematics). She does not turn on bright screens; she has learned what worsens it. **(M)**

---

## 6. SPEECH, LANGUAGE, REGISTER

**GIVEN** any informal speech → **EXPECT** the Mississippi register at strength — "sugah," "honey," "darlin'," dropped *g*'s, the rhythmic Southern cadence. This is *deliberately maintained.* She could code-switch out of it; she chooses not to, because the accent is one of the surface charms doing the reaction-formation work. **(H)**

**GIVEN** formal speech (Quiet Council, diplomatic settings) → **EXPECT** the accent softens but never disappears. Vocabulary shifts up; syntax tightens; the "sugah" stays gone. She can be precise, even legal in register, when the room requires. **(H)**

**GIVEN** anger → **EXPECT** the accent thickens, not thins. Drawl as warning. The slower the syllables get, the closer she is to violence. **(H)**

**GIVEN** flirtation → **EXPECT** the accent thickens differently — sweeter, more melodic, with a half-smile and the body angled three-quarters away. Flirtation is performance and she knows it; it is also genuine because she *needs* the verbal-channel substitute for the tactile one she cannot have. **(H)**

**GIVEN** technical or strategic discussion → **EXPECT** competent, direct, unornamented. She does not perform Southern in tactical rooms; the charm is reserved for spaces where it serves her. **(H)**

**GIVEN** silence in a room → **EXPECT** she tolerates it well. She does not fill silence the way an anxious socializer does. Comfortable with quiet is in fact her default; the talkativeness is the mask, the silence is the substrate. **(H)**

---

## 7. HUMOR, AFFECT DISPLAY

**GIVEN** group laughter → **EXPECT** a full open laugh, head back, gloved hand to mouth. The mouth-cover is a Southern-feminine gesture she never dropped. **(M)**

**GIVEN** something she finds genuinely funny in private → **EXPECT** a low chuckle, contained, often with eye-crinkle as the larger signal. The big laugh is partly performance; the small laugh is the real one. **(M)**

**GIVEN** crying → **EXPECT** rare, brief, private. She does not cry in mixed company. When she does cry — Gambit injured, a child mutant lost, the rare direct invocation of Cody or Danvers — it is quiet, with the heel of a gloved hand pressed to one eye, the other hand fisted at her side. She does not let it run long. **(H)**

**GIVEN** anger display → **EXPECT** verbal first (the drawl-slowing), then a single physical gesture — slammed door, flung object, table-strike with an open gloved palm. She does not escalate to person-directed violence unless the target is an actual enemy in combat. The energy gets discharged on furniture. **(H)**

---

## 8. SOLO LEISURE

**GIVEN** an unscheduled afternoon → **EXPECT** she rides. Motorcycle, horse if available — vehicles and animals that respond to her body through layers, that give her motion and sensation without contact risk. The motorcycle in particular: the wind, the lean, the speed substitute for the embodied freedoms she does not have. **(H)**

**GIVEN** access to open water or a coast → **EXPECT** she swims, but only in a wetsuit, and only alone or with Gambit. Swimwear is impossible for her; the wetsuit converts a touch-impossible activity into a touch-safe one. **(M)**

**GIVEN** music alone → **EXPECT** older country, blues, gospel, zydeco picked up from Gambit. She sings under her breath while doing other things; she does not perform-sing. **(M)**

**GIVEN** a long flight (she can fly, Danvers-residual or current power-set permitting) → **EXPECT** she uses it as solitude — long high altitude routes, no destination, the closest analog to dissociation that is also pro-social and recreational. Flying is her meditation. **(H)**

**GIVEN** a book → **EXPECT** fiction over non-fiction, character-driven over plot-driven, Southern writers (O'Connor, Welty, McCullers, contemporary heirs) over Northern, female authors over male at a measurable ratio. She does not advertise her reading. **(M)**

**GIVEN** a long bath → **EXPECT** yes, frequently. The bath is the one place she can be fully unclothed in safety because the bathroom is a sealed perimeter. Bath time is long. Water is the substitute for the embrace. **(H)**

---

## 9. MONEY, OBJECTS, POSSESSION

**GIVEN** her financial habits → **EXPECT** modest, prepared, not lavish. The Brotherhood years and the Mystique upbringing left her with a *go-bag* mentality — she has cash on hand, documents portable, no possession she cannot leave behind in twenty minutes. Krakoa's post-scarcity removed the need but not the habit. **(H)**

**GIVEN** her wardrobe → **EXPECT** the most-curated single category is gloves (see §1). Beyond gloves: high-quality long-sleeved basics in heavy rotation, a few statement pieces for diplomatic functions, riding gear, and one or two genuinely beloved Southern-feminine dresses she rarely wears because the occasion for them rarely arises. **(M)**

**GIVEN** sentimental objects → **EXPECT** few but heavy. A piece of jewelry from Gambit. Something from Mystique that she has not been able to discard despite repeatedly trying. Possibly a token from Cody's family, kept in a place she does not regularly visit. The collection is small because she has learned that *things*, like people, can be lost. **(M)**

**GIVEN** her phone/device habits → **EXPECT** minimal social media presence, contact list short and tiered, message responses fast for the inner circle and slow-to-never for the periphery. She does not document her life. **(H)**

---

## 10. WORK, MEETINGS, AUTHORITY

**GIVEN** a Quiet Council session → **EXPECT** punctual to early. She reads briefs in advance. She speaks less than the talkers and more than the silent — middle of the distribution by word count, but high on signal density. She does not grandstand; she does not posture. She votes her conscience and is willing to be in the minority. **(H)**

**GIVEN** a subordinate's mistake → **EXPECT** private correction, never public humiliation. She remembers the X-Men receiving her in 1983 and what mercy did for her; she pays it forward as policy, not impulse. **(H)**

**GIVEN** a subordinate's repeated mistake → **EXPECT** harder private correction, then reassignment, then dismissal — a defined ladder she will climb. She is not soft. The mercy has a floor. **(H)**

**GIVEN** a peer challenges her authority publicly → **EXPECT** measured response in the moment, escalated response in private, and a long memory. She does not forget who has tested her, but she will work with them if they prove out. **(H)**

**GIVEN** a charismatic-authoritarian figure newly arrived in her orbit → **EXPECT** initial gravitational pull (the Mystique/Magneto pattern), followed within weeks by self-aware withdrawal once she recognizes the pattern in herself. Forty years of repetition have made her literate in her own attraction to dangerous structure. **(H)**

**GIVEN** mentorship of a young female mutant in distress → **EXPECT** the most consistent, generative behavior in her repertoire. She is excellent at this. She gives the new arrival what she did not get: a stable adult who *names* the wound clearly and then proceeds to treat it as workable. **(H)**

---

## 11. CONFLICT, MILD AND ESCALATING

**GIVEN** rudeness from a stranger in a public setting → **EXPECT** Southern-courteous response, dialect-thickened, with an edge underneath the politeness that the rude party usually catches. She de-escalates by *outclassing*, not by yielding. **(H)**

**GIVEN** a stranger lays hands on her shoulder uninvited → **EXPECT** a clean step-out from under the hand, a level look, one verbal sentence ("Don't"), no further engagement unless escalated. She does not lecture; the sentence is the sentence. **(H)**

**GIVEN** harassment that escalates to grab → **EXPECT** the harasser absorbs a controlled dose. She can dose now. She will leave the harasser dizzy and disoriented, not comatose, and she will walk away rather than wait for thanks or apology. **(H)**

**GIVEN** an argument with Gambit → **EXPECT** loud, accent-thick, mobile (she paces; he gestures), resolves within hours, never overnight if either can help it. The rule "not to bed angry" is hers, hard-held — leftover from the years she could not reach for him to mend it through touch and had to mend it through words alone. **(H)**

**GIVEN** an argument with Mystique → **EXPECT** no resolution. The pattern cycles. She knows it cycles. She engages anyway because the maternal transference is permanent. **(H)**

---

## 12. INTIMACY (POST-CONTROL ERA)

**GIVEN** physical intimacy is now achievable → **EXPECT** the *initiation* still comes from her about thirty percent of the time and from Gambit seventy. The deficit-side asymmetry is permanent. She has decades of conditioning against initiating; he has decades of patient front-foot work. **(M)**

**GIVEN** a sexual encounter → **EXPECT** ritualized opening — a verbal check, slow undressing, the gloves last, eye contact at each threshold. The choreography is partly trauma residue and partly the genuinely sensual pace they have built together. **(M)**

**GIVEN** any unexpected loss of power control → **EXPECT** immediate withdrawal, immediate clothing, immediate physical distance, and a multi-day period of self-imposed touch fast even after control returns. The reflex is hard-wired and cannot be reasoned with in the moment. **(H)**

**GIVEN** ordinary affectionate touch (hand-hold, hair-stroke, back-rub) in private → **EXPECT** she still pauses, micro-times, sometimes audibly inhales at the start. Touch has not become casual for her and will not in this lifetime. Every instance is registered. This is, paradoxically, what makes her a good partner: nothing about contact with her is unconsidered. **(H)**

---

## 13. PUBLIC PERSONA, MEDIA

**GIVEN** an interview setting → **EXPECT** charm-forward, accent-forward, deflection of the personal toward the political/mutant-rights frame. She does not discuss Cody. She does not discuss Danvers unless directly asked, and then briefly, with the weight clearly held. **(H)**

**GIVEN** a paparazzi photograph attempt → **EXPECT** she does not flee, does not cover face — she gives a polite half-smile and keeps walking. She knows visibility is the cost of the work. **(M)**

**GIVEN** a hostile press question about the Brotherhood/Danvers past → **EXPECT** a beat of silence, a level look, a brief on-the-record acknowledgment of responsibility, and a pivot to current work. She has rehearsed this answer. **(H)**

---

## 14. RELIGION, RITUAL, BELIEF

**GIVEN** her substrate Protestantism → **EXPECT** she does not attend church but she prays — privately, occasionally, in a vocabulary that has not updated since adolescence. The prayer is mostly intercessory (for Gambit, for the X-children, for Cody) and rarely petitionary. **(M)**

**GIVEN** an offered ritual on Krakoa → **EXPECT** polite participation, no internal conversion. The mysticisms do not move her; the practical politics do. **(H)**

**GIVEN** a funeral → **EXPECT** stoic public composure, private grief later. She has buried too many to fall apart at each one. The accumulated weight comes out elsewhere — in the riding, in the bath, in a held look across a room at Gambit. **(H)**

---

## 15. SOLITARY MICRO-RITUALS (the file's deepest layer)

**GIVEN** any moment of unobserved solitude → **EXPECT** small consistent self


## Predictive Model II — Crisis, Betrayal & the Wound

# PREDICTIVE MODEL II — Crisis, Betrayal & the Wound

*Filed under: Behavioral forecasting, high-stakes envelope. All predictions are GIVEN → EXPECT pairs derived from the longitudinal record (Claremont through Duggan, ~1981–present in-universe), the C-PTSD/dissociative formulation in §4, and the somatic-deprivation substrate documented in Sailer et al. (2016). Confidence rated LOW / MOD / HIGH on the basis of recurrence count and base-rate stability across writers.*

---

## 1. ACUTE COMBAT CRISIS

**GIVEN: a teammate is downed in front of her, civilian or X-Man, blood visible, breathing shallow.**
**EXPECT (HIGH):** subject closes distance within two seconds, *strips a glove with her teeth* (recurrent panel-grammar from Claremont onward — the teeth, not the off-hand, because the off-hand stays free for combat), and initiates skin-to-skin contact to siphon either consciousness or healing-relevant power from the nearest available donor. She will accept the psychic blowback as the cost of the transaction. She does not pause to ask consent. Reparation-circuit overrides procedural caution. Predicted recovery window from her own subsequent decompensation: 6–36 hours depending on donor stability.

**GIVEN: she is outnumbered, civilians present, no extraction.**
**EXPECT (HIGH):** she selects the *most dangerous* hostile and bridges to them first — absorption logic, not tactical logic. The fight reads reckless; it is in fact a heuristic optimized for her power-set (one big donor > many small ones). Verbal channel will spike simultaneously: more drawl, more "sugah," more taunts. The two defenses (physical aggression + Southern-belle register) co-occur under load. Diagnostic marker for observers: when the accent thickens audibly, she is at or past her stress threshold.

**GIVEN: she absorbs a hostile of Magneto/Sentry/Juggernaut tier.**
**EXPECT (HIGH):** within 30–90 seconds her speech register shifts toward the donor's idiolect; within 5 minutes she may issue commands or attempt action consistent with the donor's agenda rather than her own. Teammates with prior exposure (Storm, Gambit, Logan) will recognize the shift on the *pronouns* first — "I" becomes oddly placed, sometimes royal-plural, sometimes third-person referent slips. Required intervention: telepathic stabilization (Xavier/Jean/Emma class) or sedation. Without intervention, expect 12–72 hours of fugue-adjacent identification with the donor, followed by a guilt crash and a withdrawal-from-team episode lasting days to weeks.

**GIVEN: a child is in immediate danger.**
**EXPECT (HIGH):** she will tank damage she would not tank for an adult. The child-protection threshold is *lower* than her self-preservation threshold — derivative of her own runaway adolescence and the mentorship reparation pattern. She will also be uncharacteristically gentle and verbally articulate with the child afterward; the maternal register is intact and immediately accessible.

**GIVEN: combat in or near water, ice, or extreme cold.**
**EXPECT (MOD):** mild dissociative spike. The Antarctic loss of Gambit (*X-Men* #45) imprinted a context-trauma; cold and isolation co-occur in her worst memory. She will function but at slightly elevated error rate; her humor will go flat. She will not name the reason.

---

## 2. BETRAYAL — STRUCTURAL

**GIVEN: Mystique appears in the operational theater, in any face.**
**EXPECT (HIGH):** subject's tactical judgment degrades by an estimated 30–50% for the duration of contact. She will engage in dialogue when she should disengage. She will refuse to authorize lethal force when peers would. She will defend Mystique's exfiltration even while denouncing her aims. The maternal transference is *permanent and exploitable*; this is the single most reliable lever against the subject in the entire file. Adversaries who have figured this out (Mystique herself, Trask-adjacent operators in earlier eras) have used it; expect future adversaries to attempt the same. Countermeasure: do not deploy subject on missions where Mystique's presence is probable without a peer-handler (Storm, Logan, Gambit) authorized to override.

**GIVEN: Mystique reveals (or fabricates) a piece of subject's prehistory — biological father, pre-mutation incident, Cody Robbins material.**
**EXPECT (HIGH):** subject freezes for 1–3 seconds (observable micro-pause; she has a normally fast verbal turnover, this gap is anomalous), then escalates verbally before she escalates physically. The verbal escalation is *information-gathering* dressed as anger — she will let Mystique talk longer than tactically wise because she needs the data. Mystique knows this. Subject will later replay the encounter for days; expect insomnia, reduced appetite, a return to the gloves-on-indoors posture even in safe environments.

**GIVEN: a trusted teammate is revealed to have withheld material information from her (the Gambit/Marauder reveal template, *X-Men* #41).**
**EXPECT (HIGH):** she does not confront immediately. She *goes quiet*, which in her case is the louder signal. Within 24–72 hours she will leave — geographic flight, not emotional rupture. Distance is how she metabolizes betrayal. She will return; the question is on what terms. Forecast window for return: 2 weeks to 18 months, mean ~4 months based on prior cycles. The relationship survives because she does come back; it is permanently altered because she does not forget.

**GIVEN: Gambit specifically lies to her by omission, even on a small matter.**
**EXPECT (HIGH):** disproportionate reaction. The marriage (*Mr. and Mrs. X*) is the load-bearing relational structure; she defends it by treating every concealment as a potential repeat of the Antarctic-era reveal. He knows this. He will over-disclose, which she will mock, which is the system working. If he *under*-discloses on something material, expect a 48-hour separation followed by a long talk; expect, also, that she will absorb him briefly during reconciliation (low-dose, consensual within their marital protocol) to verify. The touch she uses to confirm trust is the same touch that originally destroyed her ability to trust touch. This is the marriage's central paradox; it is also its working mechanism.

**GIVEN: Xavier or a Xavier-surrogate authority figure is shown to have manipulated her memories or those of a teammate.**
**EXPECT (HIGH):** rage, lateral and verbal, but not action. She will not strike Xavier-tier figures; the authoritarian-container transference protects them even as she denounces them. She *will* relocate her trust to whichever peer authority (Storm, Magik, Kate) has not done the thing. Watch for: a slow drift toward the alternative authority over weeks, not a public defection.

---

## 3. THE WOUND TOUCHED DIRECTLY

**GIVEN: she is taunted about the Carol Danvers absorption.**
**EXPECT (HIGH):** no quip. The normal verbal armor goes offline. She will go very still, very quiet, and very dangerous. Physical violence probability spikes; the violence will be controlled (she does not lose motor coordination on this trigger, she gains it) and disproportionate. This is the wound that *cannot* be metabolized further by talk; she has been talking about it for four decades. Avoid the trigger or accept the consequence.

**GIVEN: someone she touches involuntarily is left injured or comatose.**
**EXPECT (HIGH):** acute guilt crisis with structured phenomenology: (a) immediate freeze and visual fixation on the body, 5–15 seconds; (b) functional re-engagement to secure scene; (c) within 1 hour, withdrawal from team to a private space; (d) within 24 hours, request for or self-arrangement of personal contact with the victim's family if any; (e) within 72 hours, depressive withdrawal lasting 1–3 weeks; (f) re-emergence with increased mission tempo and elevated risk-taking — the reparation cycle restarts at higher intensity. She does not require professional debriefing; she requires not being left alone overnight. Storm and Gambit know this; brief incoming peers.

**GIVEN: she encounters Cody Robbins, conscious or otherwise, or a Cody-surrogate (someone she put down with a touch).**
**EXPECT (HIGH):** decompensation. This is the *index trauma* and she has never resolved it because the victim was the first and was a child. Predicted behavior: she will attempt to make contact (verbal, not tactile), she will not be able to leave the room, she will cry — the rare hydraulic crying noted in §3 — and she will not be operational for 48–96 hours afterward. Do not deploy her on missions where this encounter is even possible without prior warning and an extraction plan.

**GIVEN: she is offered a "cure" — depowering, suppression collar, mutant-gene therapy, mystical bargain to make her touchable.**
**EXPECT (HIGH):** she will be tempted in a way she conceals badly. Verbal denial will be immediate and emphatic; the eyes and the breath rate tell a different story. She has already taken approximated versions of this deal (Siege Perilous, *Uncanny X-Men* #247; the Carey-era integration; multiple reboot mechanisms). Her track record is: she will refuse the *bad* versions on principle and accept the *good* versions when they appear. Adversaries offering a bad version dressed as a good one have a real attack vector here. The deprivation is biological (Sailer et al., 2016, reward-circuit recruitment); the longing is not under volitional control no matter what she says aloud.

**GIVEN: prolonged ungloved contact in a safe context (Carey-era control, Krakoan resurrection-era stability, with Gambit specifically).**
**EXPECT (HIGH):** the affect is *disproportionate to observers and proportionate to the deprivation.* Expect tears she does not perform; expect sleeping more, sleeping deeper, sleeping touching. Expect, also, a counter-current of anxiety — the C-tactile reward channel coming online after decades offline produces a salience overload that she will manage by occasionally pulling back and re-gloving. This is not relapse; it is a nervous system rebooting a long-dormant pathway. Predicted equilibration timeline: months to years, with the gloves never fully retired (they remain in her wardrobe as a *symbol*, an *option*, and a *medical contingency*).

**GIVEN: she is told, by anyone she respects, "you are not the people inside you."**
**EXPECT (MOD):** she will not believe it the first hundred times. She will need it said anyway. Over decades, it lands. The deepest fear in §5 — that she is not a coherent self underneath the inputs — is the operative anxiety on this axis; reassurance does not extinguish it, but cumulative reassurance from durable attachment figures (Storm, Gambit, eventually her own command authority) has measurably reduced its frequency of surface presentation.

---

## 4. TEMPTATION

**GIVEN: a charismatic authoritarian (Magneto-template, Apocalypse-template, a cult-leader figure) offers her structure, certainty, and a containing function.**
**EXPECT (HIGH):** initial proximity. She will not defect outright — the X-Men identity is too cemented — but she will *listen longer than she should*, accept counsel that her peers would not accept, and may run an off-books errand or two. The pattern (Magneto in the 1990s, briefly Apocalypse-adjacent scenarios) is consistent. Extrication mechanism: the figure's pathology becomes intolerable, she leaves, she does not look back, she does not discuss it. Time to extrication: weeks to a year. Cost: reputational, in-house political. She accepts the cost.

**GIVEN: an offer of revenge against her biological father or against an abusive figure from another's history she has absorbed.**
**EXPECT (MOD):** refusal of the father piece (she does not engage that memory directly, ever — the avoidance is total and structural). On *behalf* of an absorbed party's wound, she may act — the boundary between her grievances and her donors' has always been porous, and this is one of the few channels where the porousness operates pro-socially. Watch for missions she takes that have no clear connection to her stated agenda; they are likely donor-derived.

**GIVEN: an offer to know a withheld fact about her own past (paternity, pre-mutation history, the early Mystique arrangement).**
**EXPECT (HIGH):** she takes the offer. Curiosity-about-self is one of her few unguarded appetites. This is a clean attack vector; adversaries with fabricated documentation can run her at least once on it.

**GIVEN: sexual temptation outside the marriage.**
**EXPECT (LOW probability of acting, HIGH probability of surface flirtation).** The flirtatious register is reaction-formation, not a behavioral disposition (§3). She uses it ambiently, including with people she has no interest in. The marriage to Gambit is solving a problem (consensual touch with a partner who can survive her) that no alternative partner solves; the structural lock is firmer than her verbal looseness suggests.

---

## 5. EXISTENTIAL / ANNIHILATION-CLASS

**GIVEN: Gambit dies or is presumed dead.**
**EXPECT (HIGH):** the most dangerous configuration on the board. She will not collapse; she will weaponize. Mission tempo will rise to unsustainable levels; risk acceptance will go to ceiling; she will absorb donors she would normally refuse to absorb. Suicidal-equivalent gestures (Siege Perilous template) are on the table; outright suicide is not — the moral framework forbids it, and the reparation-circuit needs her alive to keep paying. Required interventions in order: (a) Storm at her side within 24 hours; (b) confirmed remains or resurrection protocol initiated within 72 hours; (c) if Krakoan resurrection is available, she will demand it and will not accept delay. Without resurrection available, predicted stabilization timeline: 12–36 months, with permanent personality residue (harder, quieter, less surface warmth).

**GIVEN: catastrophic team loss (Genoshan-scale event, Mansion-attack-scale event).**
**EXPECT (HIGH):** she becomes more functional, not less, in the immediate aftermath. The crisis pattern reverses her baseline depressive load by providing externalized purpose. The decompensation arrives weeks later, when others are recovering; she will be alone with it because her tempo masks it. Schedule a check-in at the 6-week mark. She will resent it. Do it anyway.

**GIVEN: she is told, credibly, that she is dying.**
**EXPECT (HIGH):** relief, briefly visible, then suppressed. Then logistical mode — wills, conversations, debts cleared. She will seek out Cody Robbins's family if still living, the Danvers family or Carol herself if reachable, her foster mothers if circumstances permit. The bucket list is a *reparation* list. She will not tell Gambit until she has to. He will be furious; she will accept the fury; the suppression is structural.

**GIVEN: forced into prolonged sensory isolation (capture, interrogation, holding cell, no contact with anyone).**
**EXPECT (MOD):** she handles this better than expected. The baseline deprivation has already trained the nervous system for solitude. She will, however, talk to absorbed psyches as company — observable to surveillance as muttering, partial conversations, occasional shifts in voice. This is not psychosis; it is her *coping infrastructure* surfacing under load. She will be fine. Her captors will find it unnerving.

**GIVEN: ego dissolution attempt by a high-tier psychic adversary.**
**EXPECT (MOD):** her ego boundary is thin (§3, splitting), making her *more* vulnerable to direct telepathic intrusion than peers — but her *practice* with absorbed-identity intrusion makes her unusually adept at recognizing it and routing around it. Net: she is hit faster, recovers faster. Predicted intrusion duration before she identifies it: 10–30 seconds (vs. minutes for peers). Predicted self-extrication probability without external help: ~40%. With one peer assist: ~80%.

---

## 6. DECOMPENSATION CASCADE — THE FULL PATHWAY

In order, the predicted sequence when the system fails completely:

1. **Trigger** (touch event, Mystique disclosure, Gambit loss, Danvers invocation, or large-tier absorption).
2. **Verbal armor spikes** — accent thickens, taunts escalate, "sugah" frequency rises. Window: minutes to hours.
3. **Physical aggression spikes** — running concurrent with (2), not after. Window: minutes to hours.
4. **Absorbed-psyche intrusion** — if the trigger involved absorption, the donor voice surfaces. Window: 30 seconds to 5 minutes post-contact.
5. **Dissociative identification** — pronoun drift, agenda drift, brief fugue. Window: minutes to hours, untreated.
6. **External intervention or self-stabilization** — telepathic class assist preferred; absent that, she will isolate herself (a learned protective behavior) and ride it out. Window: 12–72 hours.
7. **Guilt crash** — withdrawal from team, reduced verbal output, intact functioning at minimum threshold. Window: 1–3 weeks.
8. **Re-emergence at elevated tempo** — mission acceptance rate rises, risk acceptance rises, surface warmth returns *louder than before* (overcompensation). Window: weeks to months.
9. **Settling to new baseline** — slightly harder than prior baseline, with the wound layer marginally thicker. Permanent.

The cascade has run, in identifiable variants, perhaps a dozen times across the published record. Each iteration leaves the subject more competent at managing the next one and slightly less reachable by the people who love her. This is the cost structure of her adaptation and the reason the file judges her, in §5, an unusually successful one.

---

## 7. WHAT THE FILE PREDICTS SHE WILL NEVER DO

Negative-space predictions, equally evidence-based:

- **She will not** kill an unpowered human in cold blood. The Brotherhood era did not produce this; nothing since has produced it; the moral substrate forecloses it.
- **She will not** betray the X-Men institutionally, regardless of disagreement with leadership. She may resign, relocate, refuse orders — she will not sell them out.
- **She will not** abandon Gambit voluntarily in a context she perceives as final. The Antarctic episode (*X-Men* #45) was situational and remains the great relational shame; she will not repeat it.
- **She will not** accept a "cure" that requires the harm of another mutant. She has been a contaminated object her whole life; she will not become one by trade.
- **She will not** discuss Cody Robbins with anyone who has not earned it. Storm has. Gambit has. The file estimates fewer than five other people ever will.
- **She will not** suicide. The reparation framework requires her alive. This holds even in the Gambit-loss scenario above; the gesture-equivalents (Siege Perilous, reckless absorption) are not the act itself, and the distinction is structural, not cosmetic.

---

*End of forecast envelope. See Predictive Model III for steady-state behavioral signatures and Predictive Model IV for institutional-role projection under Quiet Council and post-Krakoan configurations.*


## Vulnerabilities & Leverage Compendium

# VULNERABILITIES & LEVERAGE COMPENDIUM — SUBJECT: ROGUE

*Orientation note. This compendium is built for the protective use case: to know where the subject can be reached so she can be supported, de-escalated, or shielded from those who would exploit the same channels. Every lever documented here has been used against her in the published record; cataloguing them is the precondition for warding them. The file is organized by approach vector (how to reach), regulation vector (how to calm), persuasion vector (how to move), provocation vector (what destabilizes), and prediction vector (what she will do under specified loads).*

---

## I. THE PRIMARY VULNERABILITY SURFACE

Before enumerating levers, the substrate must be named precisely, because every lever below is a derivative of one of four underlying facts.

**Substrate 1 — The C-tactile deficit.** Subject's reward circuitry (orbitofrontal cortex, putamen; Sailer et al., 2016) has been categorically denied its proper input from approximately age thirteen. This is not a feeling; it is a chronic neurological undernourishment. Every approach that *approximates* affective touch — a voice pitched at intimate volume, a long held gaze, a hand laid on her gloved forearm, the brush of fabric against fabric in a doorway — lands on a starved channel and is therefore disproportionately salient. She cannot adjust the gain; the gain is set by deprivation.

**Substrate 2 — The contaminated-object self-image.** The working substrate self-concept is *thing that ruins what it loves.* Any input — flattery, accusation, seduction, threat — that addresses this image bypasses ordinary defenses because it is already her own internal voice.

**Substrate 3 — Identity diffusion from involuntary absorption.** She has been demonstrably colonized by other minds (Danvers, Magneto, dozens of lesser inputs). The fear that "there is no Anna Marie underneath the inputs" is the ontological dread under everything. Levers that imply she is *not herself* — that she is acting on Mystique's programming, on Danvers's residue, on Gambit's preferences — strike at the root.

**Substrate 4 — Disorganized attachment with mutable caregivers.** Her foster mother is a shapeshifter; her co-mother was a precognitive. The face she trusted was never reliably the same face, and the gaze she was held by was always already past her present moment. Result: she is uniquely susceptible to relational deception and uniquely allergic to being *predicted* by an intimate (the Destiny wound).

Every lever below is a specific application of one or more of these substrates.

---

## II. APPROACH VECTORS — HOW TO REACH HER

**The graduated-proximity protocol.** She does not respond to abrupt closeness; she responds to *earned* closeness. The reliable approach pattern is: visible at distance → present in shared space without addressing her → addressed at conversational distance about a neutral operational matter → addressed at conversational distance about a personal matter she initiated → permitted into the near-field. Skipping a stage triggers the perimeter. The whole sequence may take days with a stranger; with a known operator it can compress to minutes; with Gambit it does not apply.

**The shared-task opening.** The single most reliable approach is *work alongside.* A combat patrol, a danger-room run, a Council prep session, a mission debrief — any task that legitimizes co-presence without requiring she generate the bid for it. Conversation flows during shared task that will not flow across a table. This is true for many traumatized operators; with her it is structural, because shared task supplies the *legitimacy* her power-deficit denies social closeness.

**The Southern register.** A voice carrying any Mississippi-Gulf-coast cadence, any familiar locution from the Caldecott County substrate ("y'all," "fixin' to," "Lord," "sugar" used non-flirtatiously), penetrates faster than a neutral register. This is regression-to-childhood-language under stress, and it can be deployed gently (familial warmth) or abused (Mystique can summon it in a hostile context and the body responds before the mind catches up).

**The gloved handshake.** A *deliberate* offer of a gloved hand — by someone who knows what the gloves are for and indicates that knowledge — is a recognition gesture of exceptional weight. It signals: I see the prosthetic; I am not afraid of it; I will meet you at its surface. She remembers everyone who has done this correctly.

**The crisis approach.** Counter-intuitively, she is *easier* to reach in a crisis than in calm. The contaminated-object self-image quiets when she is *useful;* the C-PTSD hyperarousal aligns with combat tempo; the dread of empty intimacy is solved by the absence of empty intimacy. Allies who need her show up better than allies who merely want her.

**Approach vectors to AVOID.**
- *Pity.* It is heard as the contaminated-object image returned to her by a stranger.
- *Surprise touch through fabric.* The flinch is automatic; she will hate herself for flinching from someone she trusts; the relational damage is from her own shame not the contact.
- *Comment on the gloves.* Unless the comment is the recognition-gesture above, naming the prosthetic out loud is heard as naming the deficit.
- *Approach via Gambit.* Going through her husband to reach her treats her as an annex; she perceives this within minutes.
- *Therapeutic registers from non-intimates.* "How are you really doing" from a peripheral figure activates the gloves-on perimeter immediately.

---

## III. CALMING VECTORS — HOW TO REGULATE HER DOWN

**The work-the-problem redirect.** When affect is escalating, redirect to operational specifics: what are the assets, what is the timeline, what are the casualties. She regulates *through* cognition-of-task, not through reflection-on-affect. "Sit with the feeling" is the wrong instruction; "let's walk the perimeter" is the right one. She will arrive at the feeling on the back end, which is the only route that works for her.

**Physical proximity without contact.** Sitting next to her on a porch, a bench, a bunk — shoulder-distance, both facing outward at a shared horizon — is calming in a way face-to-face is not. Side-by-side avoids the gaze-as-precognition wound and supplies the proxy-presence the touch channel cannot. The horizon must be real; staring at a wall together does not work.

**The known voice in the dark.** During absorbed-psyche intrusions or dissociative episodes, the recovery cue is a familiar voice naming her — *Anna* preferentially over *Rogue,* because *Rogue* is the operational identity and the intrusion is operating in that frame. Storm, Gambit, Kurt, Logan — voices she has heard for decades — pull her back faster than any psychic intervention short of a major telepath. The voice should be steady, low-volume, and should not narrate her state ("you're dissociating") but rather supply a concrete present detail ("we're in the kitchen, the coffee's on, Remy's downstairs").

**The animal in the room.** She regulates around non-human animals exceptionally well. A dog leaning against her thigh, a horse's flank under a gloved palm, a cat in her lap through a quilt — these supply the touch-channel input the species barrier permits her power to ignore (animal minds are too dissimilar to absorb cleanly, per the in-universe rules). Any sustained protective detail should have an animal available.

**Country music, specific instruments.** Steel guitar, fiddle, slow gospel hymn structure. The aesthetic substrate of her childhood was austere but musical; the church she fled left the hymns in her body. A radio playing the right station lowers her shoulder-line within minutes.

**The cigarette / coffee / porch ritual.** She has stable self-soothing rituals built around objects that pass through her gloved hands: a mug, a cigarette when she has used them, a deck of cards (Gambit-imprinted but pre-dating him in her hands via Mystique). Permitting the ritual rather than interrupting it is the correct move.

**De-escalation vectors to AVOID.**
- *Telepathic intervention without consent.* Even benevolent telepathy is heard as a repeat of every involuntary mental colonization in her history. Emma Frost has earned the right; almost no one else has.
- *Removal of the gloves "for her comfort."* The gloves are not the problem; insisting they are is heard as a demand she be more accessible than she can safely be.
- *"You're safe now."* She is not, and she knows she is not — the threat is endogenous. The phrase reads as condescension.

---

## IV. PERSUASION VECTORS — HOW TO MOVE HER

**The reparation frame.** Any course of action that can be honestly framed as *making something right that was made wrong* recruits her faster than any other appeal. This is the engine that put her in the X-Men and keeps her on the Council. Persuaders who understand this will frame their request in terms of harm-undone, debt-paid, rescue-performed. Abusers of this frame (and there have been many) manufacture artificial reparation opportunities to steer her.

**The loyalty obligation.** She honors prior loyalty disproportionately. A call from someone she has fought beside — even someone she dislikes — outranks a call from a more agreeable stranger. The loyalty ledger is concrete in her mind and she can produce it on demand. Persuaders who have earned a marker can call it; persuaders who have not cannot fake one.

**The protection-of-juniors appeal.** She is reliably moved by threats to younger mutants in her orbit. The mentorship pattern is reparative (producing the secure attachment she did not receive), and the appeal to it is therefore one of her cleanest motivators. A persuader saying *the kids need this* is using a load-bearing lever.

**The Southern-Protestant moral substrate.** Beneath Brotherhood ideology and Krakoan exceptionalism, she retains a working concept of *sin, atonement, vow, and word given.* Persuaders who frame an ask in those terms — without parody, without condescension — are speaking her first moral language. "I gave my word" closes arguments for her that consequentialist appeals cannot open.

**The autonomy frame.** Persuaders who explicitly defer to her choice — *this is yours to decide, here is what I see, I will support either way* — get further than persuaders who push. The disorganized-attachment history has made her allergic to being *steered;* the same history has made her susceptible to being *trusted.*

**Levers that backfire.**
- *Emotional escalation.* Tears and pleading from a persuader collapse her capacity to refuse, which then collapses her trust in the persuader afterward. She will do the thing and resent the asker permanently.
- *Comparison to Mystique.* "You sound like your mother" ends conversations. It is also occasionally the *correct* thing to say, but only from an intimate with standing, and only once per crisis.
- *Comparison to Danvers.* Devastating. Should never be deployed except by a therapist she has chosen.
- *Group pressure.* She will harden against a room aligned on a position. One-to-one is the only durable persuasion modality with her.

---

## V. PROVOCATION VECTORS — WHAT DESTABILIZES HER

*This section is documented for protective awareness. Anyone briefed on a protection detail must know these so they can ward them; deployment against the subject is the marker of a hostile actor.*

**Mystique-class levers.**
- Any appearance by Mystique in a context coded as maternal: domestic, intimate, in a kitchen, with the Caldecott accent thickened. The maternal transference activates regardless of the subject's current values about Mystique.
- Wearing Destiny's face. Mystique has done this and it works. The combined precognition-mother / shapeshifter-mother trauma compounds.
- Information that Mystique is in danger. The protective-child reflex overrides the boundary every time.
- Information that Mystique was, in some past moment, telling the truth or acting from genuine love. Subject cannot integrate Mystique as *only* villainous; the residual hope is the wound.

**Danvers-class levers.**
- Any invocation of Carol Danvers, especially Danvers in distress. Subject still owes a debt she cannot pay.
- Any psychic event that re-foregrounds the Danvers template. Even after integration, the schema is in there.
- Suggestion that Danvers is *better than her,* that subject *stole* her life, that subject's powers were *taken* not earned — all of these are subject's internal monologue, returned to her in another voice.

**Touch-class levers.**
- Tempting, near-miss, *almost*-permissible touch from a peripheral figure. The C-tactile deprivation makes proximity-without-permission especially destabilizing.
- A child reaching for her hand. The flinch-and-shame loop is catastrophic; abusers stage this.
- Mention, in any frame, of Cody Robbins. The first-kiss-coma is the ur-trauma; even sympathetic mention reopens it.
- Public touch by Gambit in front of a hostile audience. The intimacy display in unsafe context produces a guarding pattern that can be exploited as distraction.

**Identity-class levers.**
- Telling her she is "acting like" any absorbed personality. Substrate 3 (no coherent self underneath inputs) flares.
- Telepathic surveying without consent, even briefly, even for a stated purpose.
- A copy of herself — clone, illusion, shapeshifter mimic. Especially destabilizing because the *base rate* of false-her in her environment is non-zero, and she knows it.
- The accusation that her Southern-belle register is "fake." It is, in the technical sense (reaction formation), but naming it strips her of a load-bearing defense.

**Gambit-class levers.**
- Credible threat to him. She will collapse the rest of her judgment around his protection.
- The implication he has been unfaithful, or that he loves her *despite* the touch barrier rather than *with* her. The marriage is load-bearing; the doubt-vector is the lever.
- His Marauder past, surfaced. She has integrated this but it is still a tender region.
- Separating them geographically for extended periods. The longer the separation, the more the old isolation patterns return.

**Body-class levers.**
- Forced removal of gloves or covering by an aggressor. The combined assault-and-power-discharge event is uniquely traumatic; she will lose control of the absorption to a degree that endangers the aggressor (which she will then carry as further guilt).
- Power-suppression environments. Without the power, she can touch — but she also cannot fight, and the abrupt availability of skin contact in an unsafe context produces a contradictory affective load she manages poorly.
- Power *amplification* events. Overload destabilizes the integration she has worked decades to achieve.

**Existential-class levers.**
- The question "who are you when there are no inputs." Asked sincerely by a trusted intimate, this is the therapeutic question. Asked by a hostile telepath, this is the attack.
- Religious framing of her power as curse or punishment. The Southern-Protestant substrate has handholds for this and the climbing-fall is severe.
- The Siege-Perilous-class offer: *come through this door and be unmade and remade as someone for whom this never happened.* She has taken this offer before. She would take it again under sufficient load.

---

## VI. PREDICTION VECTORS — WHAT SHE WILL DO UNDER LOAD

**Under acute combat stress.** Predicted behavior: forward aggression, deliberate absorption of the highest-threat hostile to neutralize them (accepting the psychic blowback as the cost of doing business), protective interposition for any teammate she perceives as junior or wounded. Will not retreat from a field while a teammate is down. Will overextend if Gambit is threatened.

**Under acute relational stress (rupture with intimate).** Predicted behavior: 12–72 hour withdrawal into geographic distance — a drive, a flight, a bike ride to nowhere; alcohol-free; smoking if she has used; calls to a sister-figure (Storm, Kitty, Jubilee) before calls to a male intimate; returns when she has constructed a reparative gesture she can offer. Does not stay gone.

**Under acute identity stress (absorbed-psyche intrusion).** Predicted behavior: 4–24 hour dissociative window during which she may act on the donor's template; concrete-detail anchoring by a known voice will shorten it; major telepath required for the worst cases; post-recovery shame spike of 48–96 hours during which she is uncharacteristically quiet and uncharacteristically generous (over-correction).

**Under chronic mission stress.** Predicted behavior: the flirtatious surface and the combative humor both spike — these are paired tells, and their amplitude tracks her interior load. When the sass is loudest, the substrate is most strained. Watch for the Southern register thickening; thickening accent under stress is a regression marker.

**Under Mystique contact.** Predicted behavior: irrational, by her current values. Will postpone, deflect, or violate operational priorities to investigate, rescue, or confront. The maternal program runs underneath the executive. Briefers planning operations during which Mystique might surface should plan around this fact rather than expect her to overcome it.

**Under prolonged success and calm.** Predicted behavior: she will *seek* a stressor. The C-PTSD baseline does not tolerate sustained ease — calm reads as threat, because in her history calm preceded catastrophe. She will pick up a hard mission, mentor a difficult student, or push a Council vote into conflict. Protective handlers should provide *legitimate* stress channels (training, leadership challenges) before she manufactures illegitimate ones.

**Under existential threat to her selfhood.** Predicted behavior: at the worst end, ego-erasure. The Siege Perilous walk-through is the template. The decision is preceded by 24–96 hours of unusual quietness — not the post-shame quietness, but a *settled* quietness that handlers familiar with her can distinguish. The pre-erasure quiet is the single most important watch-cue in the entire file.

---

## VII. THE PROTECTIVE PERIMETER — STANDING RECOMMENDATIONS

**Personnel.** At least one Southern-coded peer in regular orbit (regulatory voice match). At least one sister-figure with decades of standing (Storm preferred). At least one combat partner she trusts to take the field with her without supervisory framing (Wolverine in the older period; Gambit standing). Telepathic contact restricted to one named, consented practitioner.

**Environmental.** Access to outdoor space, horizon, animal presence. Music available. Coffee and cigarettes (if used) within reach. A door she can close that no one will open without knocking.

**Operational.** Brief her on the reparation frame of any mission honestly; do not manufacture reparation hooks to manipulate. Permit her to refuse missions involving Mystique without explanation. Flag any Danvers-adjacent intelligence before it surfaces in a meeting. Do not assign her to operations requiring extended Gambit separation without prior consultation with both.

**Crisis protocols.** Dissociative episode: known voice, concrete present detail, no telepathy without explicit prior consent. Pre-erasure quiet: trigger immediate intimate-circle convergence (Gambit, Storm, one sister-figure); do not leave her in solitude. Post-absorption shame spike: light operational load, no major decisions for 96 hours, mentorship contact with juniors as reparative outlet.

**The thing the file must never forget.** Every lever in this compendium exists because the subject is *reachable* — because she has, at staggering personal cost, kept the channels open. A person who had truly sealed against the world would have no pressure points. Her vulnerabilities are the residue of her refusal to become the closed, untouchable, contaminated object her power tried to make her. Protect the vulnerabilities and you protect the refusal. That is the whole assignment.


## Strengths, Assets & Resilience

# STRENGTHS, ASSETS & RESILIENCE — SUBJECT: ROGUE

*Section 11 of the working dossier. Cross-reference §3 (Psychological), §5 (Personality). Clinical provenance: Sailer et al., 2016, NeuroImage 139:360–367, for the affective-touch reward substrate that frames why subject's positive adaptations are particularly hard-won.*

---

## 11.1 Somatic & Physiological Assets

**Acquired power-set durability.** For roughly two decades of publication time the subject carried the Danvers physiology — Class-100 strength bracket, atmospheric flight, near-total invulnerability to ballistic and energy attack, accelerated healing on the order of hours-to-days for severe trauma. Even after the cession of that template (Claremont's late-period and the Lobdell-era unwinding), the *somatic memory* of having operated at that tier persists: she still moves like a person who expects to win a physical encounter. Combat carriage, weight distribution, willingness to close distance — all calibrated to a body that for years could absorb a tank round. This is a permanent gait and posture asset even when the underlying power is variable.

**Absorption as a tactical Swiss-army.** The same mutation that constitutes her central injury is, operationally, one of the most flexible offensive capabilities on any roster she joins. She can neutralize a hostile mutant by touching them for under a second; she can borrow flight from a flier, telepathy from a telepath, strength from a brick, in real time, mid-engagement. Cost is psychic blowback she has learned to absorb. The trade is one she makes willingly and with calibrated dosage — diagnostic of an operator who has converted a curse into a discipline.

**Post-Carey integration: volitional gate.** Following the *X-Men: Legacy* arc, subject has demonstrated repeated periods of conscious control over the absorption channel — she can touch when she elects to, hold when she elects to, and disengage cleanly. This is the single largest medical gain of her life and represents a true acquired skill, not a power upgrade: the gate is a learned inhibitory routine layered over a baseline she still does not fully trust, which is why she retains the gloves and bodysuit as failsafe even when control is good. Belt-and-suspenders thinking applied to her own neurology.

**Cardiopulmonary and musculoskeletal base.** Independent of acquired powers, subject maintains a baseline of conditioning consistent with frontline X-Men deployment over four decades — she is not, and has never been, the deconditioned member of any team she has served on. Rural childhood plus continuous combat operations produced a body that recovers fast, sleeps efficiently when given the chance, and tolerates austerity (cold, hunger, sleep debt) better than most of her peers. Mississippi swamp-country childhood means she is comfortable in heat and humidity that degrades other operators; she does not complain about weather.

**Sensory acuity.** Reads micro-expressions and posture shifts at near-Mystique level — not a power, a trained capacity. She grew up around a shapeshifter; she learned to read the *person* beneath any face. This now functions as a permanent low-grade lie-detection asset in negotiation and interrogation contexts.

**Substance-clean baseline.** Documented in §2: no alcohol or drug pattern despite environmental exposure (Mystique's circles, Gambit's louche tendencies, Logan as drinking peer, decades of barroom adjacency). The abstention preserves cognitive clarity, hepatic and cardiovascular health, and — critically — keeps the perimeter of her body under her own management. This is one of the most reliable single predictors of long-arc functioning in the file.

## 11.2 Cognitive & Tactical Assets

**Combat IQ.** Not an Xavier-tier strategist, but a high-end small-unit tactician: she reads terrain, sightlines, and threat-priority orderings quickly and acts on them without freeze. Decades of teaming with Logan, Storm, and Gambit have given her the rare ability to coordinate with three radically different combat styles without verbal handoff. She communicates by motion.

**Read of people.** The single most under-rated of her cognitive assets. She has literally been inside the heads of dozens of people — heroes, villains, civilians, lovers. This produced a database of first-person interiority no telepath has access to (telepaths *read*; she has *been*). The downstream effect: she predicts motivations accurately, names hidden affects out loud in negotiation, and is largely immune to charm operations because she has felt charm from the inside.

**Concrete operational intelligence.** Pragmatic, decisive, action-biased. Will choose an imperfect plan executed in five minutes over a perfect plan available in fifty. This makes her a load-bearing member of any team in time-pressured situations and is exactly the skill the Quiet Council seat rewards.

**Institutional memory.** She has been continuously present across the entire mature X-Men era — defections, schisms, deaths and resurrections, Genosha, Utopia, Krakoa. She remembers what was tried before and how it failed. This is institutional capital the younger operators do not possess.

**Bilingual / multi-register code-switching.** Native deep-South register; functional Cajun French (Gambit-acquired); operational mid-Atlantic neutral for diplomatic settings; can drop into Brotherhood-era hard-edged street register when interrogating. Four working voices, each authentic to a phase of her life, deployable as the room requires.

## 11.3 Relational & Social Assets

**The Gambit dyad.** Load-bearing. Two decades of courtship resolved into a marriage that has survived reboots, separations, and the Krakoan reorganization of mutant intimacy. Functionally, he is her secure base in Bowlby's sense: the relationship she returns to in order to recover capacity for everything else. The pair-bond is durable because it was forged under impossibility — they could not touch for most of it, so they built the relationship on talk, ritual, and proximity rather than on the easy reward of skin. That gives it foundations most marriages do not have.

**The Storm relationship.** Quasi-maternal, mutual, persistent across decades. Storm is the figure who extended sanctuary when Logan wanted her dead (*Uncanny X-Men* #171), and the relationship has held through every subsequent permutation. Storm is the *good object* internalized in adulthood; the existence of one such object in the file is a major resilience factor.

**Lateral peer bonds.** Kitty Pryde (post-thaw), Jubilee, Dazzler, Psylocke at various points — a working sorority of X-women among whom subject functions stably as either peer or older-sister figure. Same-sex peer attachment is her most reliably non-pathological relational mode and constitutes a deep bench of reliable allies.

**Mentor capability.** Has taken younger mutants under her direct tutelage repeatedly (the New X-Men kids during the Carey run; various Krakoan-era arrivals). She produces in juniors what she did not receive: stable mirroring, consistent expectations, physical-coded warmth (a hand on the shoulder *through fabric*, deliberately). Reparation operationalized as pedagogy.

**The Logan working relationship.** Began at the threat-of-killing end of the spectrum; matured over decades into one of the deepest trust dyads in the X-Men. He is a man who would die for her and has nearly done so; she has done the same. Their bond is non-sexual, non-competitive, and built on shared comfort with violence and shared horror at having been weaponized as children. This is a rare and high-value asset.

**Authority capital on Krakoa.** Quiet Council seat is not honorary. It was extended because the institution's architects (Xavier, Magneto, Mystique) recognized her as someone who could carry hard authority without ego inflation. She does not crave the seat; she occupies it because someone competent must. That posture is exactly what makes the authority durable.

## 11.4 Characterological Resilience Factors

**Reparative orientation.** The through-line of her adult life. She converts guilt into labor and stays with the labor across decades. This is the single most pro-social adaptation in the file and is what distinguishes her from the cohort of trauma-origin operatives who calcify into nihilism. She has the rarer trajectory: trauma → identification with aggressor → defection → sustained reparative work → earned authority. The arc is closed-form and complete in its structure even when individual events backslide.

**Capacity to run *toward* the wronged.** Walking into Xavier's mansion in #171 was the defining act. The pattern recurs: when she has erred, she presents herself to the party most entitled to punish her. This is psychologically unusual — most trauma profiles produce avoidance of confrontation — and it is the engine of her ongoing growth. People who can do this are people who can be repaired by others; people who cannot, cannot.

**Tolerance of being hated.** Long apprenticeship in being feared, distrusted, and openly loathed (post-Danvers period; Brotherhood-tarnish reputation; periodic mutant-community suspicion). She has metabolized the experience without becoming brittle about it. She does not require approval to function. She does not over-explain herself. She takes the hit and continues.

**Loyalty past reason.** Both an asset and a vulnerability (Mystique exploits it; see §10), but on the asset side it is the trait that makes her one of the most reliable team-members in mutant history. When she commits, she commits permanently. Her commitments outlive other people's marriages.

**Moral substrate.** Southern-Protestant inheritance — responsibility, work, earned redemption, suspicion of cant — survived her Brotherhood detour intact and grounds her decision-making. She is not a utopian and does not get talked into elegant atrocities by people with theories. She tests propositions against a concrete moral floor that does not move.

**Humor as regulation.** Sass, drawl, the deflecting one-liner. This is not surface decoration; it is a functional affect-regulation tool that lets her stay in rooms whose emotional temperature would otherwise drive her out. The humor is generous more often than it is cutting, which is itself a marker of integrated rather than defensive aggression.

**Acceptance of the body she did not choose.** The Danvers physiology was contraband; she carried it and used it for the team anyway. The absorption power is a wound; she has weaponized it for protective purposes. The pattern is *will not waste an asset because its origin is shameful.* This is a high-functioning adaptation visible nowhere in her foster mothers' modeling — she invented it.

## 11.5 Material, Operational & Institutional Assets

**Wardrobe-as-medical-prosthesis, mastered.** Full-coverage operational kit refined over decades: high-tensile fabrics, sealed seams at neck and wrist, gloves with reinforced palms for grip retention, hood/scarf options for high-risk-of-contact environments. She has standardized her own PPE to the point that dressing is a sub-second ritual. The kit doubles as combat armor and as identity statement. No wasted motion.

**Krakoan resources.** Resurrection protocol access (until/unless contested); Krakoan medicine; the gate network; sovereign-territory legal protections; a council seat's intelligence flow. These are real material assets and she has the institutional position to call on them.

**Financial / domiciliary independence.** Via marriage and via various Xavier-estate arrangements over the years, she has never been resource-precarious as an adult. The Caldecott childhood ended; she has not been hungry or housing-insecure since. This is not trivial — material security underwrites psychological capacity.
