**Network reach.** Brotherhood-era contacts (kept warm via Mystique even when subject is estranged from her); thieves' guild access via Gambit; full X-Men institutional network; Avengers-adjacent relationships from various team-ups; Magneto-era political contacts. Few operators have her breadth of warm contacts across mutant factional lines.

**Combat-ready domestic geography.** She has lived in: Caldecott, the Xavier mansion (multiple incarnations), Australia, Muir Island, Genosha, Westchester, San Francisco, Utopia, the Jean Grey School, Krakoa, New Orleans (Gambit's family seat). Each location is a fallback she could return to under operational stress. She has more potential safe-houses than most operators have addresses.

## 11.6 Resilience Mechanisms (Process-Level)

**Sleep hygiene under duress.** Documented across the record: she sleeps when she can, where she can, deeply. This is a frontline-soldier trait and a major endogenous resilience factor. Disturbed sleep is one of the leading predictors of PTSD decompensation; she protects sleep instinctively.

**Geographic flight as *controlled* withdrawal, not collapse.** When she leaves a team, she does not disappear into substance use or self-harm; she travels, works, sometimes solo-operates, and comes back. The "Rogue leaves" beat is a regulation strategy, not a decompensation. She uses distance to recover capacity. The fact that she always returns is the asset.

**Use of ritualized near-touch as substitute reward.** The hand-on-shoulder-through-fabric, the leaning-against, the elaborate flirtation games with Gambit during the no-touch years — these are *constructed* substitutes for the affective-touch channel she is denied (Sailer et al., 2016). The construction itself is the asset. She built a workaround for a missing reward circuit. Most people in her position would not.

**Conversion of intrusive psyches into useful information.** The absorbed personalities are a wound, but she has also learned to *consult* the residue — to ask, in effect, what would this person know about this situation. This is an integration move, not a dissociative one, and it represents a substantial post-Carey gain.

**Tolerance of ambiguity in identity.** She has lived for years not fully knowing which thoughts were hers, which were Danvers, which were absorbed in the last engagement. She has stabilized a functional self anyway. The capacity to operate at high level under chronic identity ambiguity is rare and is itself a hard-won asset.

**Reality-testing preserved across all decompensations.** Even during the Danvers takeover, even during Magneto-power-blowback madness, her reality testing returned cleanly with appropriate intervention. She does not become permanently psychotic; she does not retreat into fixed delusion. The substrate is sturdy.

## 11.7 Meta-Assets (What Makes the Other Assets Durable)

**She has built a *life*, not a posture.** Marriage, council seat, mentees, residences, working relationships across factions, a body she has learned to gate. This is not a person held together by mission-tempo and adrenaline; this is a person with infrastructure. Take away the costume and there is still someone there. Many operators in the file cannot say this.

**She knows the wound is not closed and does not pretend otherwise.** Insight is preserved. She does not require the file to flatter her; she would recognize this assessment as roughly accurate. Subjects with accurate self-models are dramatically more resilient than subjects with defended ones.

**She is teachable.** The Carey-era control gains required her to accept instruction, tolerate failure, and revise long-standing protective habits. She did it. A subject in her sixties of in-universe time who can still learn at that depth is a subject whose assets will continue to compound.

**She has converted the worst single fact about her existence — categorical denial of the affective-touch reward channel — into the engine of her most valuable traits: the over-developed read of people, the constructed substitute rituals, the reparative orientation, the loyalty past reason, the humor that keeps people in the room with her. The injury and the asset ledger are the same document read from opposite ends.** This is the deepest finding of the section and the one that should govern any operational use of this file: she is durable *because of* the wound, not despite it. Remove the wound and you would not get a healthier subject; you would get a different and less capable one. The work the file should support is not cure. It is the continuation of an adaptation that is, by any reasonable clinical measure, already one of the more successful in the mutant cohort.

---
*End §11. See §12 for the corresponding vulnerability ledger; the two sections are designed to be read against each other.*


## Failure Modes & Decompensation

# FAILURE MODES & DECOMPENSATION — SUBJECT: ROGUE

## 0. Frame

Subject does not fail catastrophically often, and this is itself the most important diagnostic fact about her failure modes. She has been operational, with intervals, across roughly forty years of in-universe time, through ideological reversals, mass-casualty events, three confirmed losses of her primary power-set, two confirmed losses of her primary romantic attachment, and at least one fully successful psychic colonization of her ego by a foreign personality (Danvers, *Uncanny X-Men* #269). The system is therefore *robust under load* — but the failure surface, when reached, is unusually structured and unusually predictable. What follows is the topology of that surface.

Three discriminable collapse pathways are visible in the canon. They are not mutually exclusive; under maximum load they cascade.

- **Pathway A — Acute Absorption Collapse** (exogenous psyche overwhelms ego boundary).
- **Pathway B — Chronic Attachment Collapse** (touch-deprivation reward-deficit plus relational rupture produces depressive withdrawal, sometimes culminating in volitional self-erasure).
- **Pathway C — Maternal-Transference Collapse** (Mystique re-enters operational range; subject's current value-set is overridden by the older identification).

Each has a characteristic prodrome, escalation curve, terminal state, and recovery requirement. Each has been observed multiple times in the published record. The file treats them sequentially and then maps their interactions.

---

## 1. Pathway A — Acute Absorption Collapse

**Mechanism.** Subject takes a contact of unusual depth, duration, or psychic mass — a high-tier mutant (Magneto, *X-Men* #25), an unstable or already-fragmenting psyche (Danvers post-Brood, the cumulative residue across the early Claremont period), or multiple inputs in close succession (combat absorptions stacked). The donor template does not stay walled off in the standard "consult and discard" mode subject has trained for. It begins to interpret incoming sensory data through its own schemata, then to *initiate behavior* through subject's body.

**Prodrome (hours to days).** Pronouns slip first. She refers to herself in compound form, or catches herself using the donor's idiom — Danvers's military cadence, Magneto's Mitteleuropan vowel placement, in extreme cases the donor's primary language displacing her own English. Handedness can shift if the donor was opposite-dominant. Posture re-templates: she stands differently, occupies space differently, holds a weapon she has never been trained on competently. Sleep architecture fragments; she reports dreams that are not metaphorically but *literally* the donor's memories replayed in first person. Affect flattens or, more diagnostically, *takes on a tonality that is not hers* — Danvers's anger has a different shape than her own, colder, more procedural, and teammates who know her well (Storm, Logan, eventually Gambit) clock it before she does.

**Escalation.** Hyperarousal as the ego fights for primacy: insomnia, irritability, sudden tactical errors out of character. She begins isolating — locks doors she usually leaves open, takes long flights alone (the Danvers powerset facilitating an escape route the average decompensating patient does not have). Verbal output becomes either compressed and clipped (donor-dominant) or florid and accent-heavy (her own surface defenses spiking compensatorily, the reaction-formation working overtime). The two registers can alternate sentence by sentence. By the time third parties intervene, she has often already had hours of internal split she did not report.

**Terminal state.** Full displacement. The donor is in the driver's seat; subject is a passenger, sometimes aware, sometimes not. The Danvers takeover in *Uncanny X-Men* #269 is the type specimen: she flies to the Australian outback (Danvers-coded geography of resentment), engages prior Danvers enemies, and identifies categorically as Carol. The "Rogue" component is reachable only by external psychic intervention — historically Magneto, Xavier, Jean, Emma, or a sufficiently strong telepathic ally — and recovery requires the donor template to be *extracted or quarantined,* not merely talked down. Talking down does not work because the entity being talked to is not the patient.

**Recovery requirement.** Telepathic triage at minimum; in severe cases, a constructed psychic environment (the Siege Perilous remains the most extreme version — full ego-rebuild from constituent fragments, *Uncanny X-Men* #247, with the addendum that subject elected that procedure herself, see Pathway B). Recovery is rarely complete: residue persists. The Danvers powerset stayed with her for nearly two hundred issues after the personality itself was excised; the somatic memory of an absorbed psyche is longer than the cognitive memory of it.

**Behavioral tells visible from the outside before she can name the problem herself:**

- She stops touching teammates through clothing — even the safe contact she normally allows (a hand on a shoulder, a hip-check in the kitchen, the gloved squeezes she gives Kitty or Jubilee). The body knows the boundary is failing and over-corrects.
- She over-checks her own reflection. Mystique's daughter watching the mirror for someone else's face.
- She eats food she does not like. Donor preferences leaking through autonomic systems.
- She refuses telepathic contact she would normally accept. The displaced ego protecting the displacement.

---

## 2. Pathway B — Chronic Attachment Collapse

**Mechanism.** The somatic substrate identified in clinical_provenance (Sailer et al., 2016) is the engine here. C-tactile afferent input — the orbitofrontal/putamen reward channel served by slow, gentle, skin-to-skin contact — has been categorically offline for subject since approximately age thirteen. This is not a metaphor for loneliness; it is a chronic deficit in a specific reward circuit, with the predictable downstream effects: anhedonic baseline, heightened salience of any approximated substitute, and a constant low-grade signal that the file is justified in calling *social pain* in the affective-neuroscience sense. Subject runs on this deficit at all times. She compensates with verbal warmth, ritualized near-touch (the Gambit choreography), combat-contact through fabric, and the mentorship behaviors that produce vicarious bonding. The compensations work — until a relational rupture removes one of them.

**Triggering events in the canon.** Cody's coma persisting (*Uncanny X-Men* #182 ff.). The Antarctic abandonment of Gambit (*X-Men* #45). Mystique's serial betrayals. Destiny's death and its long aftermath. The temporary loss of Gambit during various crossover deaths. The Krakoan-era complications around the marriage. Any event that removes a compensatory channel without replacing it.

**Prodrome (weeks).** Withdrawal of the surface charm first — this is the single most reliable early warning. The accent thins. The "sugah" register drops out of address. Conversations get shorter. Replies become factual where they used to be flirted. Teammates who know her read this immediately as a red flag; teammates who do not know her well misread it as her becoming "more serious" or "more professional," which can delay intervention by weeks.

Then the geography starts. She takes longer patrols, volunteers for solo recon, accepts assignments far from the mansion/Krakoa/whichever current base. She does not announce a departure; she simply begins to be elsewhere by default. Across decades this is the most repeated behavioral pattern in her file: *under chronic stress, she translates emotional distance into physical distance.* The flight pattern is so reliable it could be plotted on a map — she goes to places associated with prior stability (Mississippi, the Australian site, anywhere Storm has been) or to places sufficiently remote that no one will see her decline.

**Escalation.** Anhedonic deepening. She stops eating regularly — not anorexic in the body-image sense, simply uninterested. Sleep extends or fragments. The combat-contact-through-fabric compensations escalate: she will take hits she does not need to take, position herself in melee where she does not need to be, *because the impact through cloth is the closest thing to touch available.* This is one of the file's grimmer findings — her combat aggression spikes downward into a depressive register where the violence is not anger but a substitute for the missing reward channel. The body seeking input by any available route.

Verbal flirtation may paradoxically *increase* in this phase, but the quality changes: it becomes mechanical, performed at people she has no actual interest in, a defense rather than an engagement. Observers who know her well report it feels "hollow" or "off" — the surface defense running without the underlying engine.

**Terminal state.** One of two endpoints. The common endpoint is extended geographic withdrawal — months or longer off-team, often with a single trusted contact maintained (historically Storm; in the modern era, Gambit). She returns when the deficit has been partially restored by solitude plus distance from the triggering rupture. This is *adaptive collapse:* the system shuts down the load-bearing structures temporarily and reboots.

The rarer endpoint is the volitional ego-erasure pathway. *Uncanny X-Men* #247 — the Siege Perilous — is the case in chief: subject walked through a device that would dissolve her self and rebuild it from scratch, fully aware of what she was doing. The file classifies this as a suicidal-equivalent act. Not suicide — she did not seek the death of the body — but she sought the death of the self that was carrying the load, which is the same act with a different mechanism. This endpoint is rare precisely because subject has built so many compensations, but it is *available to her in a way it is not available to most patients,* because devices, telepaths, and reality-altering allies exist in her operational environment. The threshold to elective dissolution is structurally lower for her than for a civilian. The file flags this as a permanent vulnerability.

**Recovery requirement.** Restoration of a compensatory channel. Historically this has been: Storm's sustained presence; the slow Gambit courtship (with its near-touch ritual functioning as partial substitute for the missing input); the Carey-era power integration arc that permitted actual skin contact and produced the largest sustained mood elevation in her recorded history; the Gambit marriage as load-bearing stabilizer. The recovery is *channel-specific:* talking does not repair a tactile-channel deficit. What works is the partial restoration of touch (or its closest approximation), or the introduction of a new bonding modality dense enough to compete (mentorship, command authority, ritualized physical co-presence). Cognitive intervention alone is insufficient. This is the single most important treatment-planning fact in the file.

---

## 3. Pathway C — Maternal-Transference Collapse

**Mechanism.** Mystique enters effective range, physically or via proxy. Subject's current value-set, command position, and adult identifications begin to lose primacy to the older identification with the foster mother. This is not seduction in the manipulative sense — it is the activation of a developmentally prior attachment structure that has never been fully resolved because the object (Mystique) has never been either lost (she keeps surviving) or repaired (she keeps betraying). The transference is permanent and exploitable, and Mystique has exploited it across every era of the publication record.

**Prodrome.** Subject defends Mystique in conversation where she would normally not. She volunteers Mystique's perspective unprompted. She becomes touchy about third-party criticism of Mystique in a way that does not match her stated current position on Mystique's politics or methods. Sleep dreams shift toward childhood content. Accent thickens (regression marker). She becomes more religious in idiom — the Mississippi Protestant substrate Mystique never fully erased reasserts under regression load.

**Escalation.** Operational compromises start small: an omission in a report, a tactical choice that incidentally serves a Mystique interest, a meeting taken that should not have been taken. She rationalizes each in isolation. The pattern is visible only in aggregate, and is visible *to her* only when a third party with standing (Storm, Gambit, Logan in earlier eras) names it directly. Even then she resists naming because the alternative is mourning, and the mourning has been deferred for forty years.

**Terminal state.** Action against current allegiance. Historically this has taken the form of mission failures whose downstream beneficiary is Mystique, intelligence leaks of the soft kind (Mystique knew because Rogue would inevitably tell her), and in extreme cases active assistance to Mystique operations against the X-Men. The terminal state is recoverable — subject has always come back — but each iteration leaves residue. She trusts herself less around Mystique each time, which paradoxically makes her *more* vulnerable to the next approach because the self-mistrust eats the compensatory vigilance.

**Recovery requirement.** Physical separation from Mystique plus mourning work that has never been completed. The file's prediction is that this pathway will not fully close in subject's lifetime. Destiny's resurrection in the Krakoan era complicates rather than resolves it.

---

## 4. Cascade dynamics

The pathways interact. A Pathway B chronic deficit lowers the threshold for Pathway A acute absorption (a depleted ego cannot fight off an incoming donor template as effectively). A Pathway C maternal-transference episode generates a Pathway B rupture when subject realizes she has been used (the resulting shame and loss of self-trust deepen the chronic deficit). Pathway A residue (an absorbed personality whose values she now half-shares) can be the mechanism by which Pathway C is initiated (Mystique knows which absorbed templates to invoke).

The worst-case scenario — and the one a surveillance file must explicitly map — is a coincident Pathway B and Pathway C event with an opportunity for Pathway A absorption. Concretely: she has just lost a primary attachment (Gambit unreachable, Storm distant), Mystique appears in a posture of apparent repair, and a high-mass psyche becomes available for contact (Mystique herself, in fact, or a teammate Mystique steers into proximity). In that configuration, all three failure modes are active simultaneously. The published record has approached this configuration more than once. It has not yet realized it fully. The file's assessment is that it would produce her most severe decompensation to date and would require the heaviest external intervention on record to recover from.

---

## 5. What collapse does *not* look like

A surveillance file is as useful for ruling out as for ruling in. Subject does not collapse via:

- **Substance use.** The absence is structural — she does not let exogenous substances breach a perimeter she already cannot trust. Do not look for her in bars, do not expect a relapse vector, do not waste resources on toxicology.
- **Promiscuity or sexual acting-out.** Foreclosed physiologically for most of her life; temperamentally absent even when (Carey era, post-marriage) it became possible. The flirtatious surface is reaction-formation, not appetite.
- **Outward violence against the innocent.** Even under Pathway A displacement, the donor templates that take over are not categorically homicidal toward bystanders. Danvers-as-Rogue fought prior Danvers enemies, not civilians. Magneto's intrusion (*X-Men* #25) produced ideologically targeted hostility, not random harm. Her decompensations are inward-pointed.
- **Suicidal action in the conventional sense.** She has never sought the death of her body. She has sought the death of her *self* (Siege Perilous) and the dissolution of her *identity* (the various reboots she has accepted). The distinction matters operationally — a body-watch would miss her actual risk vector.
- **Manic episodes, psychotic breaks of endogenous origin, autonomous mood disturbance.** Mood tracks triggers; dysregulation is reactive, not autonomous. A clinician expecting bipolar architecture will misread her.

---

## 6. Early warning signature, consolidated

For an observer with access — teammate, telepath, surveillance — the earliest reliable signals across all three pathways, ranked by sensitivity:

1. **Drop in the surface accent register.** The "sugah" and the Southern-belle cadence are the load-bearing reaction-formation. When they thin, the engine underneath is failing. This precedes every other observable by days to weeks.
2. **Withdrawal of safe gloved touch.** She stops the hand-on-shoulder, the hip-check, the small fabric-mediated contacts she normally distributes generously. The body is policing a boundary it senses is becoming porous.
3. **Geographic drift.** Patrols extend, solo assignments accepted preferentially, presence at communal meals declines.
4. **Pronoun slippage or idiom intrusion** (Pathway A specific). The donor is speaking.
5. **Defense of Mystique in contexts not requiring it** (Pathway C specific).
6. **Combat over-engagement with degraded tactical judgment.** She takes hits she does not need; she stays in melee past the optimal disengagement point. The body seeking input.
7. **Increase in flirtatious verbal output with degraded quality.** Performance without engagement. The defense running on autopilot.
8. **Refusal of telepathic contact she would normally accept.** Late signal; by this point she is already significantly displaced or significantly depleted.

---

## 7. Conditions that produce collapse

To close the topology — the conditions, in approximate order of pathogenicity:

- Mystique in operational range with apparent good faith. Maximum pathogenicity. Hits Pathways B and C simultaneously and creates Pathway A opportunity.
- Loss or unavailability of Gambit (current marriage being the load-bearing relational structure). High pathogenicity. Pathway B.
- Sustained command load without compensatory contact (the Krakoan Quiet Council role, structurally). Moderate pathogenicity, chronic — slow erosion rather than acute collapse.
- Forced high-mass absorption (combat necessity requiring her to touch a powerful or unstable mutant). Acute Pathway A risk.
- Any cue invoking the Danvers act in a context where reparation is unavailable. Spikes the chronic guilt substrate. Contributes to Pathway B drift.
- Any cue invoking the Cody event. Same mechanism, different index trauma.
- Being told, by anyone with standing, that she is "like" an absorbed personality, or that there is no coherent self underneath her inputs. This is the deepest fear in the file and the most precise destabilizer; an adversary who knew her well could collapse her with it.
- Touch-related taunts or temptations from an adversary skilled enough to make the offer credible. Engages the biological deficit directly. The longing is not under volitional control.

---

## 8. Closing observation

The collapse architecture is symmetrical with the strength architecture. The same features that produce her durability — the channeled compensations, the rituals, the chosen authority structures, the marriage, the command role, the mentorship — are precisely the features whose individual failure constitutes her collapse pathways. She is not fragile; she is *load-distributed,* across a small number of load-bearing structures, each of which is real and each of which can fail. The file's central operational note is that her resilience is high but her redundancy is low. Lose Gambit, lose Storm, put Mystique in the room, and the system that has held for forty years is in its narrowest configuration. Plan accordingly.


## Trajectory & Forward Assessment

# TRAJECTORY & FORWARD ASSESSMENT — SUBJECT: ROGUE

*Section compiled as forward projection from the longitudinal file. Probabilistic, not deterministic. Fork points flagged. Indicators given so the file can be updated in real time.*

---

## 1. THE CURRENT VECTOR (BASELINE FROM WHICH WE PROJECT)

Subject enters this forecast window in the most integrated state of her recorded life. Three structural facts define the baseline:

1. **Power-control is functionally established but not metaphysically secure.** She can touch by choice in most operational conditions. The mechanism — partly Carey-era integration of the Ms. Marvel template, partly subsequent reboots, partly marriage-era consolidation — is not load-tested against catastrophic stressors (Apocalypse-tier psychic assault, prolonged unconsciousness, brain trauma, depowering events, resurrection-protocol artifacts). The control is a behavior, not a guarantee.
2. **The marriage to Gambit is the load-bearing relational structure.** It is also, in attachment terms, a *single point of failure*. Subject has built her late-period equilibrium on one dyad. This is a stable arrangement and a fragile one simultaneously.
3. **She has accepted institutional authority** — Quiet Council, X-Men team leadership in the post-Krakoan reshuffle. This is a phase change. For most of her life she was a soldier or a refugee inside someone else's structure; she is now structure-making. The reparation engine has found its highest-output configuration: she is *useful at scale.*

From here, several trajectories are plausible. They are not mutually exclusive; she will probably traverse two or three of them in sequence.

---

## 2. THE HIGH-PROBABILITY TRAJECTORIES (next 10 years of in-universe time)

### 2a. Continued consolidation as institutional leader

Most probable single path. She stays in command roles. The flirtatious surface contracts into a leadership idiom — still warm, still Southern-coded, but increasingly deployed as a *managerial instrument* rather than a defense. She develops, in this branch, a recognizable command voice: brisk in the briefing room, gentler one-on-one, allergic to grand strategic abstraction, lethal to anyone who mistakes the courtesy for softness. Her cabinet relationships stabilize around a small number of trusted lieutenants (Storm functionally permanent; Kurt as conscience; one or two younger operators she has mentored from intake).

Predictable failure modes inside this branch: she will under-delegate emotional labor, take personal responsibility for casualties at a rate that is not sustainable, and burn through her own reserves quietly because the Southern-Protestant moral substrate does not give her permission to be tired. She will not say she is tired. The somatic tell will be earlier — sleep degradation, a return of the migraine pattern that flares around heavy psychic exposure, a slight uptick in the involuntary glove-checking gesture even when bare-handed contact is currently safe.

### 2b. Mentorship pipeline becomes the primary identity

Adjacent branch. As younger mutants (touch-affected, trauma-affected, Brotherhood-defector profile) come through the institution, she will increasingly find her center of gravity in *being the adult someone like her needed.* This is the highest-yield use of her history. It also runs the risk of over-identification — she will pick favorites whose pathology resembles hers and will be slow to set limits with them, because the limit-setting feels like the abandonment she experienced.

Indicator that this branch is dominant: she begins to ask, unprompted, after specific juniors by name in operations briefings. Counter-indicator: she avoids the intake interviews and lets others do them. The latter would suggest the mentorship pull is being suppressed because it is too costly emotionally.

### 2c. A second, integrative power evolution

Plausible. Her power has trended toward voluntary modulation over thirty years of publication time. The next step is either *selective channel control* (absorb memory without power, or power without memory, or life-force-only as combat tool with full firewall on identity) or *reversal* (give back what she has taken). The reversal capacity would be world-historical for her psychology: it would mean she could, in principle, restore Cody Robbins, give Carol Danvers back what was taken — close the index traumas at their source.

This is the single most important fork in the long arc. If reversal becomes possible and she attempts it, two outcomes:

- **Success.** The reparation engine retires. She would have to construct, for the first time in her life, an identity *not* organized around debt. This is harder than it sounds. People who lose the wound that organized them often decompensate before reorganizing — the scaffolding goes before the new structure is up. Expect a depressive trough six to eighteen months after any successful reversal event, even though the event is unambiguously good.
- **Partial success or failure.** Worse outcome than not attempting. The Cody and Danvers wounds are tolerable as long as they are framed as *irreversible original sin*; if they become *recoverable in principle but I failed*, they retraumatize at the level of agency rather than fate.

### 2d. The Mystique re-entanglement (recurrent, near-certain)

Mystique will return as a destabilizer on roughly a five-to-seven-year cadence. This is the most reliable prediction in the file. The maternal transference does not extinguish; the foster-mother continues to be the only person who can reliably get subject to act against her current values. Each cycle has the same shape: Mystique arrives in distress or with leverage; subject's affect blunts and her decision-making becomes slower and more concrete; she does one thing she will later regret; she extricates; she returns to baseline with a slight net gain in clarity about the relationship and zero net gain in capacity to refuse it next time.

Forward question: will any cycle finally include either (a) Mystique's death in a context that forecloses resurrection, or (b) a confrontation that subject *initiates* rather than absorbs. Either would be a phase change. The latter is healthier and less likely.

### 2e. Gambit-loss event and its aftermath

Probability over a ten-year window: moderate-to-high. In this medium, primary partners are removed temporarily on a recurring basis — death, possession, mind-control, alternate-timeline displacement. The marriage's resilience to *temporary* removal is well-tested. The forecast concern is a *protracted* removal (years of in-universe time) or a *betrayal-framed* removal (Gambit revealed to have been compromised, or Gambit choosing exit). The latter would be catastrophic.

Behavior under brief Gambit-loss: she fights to recover him, efficiently, with the absorption power deployed without restraint. Behavior under protracted loss: predictable regression — geographic flight returns, the flirtatious surface hardens into a brittle parody of itself, isolation increases, the Mystique-channel re-opens because the only remaining maternal object is the bad one. Behavior under betrayal-framed loss: the most dangerous branch. The substrate self-concept ("contaminated object, ruins what it loves") would be confirmed in the worst possible way and the integrative work of the last twenty years would not fully hold.

---

## 3. THE LOWER-PROBABILITY BUT HIGH-CONSEQUENCE FORKS

### 3a. Loss of power-control

Mechanism could be Krakoan resurrection artifact, neurological trauma, a power-amplification event that overwhelms her newer governance, or a writer-level retcon. The clinical consequence would be severe: she has built her current life on assumed touch-access. Reverting to gloved-and-sealed would be experienced as *re-traumatization rather than return-to-baseline,* because she now has a comparison point. Persons who have known intimacy and lost it grieve worse than persons who never had it. Watch for: sudden re-acquisition of the full-coverage costume in the field even when not tactically necessary, a hardening of the accent (it always thickens under load), and a quiet withdrawal from physical proximity to Gambit in non-private settings.

### 3b. Catastrophic absorption event

The Magneto absorption (*X-Men* #25) is the precedent. The forward risk: she absorbs a figure whose psyche is both more powerful and more *coherent* than her own current self-organization, and the displacement does not resolve with conventional psychic intervention. Candidates in the current roster of available antagonists are not hard to enumerate. If this occurs, the recovery arc would require Jean-Grey-tier or Xavier-tier telepathic surgery, and even successful recovery would leave a residue. Each major absorption event has lowered the threshold for the next one — there is a kindling pattern visible across decades.

### 3c. Children, or the foreclosure of children

This is an open question the file should track. Subject has never had a stable opportunity to consider biological parenthood; the power foreclosed it for most of her life, and the marriage period has been dominated by crisis operations. The question matters because: (i) her unresolved maternal material is enormous and would be either healed or catastrophically reactivated by parenthood, (ii) the available adoption/fostering pathways within mutant society are unusually live and would suit her temperamentally, (iii) any pregnancy in this universe carries non-trivial somatic and metaphysical risks given her power-set history.

Probable trajectory: she will not seek biological parenthood. She will accumulate quasi-adopted juniors (see 2b) and treat the mentorship pipeline as the family she is making. If a specific child arrives in her care (orphaning of a teammate, a Krakoan crèche assignment, a found-child operation), she will commit fully and the attachment will be one of the most stable in her life. The risk is the inverse: if such a child is harmed or lost, the grief will be of an order she has not previously had to metabolize.

### 3d. A formal reckoning with Carol Danvers

The Danvers wound is the one piece of unfinished business with the highest leverage. The two characters have had partial reconciliations across the publication record but no decisive closure. A sustained Rogue–Danvers work-through (extended team-up, hostage-rescue collaboration, joint trauma-processing under telepathic supervision) would do more for subject's substrate self-concept than any other available intervention. The probability is moderate; the writers periodically rediscover the pairing. The forecast value if it happens: very high. Watch for early indicators — subject volunteering for Avengers-adjacent missions, or accepting them without the usual reluctance.

---

## 4. OPEN QUESTIONS THE FILE CANNOT YET ANSWER

- **Does the C-tactile deprivation deficit fully remit with restored touch access, or is the reward-circuit set-point permanently shifted?** The Sailer et al. (2016) substrate suggests sustained reward recruitment with sustained input, but a system deprived from age 13 to roughly age 30+ in cumulative terms may not normalize fully. Behavioral prediction: she will continue to over-value touch-events relative to neurotypical baseline for the remainder of her life. This is not pathological; it is the expected calibration of a previously starved channel.
- **What is her actual relationship to mortality?** She has come close repeatedly. The Krakoan resurrection protocols (insofar as they remain available) complicate the question. A person who knows death is recoverable behaves differently than one who does not. Subject's pre-Krakoan willingness to take physical risk was already extreme; the post-Krakoan recalibration is unclear in the record.
- **Will the Southern-Protestant moral substrate hold under sustained exposure to mutant-utopian frameworks?** So far it has. Krakoa's mysticism has not converted her. But her institutional success means she will be making moral arguments at the policy level, and her substrate is closer to a 20th-century American liberal-Protestant individualism than to anything indigenous to mutant culture. She is, quietly, an ideological outlier on the Council.
- **What happens to the flirtatious surface as the underlying deficit is treated?** Reaction-formation defenses sometimes attenuate as the deficit they covered resolves. The "sugah" register may soften into something less performed. Or it may calcify into a stylistic trademark that outlives its psychological function. The latter is more likely; defenses that become identity-features are sticky.
- **Is there an integration ceiling on absorbed identities?** She carries residue from every meaningful absorption. The cumulative load is unmeasured. If there is a ceiling, we do not know where it is.

---

## 5. WHAT WOULD PUSH HER TOWARD GROWTH

Concrete, in priority order:

1. **Sustained, low-stakes affective touch.** Not the marriage's high-stakes intimacy — that is already in place. The unmet need is *casual, social, non-romantic* touch: a hand on the shoulder, an embrace at a funeral, a child falling asleep against her. The reward channel needs repetition at low amplitude, not occasional peaks. The institutional setting (team huddles, sparring, communal meals) is the right environment if she allows it.
2. **A completed reparation event with Danvers.** See 3d.
3. **A confrontation with Mystique that she initiates and terminates on her own terms.** See 2d.
4. **Mentorship of a specific named junior with a touch-related or absorbed-identity pathology,** sustained over years. The act of guiding someone through the wound she could not be guided through is the single most consolidating activity available to her.
5. **Permission, from a trusted figure, to be tired.** This sounds small. It is not. The Protestant-reparation engine does not have an off-switch she can find from inside. Storm or Kurt could install one.
6. **A creative or domestic project unrelated to reparation.** She has never been observed to have a hobby in the file. A garden, a vehicle restoration, a music practice — anything that produces value not indexed to debt — would be diagnostic of the reparation drive loosening its grip.

## 6. WHAT WOULD PUSH HER TOWARD CATASTROPHE

Concrete, in order of severity:

1. **Betrayal-framed loss of Gambit.** See 2e. Substrate-confirming, hardest to recover from.
2. **Catastrophic absorption with residue.** See 3b. Risk of long-term identity displacement.
3. **A failed reversal attempt on Cody or Danvers.** See 2c. Worse than not trying.
4. **Mystique-orchestrated event in which subject acts against her current values at scale** (against the X-Men, against a junior under her care, against Gambit). The shame yield would exceed her metabolizing capacity.
5. **Loss of power-control accompanied by an immediate harm event** — touching someone in the moment of decompensation and injuring them. The Cody-template would re-instantiate at full intensity.
6. **Institutional collapse of the mutant polity** without a successor structure. She is now an institutional creature; she needs institutions to do reparation through. Sustained statelessness would route her back to geographic-flight patterns and Mystique-channel dependency.
7. **Forced solitary confinement of any duration** (capture, exile, depowering-and-isolation). The deprivation substrate is already at threshold; remove all input and she decompensates faster than most operators.

---

## 7. INDICATORS FOR REAL-TIME FILE UPDATE

The following observables, if logged, should trigger reassessment:

- **Glove behavior in non-tactical settings.** Re-adoption of gloves when not required = anxiety spike, possible control regression. Removal of gloves in a new social context = consolidation gain.
- **Accent thickness.** Baseline is moderate. Thickening = stress load. Flattening = either deliberate code-switching for command settings (healthy) or dissociative blunting (not healthy); context distinguishes.
- **Frequency of casual physical contact initiated by subject.** Baseline still low. Any uptick is a meaningful positive indicator.
- **Mention of Cody Robbins by subject, unprompted.** Has never been a routine occurrence. Would indicate active processing.
- **Pattern of mission selection.** Volunteering for Avengers-adjacent or Danvers-adjacent operations = approach behavior toward the index trauma. Sustained avoidance of same = ongoing suppression.
- **Sleep, appetite, migraine.** Standard somatic dashboard. The migraine pattern is the earliest reliable tell for psychic overload.
- **Quality of Gambit interactions in public.** Public warmth is the baseline; public formality or distance is the early indicator of private trouble.
- **Engagement with juniors.** See 2b indicator structure.
- **Any new hobby or non-instrumental practice.** See growth-indicator 6.

---

## 8. SUMMARY FORECAST

Subject is on the most favorable trajectory of her recorded life and remains structurally vulnerable in specific, predictable ways. The probable ten-year path is continued consolidation as an institutional leader and mentor, punctuated by one or two Mystique-cycle disruptions, at least one absorption-event scare, and a moderate probability of a Gambit-loss episode that she survives. The lower-probability forks include outcomes (Danvers reconciliation, reversal-capacity acquisition) that would be genuinely transformative and outcomes (betrayal-loss, catastrophic absorption with residue, Mystique-orchestrated values-violation) that would not be cleanly recoverable.

The single most important fact for forward planning: the wound is real, the adaptation built on top of it is unusually successful, and the *adaptation has become the person.* She cannot be lifted off her history without losing the structure her history produced. Growth, for this subject, does not mean undoing the past. It means continuing to convert the past, at a steady output rate, into work that the past would not have predicted she could do.

She has been doing exactly that, observably, for four decades. The base rate favors her.
